<p><b><a href="/wiki/February" title="February">February</a></b> <b><a href="/wiki/2011" title="2011">2011</a></b> was the second month of that common year. The month, which began on a <a href="/wiki/Tuesday" title="Tuesday">Tuesday</a>, ended on a <a href="/wiki/Monday" title="Monday">Monday</a> after 28 days.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_holidays">International holidays</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/February_2011&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: International holidays">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>(See <b>Holidays and observances,</b> on sidebar at right, below)</i></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portal:Current_events"><a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Portal:Current events</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/February_2011&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Portal:Current events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>This is an <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events/How_to_archive_the_portal" title="Portal:Current events/How to archive the portal">archived version</a> of Wikipedia's <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Current events Portal</a> from February 2011.</i></p>

<tr>
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div id="2011_February_1"></div>
<div id="2011_February_01"></div>
<table class="vevent" style="width:100%; margin:7px 0px; padding:2px; background-color:white; border:1px #cef2e0 solid;">
<tr>
<td>
<table cellspacing="0" class="plainlinks" style="background-color:#cef2e0" width="100%">
<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> February 1, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-02-01</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_1&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_1&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_1&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>
<ul>
<li>Protesters plan a "million-man march" on <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a>'s presidential palace in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a> starting at <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.voanews.com/breaking-news/2011/01/31/egypt-braces-for-million-man-march-as-army-pledges-restraint/" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/01/31/live-blog-feb-1-egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>At least two million people gather in <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a> in the biggest demonstration since the popular revolution against the Mubarak regime began. <a class="external text" href="http://www.hindu.com/2011/02/02/stories/2011020263100100.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hindu</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112113115442982.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/02/world/middleeast/02egypt.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-world/egyptians-amass-for-biggest-day-of-anger-yet-20110201-1acjj.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Egypt" title="Government of Egypt">government</a> closes down <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_National_Railways" title="Egyptian National Railways">Egyptian National Railways</a> as well as Internet and mobile phone services. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/africa/01/31/egypt.protests/?hpt=T1" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Mubarak addresses the nation to tell the people of his refusal to leave Egypt, though promises to resign at the end of his term. He tells the people of Egypt that he is "proud of his achievements over the years in serving Egypt and its people". <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/01/us-egypt-mubarak-reform-idUSTRE7108HR20110201" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-world/mubarak-says-he-will-not-seek-reelection-20110202-1aco7.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201121191413252982.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/egypt-uprising-jordan-king-abdullah-sacks-cabinet-cairo/story?id=12809623" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
<li>Protesters vow to stay in Tahrir Square until Mubarak goes. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/MiddleEast/Article.aspx?ID=206293&amp;R=R1&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>International response to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> urges Hosni Mubarak not to run for the presidency again, though stops short of telling him to resign immediately. He also called for the transition to democracy "to begin now". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-12340885" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/02/world/middleeast/02transition.html?_r=1" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/01/obama-pressures-mubarak-to-step-down" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/01/AR2011020105291.html?hpid=topnews" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post)</i></a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Turkey" title="Prime Minister of Turkey">Prime Minister of Turkey</a> <a href="/wiki/Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan" title="Recep Tayyip Erdoğan">Recep Tayyip Erdoğan</a> completely backs the people of Egypt in their battle against the Mubarak regime. Newspapers had previously criticised him for his lack of a response to the revolution there. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201121115128839350.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a> and <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> team up to build a voice-to-tweet system to allow <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptians</a> to tweet despite the closure of <a href="/wiki/Internet" title="Internet">Internet</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mobile_phone" title="Mobile phone">mobile phone</a> systems. <a class="external text" href="http://tech.fortune.cnn.com/2011/01/31/google-and-twitter-hook-up-to-allow-egyptians-to-tweet/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Fortune</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> reports that its signal is being jammed in parts of the Middle East, days after Egypt shut the news network's operations there. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/egyptNews/idAFLDE7102EP20110201" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abdullah_II_of_Jordan" title="Abdullah II of Jordan">Abdullah of Jordan</a> sacks the <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordanian</a> government <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Jordanian_protests" title="2011 Jordanian protests">amid protests</a> over prices in the country. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112113957115258.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/01/c_13716520.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.monstersandcritics.com/news/middleeast/news/article_1616224.php/Jordanian-government-resigns-Urgent" rel="nofollow">(M&amp;C)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Buddhism" title="Buddhism">Buddhist</a> family of four is shot killed by suspected <a href="/wiki/South_Thailand_insurgency" title="South Thailand insurgency">Muslim separatists seeking autonomy</a> from predominantly Buddhist <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> in the latest attack in an escalation of violence in the southern <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/01/idINIndia-54568420110201" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The owner of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>'s fourth-most visited website, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sohu.com" title="Sohu.com">Sohu.com</a> Inc, posted a better-than-estimated 41 percent gain in profit after the company raised prices and boosted services such as video sharing. <a class="external text" href="http://europe.chinadaily.com.cn/2011-02/01/content_11953035.htm" rel="nofollow">(China Daily)</a></li>
<li>A court in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> bars the oil company <a href="/wiki/BP" title="BP">BP</a> from entering into a planned joint venture and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Share_swap" title="Share swap">share swap</a> with Rosneft, a state-controlled Russian company. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/01/us-bp-idUSTRE70T1S420110201" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cyclone_Yasi" title="Cyclone Yasi">Cyclone Yasi</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> state of <a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">Queensland</a> evacuates off-shore islands and low-lying parts of <a href="/wiki/North_Queensland" title="North Queensland">North Queensland</a> ahead of <a href="/wiki/Cyclone_Yasi" title="Cyclone Yasi">Cyclone Yasi</a> which is expected to hit the state as a <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">Category 4 tropical cyclone</a> late on Wednesday or early Thursday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.couriermail.com.au/news/queensland-facing-a-deadly-event-with-cyclone-yasi-anna-bligh/story-e6freon6-1225997904763" rel="nofollow">(<i>Courier Mail</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/s/nm/20110131/wl_nm/us_australia_cyclone" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
<li>Cyclone Yasi is upgraded to Category 5 and is predicted to be the worst storm to hit Australia in generations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/environment/weather/yasi-upgraded-to-a-category-five-cyclone-20110201-1acgp.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/January_31_%E2%80%93_February_2,_2011_North_American_winter_storm" title="January 31 – February 2, 2011 North American winter storm">US blizzard</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Weather_Service" title="National Weather Service">National Weather Service</a> issues a blizzard warning for nine states in the <a href="/wiki/Midwestern_United_States" title="Midwestern United States">Midwestern United States</a> with a storm affecting a total of 30 states from <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a> to <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">Maine</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chicagotribune.com/news/local/breaking/chibrknews-weather-snowfall-chicago-indiana-20110130,0,3874341.story" rel="nofollow">(<i>Chicago Tribune</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-01/storm-cancels-flights-may-set-chicago-snow-record-coat-new-york-with-ice.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/specials/interactives/_national/snowstorm-020111/" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://voices.washingtonpost.com/capitalweathergang/2011/02/amazing_reports_about_massive.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.adelaidenow.com.au/news/breaking-news/mammoth-snow-storm-pounds-central-us/story-e6frea73-1225998725910" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Adelaide Now)</a></li>
<li>The storm is expected to affect as much as a third of the U.S. population, and has already created dangerous travel conditions and forced the cancellation of thousands of flights and the closure of <a href="/wiki/Interstate_Highway_System" title="Interstate Highway System">major interstate highways</a>.<a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/01/idINIndia-54572920110201" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/english/news/usa/US-Winter-Weather-Forces-6400-Flight-Cancelations-115033949.html" rel="nofollow">(VOA)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chicago" title="Chicago">Chicago</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chicago_Midway_International_Airport" title="Chicago Midway International Airport">Midway International Airport</a> closes due to the snow with 1,300 flights cancelled at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/O%27Hare_Airport" title="O'Hare Airport">O'Hare Airport</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.suntimes.com/3605053-417/flights-cta-midway-rail-tuesday.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Chicago Sun Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Wisconsin" title="Governor of Wisconsin">Governor of Wisconsin</a> <a href="/wiki/Scott_Walker_(politician)" title="Scott Walker (politician)">Scott Walker</a> declares a <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">state of emergency</a> in southern <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin" title="Wisconsin">Wisconsin</a> as a result of the blizzard. <a class="external text" href="http://www.channel3000.com/weather/26692720/detail.html" rel="nofollow">(Channel 3000)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Shinmoedake" title="Shinmoedake">Shinmoedake</a> volcano on the <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> island of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ky%C5%ABsh%C5%AB" title="Kyūshū">Kyūshū</a> erupts again with its biggest explosion since becoming active again. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5jhpJUyfitCQbLhIwKIDUJhn1Gxcg?docId=8c79fcef3f664b5ebc7cd3a03937df5e" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> police arrest three people in connection with a fire on a <a href="/wiki/Ferry" title="Ferry">ferry</a> last week that killed 27 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/world/114989984.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Minneapolis Star Tribune</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shanghai_Cooperation_Organization" title="Shanghai Cooperation Organization">Shanghai Cooperation Organization</a> to mark 10th anniversary in <a href="/wiki/Astana" title="Astana">Astana</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/world/20110201/162403689.html" rel="nofollow">(Rian)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> urges Iran to <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_Iran" title="Capital punishment in Iran">halt executions</a> after the hanging of a Dutch-Iranian woman, <a href="/wiki/Zahra_Bahrami" title="Zahra Bahrami">Zahra Bahrami</a>, accused of being drug smuggler; the U.S. State Department expresses concern that Iran "continues to <a href="/wiki/Human_rights_in_the_Islamic_Republic_of_Iran" title="Human rights in the Islamic Republic of Iran">deny its citizens their human rights</a>" and that cases, trials, and sentences continue to proceed "without transparency and the due process rights enshrined in <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_the_Islamic_Republic_of_Iran" title="Constitution of the Islamic Republic of Iran">Iran's own constitution</a>." <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/meast/02/01/iran.execution/?hpt=T2" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> agree to hold working-level military talks on 8 February, their first since the <a href="/wiki/Bombardment_of_Yeonpyeong" title="Bombardment of Yeonpyeong">attack</a> on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yeonpyeong_Island" title="Yeonpyeong Island">Yeonpyeong Island</a> in November last year. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/national/2011/02/01/79/0301000000AEN20110201008300315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">Palestine</a> is <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_State_of_Palestine" title="International recognition of the State of Palestine">recognised</a> within its 1967 borders by <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">Suriname</a>.<a class="external text" href="http://www.maannews.net/eng/ViewDetails.aspx?ID=356264" rel="nofollow">(Maan News)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Headlines/Article.aspx?id=206289" rel="nofollow">(Jerusalem Post)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>U.S. soldier <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bradley_Manning" title="Bradley Manning">Bradley Manning</a>, the alleged <a href="/wiki/Whistleblower" title="Whistleblower">whistleblower</a> who is thought to have revealed secret U.S. government documents to the international public, is reported to be held in solitary confinement awaiting trial by the United States for seven months now, treatment which the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> deems a form of torture when used for such prolonged periods. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/video/americas/2011/02/20112154519935748.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Karmapa" title="Karmapa">Karmapa Lama</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ogyen_Trinley_Dorje" title="Ogyen Trinley Dorje">Ogyen Trinley Dorje</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tibetan_Buddhism" title="Tibetan Buddhism">Tibetan Buddhism</a>'s third-highest lama, is questioned by police after large amounts of foreign money are found at his monastery in <a href="/wiki/Dharamsala" title="Dharamsala">Dharamsala</a>, northern <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>. Some Indian media allege he is acting as a spy for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.atimes.com/atimes/China/MB02Ad01.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Asia Times Online</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Irish_general_election,_2011" title="Irish general election, 2011">Irish general election, 2011</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brian_Cowen" title="Brian Cowen">Brian Cowen</a> resigns by requesting the <a href="/wiki/Dissolution_of_parliament" title="Dissolution of parliament">dissolution</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/30th_D%C3%A1il" title="30th Dáil">30th Dáil</a>, allowing <a href="/wiki/Irish_general_election,_2011" title="Irish general election, 2011">a general election</a> to take place, the first such election of the eurozone debt crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/01/us-ireland-idUKTRE71057C20110201" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12339623" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0201/politics.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/europe/02/01/ireland.politics/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/01/irish-brian-cowen-election-campaign" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>25 February is later announced as the date of the election. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0201/politics2.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>In the wake of several recent deadly plane crashes in Iran, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamic_Consultative_Assembly_(Iran)" title="Islamic Consultative Assembly (Iran)">Parliament</a> of <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> passes a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vote_of_no_confidence" title="Vote of no confidence">vote of no confidence</a> in the country's <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Roads_and_Transportation_(Iran)" title="Ministry of Roads and Transportation (Iran)">Minister of Roads and Transportation</a> <a href="/wiki/Hamid_Behbahani" title="Hamid Behbahani">Hamid Behbahani</a> and impeaches him. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/163028.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/01/AR2011020101232.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> and Defense Minister <a href="/wiki/Ehud_Barak" title="Ehud Barak">Ehud Barak</a> cancel the appointment of <a href="/wiki/Yoav_Galant" title="Yoav Galant">Yoav Galant</a> to the post of <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_General_Staff_(Israel)" title="Chief of General Staff (Israel)">Israel Defense Forces chief</a>. The announcement came after months of scandal surrounding his appointment due to allegations that he had illegally seized public lands near his home in Moshav <a href="/wiki/Amikam" title="Amikam">Amikam</a>, and after the <a href="/wiki/State_Comptroller_of_Israel" title="State Comptroller of Israel">State Comptroller</a> <a href="/wiki/Micha_Lindenstrauss" title="Micha Lindenstrauss">Micha Lindenstrauss</a> stated that Galant lied to in a sworn affidavit about exceeding his building rights.<a class="external autonumber" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/egyptNews/idAFLDE7102DM20110201" rel="nofollow">[1]</a> <a class="external autonumber" href="http://www.jpost.com/NationalNews/Article.aspx?id=205525" rel="nofollow">[2]</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> starts a search for a missing <a href="/wiki/Military_satellite" title="Military satellite">military satellite</a> launched into the wrong orbit. <a class="external text" href="http://www.antaranews.com/en/news/1296600959/russia-loses-military-satellite-reports" rel="nofollow">(Antara)</a></li>
</ul>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Egyptian protesters continue nationwide demonstrations against President <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> for a ninth day. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/01/live-blog-feb-2-egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/02/egypt-protests-live-updates" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mohamed_ElBaradei" title="Mohamed ElBaradei">Mohamed ElBaradei</a>, an emerging leader of anti-regime protests, and other protesters say that Mubarak must leave Egypt by Friday at the latest to avoid further bloodshed and turmoil. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/world/hosni-mubarak-must-go-by-friday-says-mohamed-elbaradei/story-e6frg6so-1225998404724" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The protestors increase their demands for the end of the Mubarak regime and are not impressed by Hosni Mubarak's promise to resign at the end of his current term. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112272918301323.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Clashes occur in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alexandria" title="Alexandria">Alexandria</a> between supporters and opponents of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President of Egypt</a> <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> with one person dead and 700 injured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12345656" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.net/2011/02/02/clashes-erupt-in-a-tense-egypt/" rel="nofollow">(Euronews)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2011/02/02/egyptian-military-calls-end-demonstrations-1705880116/" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/photo_galleries/middleeast/201122163520566506.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Mubarak supporters, rumored to be directed by the Mubarak regime, protest in central Cairo, Alexandria and other cities, attacking anti-government protestors with stones, knives and <a href="/wiki/Molotov_cocktail" title="Molotov cocktail">Molotov cocktails</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://voices.washingtonpost.com/postpartisan/2011/02/mubarak_unleashes_chaos.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Some supporters of the Mubarak regime ride horses and camels and attack anti-government protesters with whips. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/02/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-31" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/Molotov_cocktail" title="Molotov cocktail">Molotov cocktails</a> are thrown into the grounds of the <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Museum" title="Egyptian Museum">Egyptian Museum</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/02/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-66" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> (<a href="/wiki/Navi_Pillay" title="Navi Pillay">Navi Pillay</a>) believes as many as 300 people have been killed in Egypt over the last nine days. <a class="external text" href="http://www.almasryalyoum.com/en/news/un-300-killed-nationwide-protests" rel="nofollow">(<i>Almasry Alyoum</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amr_Moussa" title="Amr Moussa">Amr Moussa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arab_League#Secretaries-General" title="Arab League">Arab League Secretary General</a> and a former <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Egypt)" title="Minister of Foreign Affairs (Egypt)">Egyptian foreign minister</a>, says he would "seriously" consider whether to seek the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">Egyptian presidency</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Headlines/Article.aspx?id=206306" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Army" title="Egyptian Army">Egyptian Army</a> calls on protesters to "help restore normal life". <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/02/egypt-army-statement-idUSWEA517720110202" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mohamed_ElBaradei" title="Mohamed ElBaradei">Mohamed ElBaradei</a>, of the <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> opposition, raises concerns that clashes in Cairo could escalate into a "bloodbath". <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/babylonbeyond/2011/02/egypt-opposition-leader-mohamed-elbaradei-says-he-fears-coming-bloodbath.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Egyptian state television warns the people of Egypt to evacuate <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/02/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-74" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Internet access is partially restored in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> after a five-day blackout. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201122113055781707.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> urges Egyptian satellite company <a href="/wiki/Nilesat" title="Nilesat">Nilesat</a> to resume broadcasting its signal or face legal action. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/egyptNews/idAFLDE7110P320110202" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al_Arabiya" title="Al Arabiya">Al Arabiya</a> journalist <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ahmad_Abdallah&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ahmad Abdallah (page does not exist)">Ahmad Abdallah</a> is reported missing but later found after being beaten by pro-Mubarak supporters. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/02/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-83" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Pro-Mubarak protestors attack <a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">CNN</a> anchor <a href="/wiki/Anderson_Cooper" title="Anderson Cooper">Anderson Cooper</a> and his crew. The attack is successfully filmed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2011/02/02/anderson-cooper-attacked-punched-egypt_n_817352.html" rel="nofollow">(Huffington Post)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/02/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-92" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Committee_to_Protect_Journalists" title="Committee to Protect Journalists">Committee to Protect Journalists</a> (CPJ) compiles a list of members of the media who have come under attack in Egypt today. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/02/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-90" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://cpj.org/2011/02/journalists-under-physical-assault-in-egypt.php" rel="nofollow">(Committee to Protect Journalists)</a></li>
<li>International response to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> makes his first comments on Egypt since <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> announced he would step down before the next elections; Obama tells the people of Egypt "We hear your voice", and calls for an "orderly transition" of power that "must begin now". <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/International/Article.aspx?id=206304" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_State" title="United States Department of State">United States Department of State</a> spokesman <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/P._J._Crowley" title="P. J. Crowley">P. J. Crowley</a> is criticised after appealing for "<i>all sides</i>" in Egypt to "show restraint and avoid violence". <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/02/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-62" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Secretary-General_of_the_United_Nations" title="Secretary-General of the United Nations">Secretary-General of the United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/Ban_Ki-moon" title="Ban Ki-moon">Ban Ki-moon</a> warns against attacks on demonstrators while visiting the English cities of <a href="/wiki/Oxford" title="Oxford">Oxford</a> and <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/egyptNews/idAFLDE71120F20110202" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/breakingnews/219587/attacks-on-protestors-unacceptable" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Other world leaders offer their views on the ongoing crisis in Egypt. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/meast/02/02/egypt.world.reaction/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112215651396175.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>: <a href="/wiki/President_of_Yemen" title="President of Yemen">President of Yemen</a> <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a> backtracks on his plan to rule <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a> for life and to then allow his son to inherit his rule during an emergency session of parliament ahead of tomorrow's "day of rage" against his three-decade rule. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/2011228541277951.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/M/ML_YEMEN?SITE=RIPAW&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/middle-east/Yemeni-president-says-he-wont-seek-another-term-/articleshow/7412112.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Military_of_Mauritania" title="Military of Mauritania">army</a> in <a href="/wiki/Mauritania" title="Mauritania">Mauritania</a> destroy a car packed with explosives outside the capital <a href="/wiki/Nouakchott" title="Nouakchott">Nouakchott</a>, killing three people suspected of being members of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda_Organization_in_the_Islamic_Maghreb" title="Al-Qaeda Organization in the Islamic Maghreb">Al Qaeda in the Islamic Maghreb</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12344931" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iZbkDXhCi1XFJfO7G4Xi-ioNjovA?docId=CNG.8c92962f42ad9eaed99e60f1dd4aadf9.2d1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/WikiLeaks" title="WikiLeaks">WikiLeaks</a> reveals that the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">Federal Bureau of Investigation</a> had launched an investigation of a previously unknown group of men believed to be involved in the <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">September 11 attacks</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/wikileaks/8296860/WikiLeaks-FBI-hunts-the-911-gang-that-got-away.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least two people are dead and ten injured following the explosion of a <a href="/wiki/Car_bomb" title="Car bomb">car bomb</a> in a commercial area of the <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Peshawar" title="Peshawar">Peshawar</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ajc.com/news/nation-world/bomb-kills-2-wounds-824355.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Atlanta Journal Constitution</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Headlines/Article.aspx?id=206326" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> <a href="/wiki/Rock_music" title="Rock music">rock</a> duo <a href="/wiki/The_White_Stripes" title="The White Stripes">The White Stripes</a> announce that they are breaking up. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Entertainment/wireStory?id=12822369" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News America)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Cyclone Yasi:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> state of <a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">Queensland</a> braces for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Severe_Tropical_Cyclone_Yasi_(2011)" title="Severe Tropical Cyclone Yasi (2011)">Severe Tropical Cyclone Yasi</a> predicted to be one of the most powerful in the nation's history. <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/2011/02/01/idINIndia-54576720110201?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=worldNews&amp;utm_source=Reuters+India&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_campaign=Feed:+reuters/INworldNews+(News+/+IN+/+World+News)" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Airports in <a href="/wiki/North_Queensland" title="North Queensland">North Queensland</a> including <a href="/wiki/Cairns_Airport" title="Cairns Airport">Cairns Airport</a> and <a href="/wiki/Townsville_Airport" title="Townsville Airport">Townsville Airport</a> are closed ahead of Cyclone Yasi. <a class="external text" href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/nz-newspapers/west-coast-6013/news-6662/4609661/Yasi-shuts-Queensland-airports" rel="nofollow">(New Zealand Stuff)</a></li>
<li>Cyclone Yasi crosses northeastern Australia. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2011/02/201122141533487439.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Over 60,000 people are evacuated in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China's</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yunnan_Province" title="Yunnan Province">Yunnan Province</a> following an earthquake. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-02/02/c_13717029.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Headlines/Article.aspx?id=206313" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Fourteen job seekers traveling home on the rooftop of an overcrowded <a href="/wiki/Indian_Railways" title="Indian Railways">train</a>, are killed when they hit a low overhead bridge in northern <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/india/Six-passengers-travelling-on-rooftop-killed-after-train-passes-under-low-bridge/articleshow/7405467.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Headlines/Article.aspx?id=206327" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Six thousand flights are cancelled in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> following the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/January_31%E2%80%93February_2,_2011_North_American_winter_storm" title="January 31–February 2, 2011 North American winter storm">January 31–February 2, 2011 North American winter storm</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.centredaily.com/2011/02/02/2493968/flight-cancellations-pile-up-for.html?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter#" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Centre Daily</i>)</a></li>
<li>A fire destroys a <a href="/wiki/Star_(classification)" title="Star (classification)">five-star</a> <a href="/wiki/Sheraton_Hotels_and_Resorts" title="Sheraton Hotels and Resorts">Sheraton</a> hotel in the <a href="/wiki/Heping_District,_Shenyang" title="Heping District, Shenyang">Heping District</a> of <a href="/wiki/Shenyang" title="Shenyang">Shenyang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Liaoning" title="Liaoning">Liaoning</a>, China, then the tallest building in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Northeastern_China" title="Northeastern China">Northeastern China</a>, after midnight <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Firework" title="Firework">fireworks</a> celebrating the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_New_Year" title="Chinese New Year">Chinese New Year</a> set ablaze flammable <a href="/wiki/Thermal_insulation" title="Thermal insulation">thermal insulation</a> outside the hotel walls. Firefighters were unable to put out the blaze as ladders could not reach the higher storeys of the building, but no casualties or injuries were reported. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Hotel-In-China-Catches-Fire-Believed-To-Have-Been-Caused-By-New-Year-Fireworks/Article/201102115922000" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-02/03/c_13717480.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-02/03/c_13717480.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>RTHK English News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Sudan" title="Politics of Sudan">Sudanese government</a>, in its first official reaction after preliminary results were announced indicating a landslide <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Southern_Sudanese_independence_referendum,_2011" title="Southern Sudanese independence referendum, 2011">vote in favor of Southern Sudan's independence</a>, agrees to accept the results; Vice-President <a href="/wiki/Ali_Osman_Taha" title="Ali Osman Taha">Ali Osman Taha</a> says the government intends "to pursue a policy of good neighbourly relations with the south". <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/world/sudanese-accept-souths-vote-to-secede/story-e6frg6so-1225998343187" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Awards for the <a href="/wiki/WikiLeaks" title="WikiLeaks">WikiLeaks</a> website and <a href="/wiki/Julian_Assange" title="Julian Assange">Julian Assange</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Julian_Assange" title="Julian Assange">Julian Assange</a>, the founder of <a href="/wiki/WikiLeaks" title="WikiLeaks">WikiLeaks</a>, is awarded the <a href="/wiki/Sydney_Peace_Prize" title="Sydney Peace Prize">Sydney Peace Medal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/breaking-news/julian-assange-awarded-sydney-peace-medal/story-e6frfku0-1225998732639" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norwegian</a> MP nominates <a href="/wiki/WikiLeaks" title="WikiLeaks">WikiLeaks</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Nobel_Peace_Prize" title="Nobel Peace Prize">Nobel Peace Prize</a>, saying "Wikileaks have contributed to the struggle for human rights, democracy and <a href="/wiki/Freedom_of_speech" title="Freedom of speech">freedom of speech</a> globally, by exposing (among many other things) corruption, war crimes and torture — sometimes even conducted by allies of Norway". <a class="external text" href="http://www.nation.co.ke/News/world/-/1068/1100512/-/4hq8axz/-/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Nation</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/02/201122184159731783.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/egyptNews/idAFLDE7111KE20110202" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Colleen_LaRose" title="Colleen LaRose">Colleen LaRose</a>, known as "Jihad Jane", pleads guilty to participating in a terrorist plot to kill a <a href="/wiki/Lars_Vilks" title="Lars Vilks">Swedish cartoonist</a> whose <a href="/wiki/Lars_Vilks_Muhammad_drawings_controversy" title="Lars Vilks Muhammad drawings controversy">work offended many Muslims</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/world/jihadjane-colleen-larose-pleads-guilty-to-terror-charges/story-e6frg6so-1225998576541" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> <a href="/wiki/Central_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Central Bureau of Investigation">Central Bureau of Investigation</a> arrests former minister for communications <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/A._Raja" title="A. Raja">A. Raja</a> and other officials associated with the <a href="/wiki/2G_spectrum_scam" title="2G spectrum scam">2G spectrum scam</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dnaindia.com/india/report_breaking-news-cbi-arrests-a-raja_1502149" rel="nofollow">(DNA India)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2011/02/201122182618654798.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>

Barbier</a> rules that <a href="/wiki/Deepwater_Horizon_oil_spill" title="Deepwater Horizon oil spill">Deepwater Horizon oil spill</a> compensation fund administrator <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ken_Feinberg" title="Ken Feinberg">Ken Feinberg</a> should advise people that he is working for <a href="/wiki/BP" title="BP">BP</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.newser.com/article/d9l4v5tg0/us-judge-oil-spill-claims-czar-not-independent-of-bp-cannot-tell-potential-claimants-he-is.html#" rel="nofollow">(AP via Newser)</a></li>

<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_Authority" title="Palestinian Authority">Palestinian Authority</a> announces that it will hold local <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Elections_in_the_Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Elections in the Palestinian National Authority">elections</a> originally due to be held in June 2010. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/MiddleEast/Article.aspx?id=206300&amp;R=R3" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Chinese Premier <a href="/wiki/Wen_Jiabao" title="Wen Jiabao">Wen Jiabao</a> visits rural <a href="/wiki/Jinzhai_County" title="Jinzhai County">Jinzhai County</a> in <a href="/wiki/Jiangxi" title="Jiangxi">Jiangxi</a> province to celebrate Chinese New Year with local farmers. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-02/02/c_13717338.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_New_Zealand" title="Prime Minister of New Zealand">Prime Minister of New Zealand</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Key" title="John Key">John Key</a>, announces a <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_general_election,_2011" title="New Zealand general election, 2011">general election for November 26</a>, giving an unusually long notice for poll. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/world/new-zealand-calls-election-for-november-26/story-e6frg6so-1225998644017" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">President of Russia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dmitry_Medvedev" title="Dmitry Medvedev">Dmitry Medvedev</a>, expands the <a href="/wiki/Kremlin" title="Kremlin">Kremlin</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Human_rights_in_Russia" title="Human rights in Russia">human rights</a> council and authorises it to investigate the cases of <a href="/wiki/Sergei_Magnitsky" title="Sergei Magnitsky">Sergei Magnitsky</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Khodorkovsky" title="Mikhail Khodorkovsky">Mikhail Khodorkovsky</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.themoscowtimes.com/news/article/for-yeltsin-kremlin-seeks-yukos-review/430200.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Moscow Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> executive <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Craig_Oliver_(media_executive)" title="Craig Oliver (media executive)">Craig Oliver</a> is chosen to replace <a href="/wiki/Andy_Coulson" title="Andy Coulson">Andy Coulson</a> as British Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a>'s Director of Communications. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-12348159" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/politics/2011/feb/02/craig-oliver-andy-coulson-no-10-communications-chief" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> votes down a <a href="/wiki/Repeal" title="Repeal">repeal</a> of <a href="/wiki/Patient_Protection_and_Affordable_Care_Act" title="Patient Protection and Affordable Care Act">healthcare reforms</a> 47-51. <a class="external text" href="http://thehill.com/blogs/healthwatch/health-reform-implementation/141829-senate-rejects-healthcare-repeal" rel="nofollow">(The Hill)</a></li>
</ul>

<li>Part of New Zealand's <a href="/wiki/Pink_and_White_Terraces" title="Pink and White Terraces">Pink and White Terraces</a>, a natural wonder apparently destroyed in <a href="/wiki/1886_eruption_of_Mount_Tarawera" title="1886 eruption of Mount Tarawera">an eruption 125 years ago</a>, has been rediscovered by scientists. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/travel/news/article.cfm?c_id=7&amp;objectid=10703655" rel="nofollow">(<i>New Zealand Herald</i>)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kepler_Mission" title="Kepler Mission">Kepler Mission</a> announces the discovery of a <a href="/wiki/Planetary_system" title="Planetary system">planetary system</a> of six <a href="/wiki/Planet" title="Planet">planets</a> circulating the star <a href="/wiki/Kepler-11" title="Kepler-11">Kepler-11</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thaindian.com/newsportal/sci-tech/nasa-scientists-discover-planetary-system-with-six-planets_100497437.html" rel="nofollow">(Tha Indian)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Anti-government protestors continue to protest against the Mubarak regime for a tenth day. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/02/live-blog-feb-3-egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Protesters detain 120 people with IDs linking them to the police or ruling party; most were attacking protesters at the time. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-3#block-11" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4023474,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynetnews)</a></li>
<li>A tense standoff between supporters and opponents of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> continues in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>, with at least three people killed and 1,500 injured in fighting on Wednesday. <a class="external text" href="http://news.blogs.cnn.com/2011/02/02/egypt-crisis-prepping-for-another-day-of-protests/?hpt=T1" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.philstar.com/Article.aspx?articleId=654046&amp;publicationSubCategoryId=200" rel="nofollow">(AP via PhilStar)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Article/201102115920969" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>At least three people are killed as a result of gunfire in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.brisbanetimes.com.au/breaking-news-world/two-people-killed-in-cairo-witnesses-20110203-1aewn.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Brisbane Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/02/live-blog-feb-3-egypt-protests#" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Egyptian prime minister <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ahmad_Shafiq" title="Ahmad Shafiq">Ahmad Shafiq</a> says "sorry" for all the violence that has occurred in Tahrir Square and promises there will be no more. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201123133551858568.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Journalists from <a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> and the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> are among those targeted in fresh attacks from Mubarak regime "thugs". The UK's <a href="/wiki/Channel_4_News" title="Channel 4 News">Channel 4 News</a> reports that Mubarak's "secret police" are threatening journalists to keep off the streets of <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/feb/03/journalists-attacked-in-egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Prominent Egyptian blogger and anti-Mubarak activist sandmonkey is arrested and <a class="external text" href="http://www.sandmonkey.org/cgi-sys/suspendedpage.cgi" rel="nofollow">his blog</a> is taken offline by authorities in Egypt. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-40" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://hotair.com/greenroom/archives/2011/02/03/egypt-blogger-sandmonkey-arrested-by-state-security/" rel="nofollow">(Hot Air)</a></li>
<li>Egyptian state television forments the unrest by reporting that "Israeli spies" have infiltrated Cairo, leading to an increase in <a href="/wiki/Antisemitism" title="Antisemitism">antisemitic</a> sentiment among the pro-Mubarak forces attacking people and journalists on the streets. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201123131258705359.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jta.org/news/article/2011/02/03/2742846/pro-mubarak-supporters-target-journos-as-jews" rel="nofollow">(Jewish Telegraphic Agency)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.channel4.com/world-news-blog/egypt-the-man-staring-at-me-made-a-throat-slitting-gesture/14990" rel="nofollow">(Channel 4 News)</a></li>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> journalists are attacked on their way from the airport to central Cairo. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-48" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nile_TV" title="Nile TV">Nile TV</a> (state television) journalist <a href="/wiki/Shahira_Amin" title="Shahira Amin">Shahira Amin</a>, deputy head of the station, resigns after being threatened and intimidated; she tells <a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> "I can't be part of the <a href="/wiki/Propaganda" title="Propaganda">propaganda</a> machine and I refuse to be a hypocrite", adding that she feels "liberated". <a class="external text" href="http://iloubnan.info/politics/actualite/id/55656/titre/Nile-Sat-journalist-resigns-after-being-intimidated-by-the-state" rel="nofollow">(iloubnan)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://gulfnews.com/news/region/egypt/new-clashes-as-egypt-protesters-push-back-rivals-1.756374" rel="nofollow">(<i>Gulf News</i>)</a></li>
<li>Journalists from <a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Washington_Post" title="The Washington Post">The Washington Post</a></i> are arrested by Egyptian authorities; Swedish television loses contact with correspondent <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Bert_Sundstr%C3%B6m&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Bert Sundström (page does not exist)">Bert Sundström</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.monstersandcritics.com/news/middleeast/news/article_1616897.php/Swedish-television-reporter-missing-in-Egypt" rel="nofollow">(M&amp;C)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-67" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/03/AR2011020302747.html?hpid=topnews" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Representatives of <a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a> and <a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> are arrested. <a class="external text" href="http://www.amnesty.org/en/news-and-updates/amnesty-international-representative-detained-cairo-2011-02-03" rel="nofollow">(Amnesty International)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12307698" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-74" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Mobile phone firm <a href="/wiki/Vodafone" title="Vodafone">Vodafone</a> says the Egyptian authorities have hijacked its network to send unattributed text messages supporting the government. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-12357694" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Egypt's attorney-general bans several former ministers and <a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/Ahmed_Ezz" title="Ahmed Ezz">Ahmed Ezz</a>, a prominent member of the ruling party who resigned last week, from travelling abroad; their bank accounts are also frozen. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201123142759661467.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Video footage emerges on <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a> of a police van being driven at high speed into peacefully marching anti-regime protesters. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-3#block-69" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3wi3K8T3pPQ" rel="nofollow">(Direct link)</a></li>
<li>Four members of the <a href="/wiki/April_6_Youth_Movement" title="April 6 Youth Movement">April 6 Youth Movement</a>, an opposition group known for organising events on <a href="/wiki/Facebook" title="Facebook">Facebook</a>, are arrested by Egyptian authorities. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-3#block-92" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.wired.com/dangerroom/2011/02/egypt-arrests-four-facebook-activists/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wired</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> breaks his silence to grant an interview to <a href="/wiki/Christiane_Amanpour" title="Christiane Amanpour">Christiane Amanpour</a> of America's <a href="/wiki/ABC_News" title="ABC News">ABC News</a> inside his palace. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-3#block-99" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/03/us-egypt-mubarak-idUSTRE7127RQ20110203" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12361948" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/ABC_News" title="ABC News">ABC News</a> crew are carjacked and threatened with <a href="/wiki/Decapitation" title="Decapitation">decapitations</a> by pro-Mubarak supporters. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/03/egypt-protests-live-updates#block-3#block-103" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.hollywoodreporter.com/news/abc-news-crew-hijacked-threatened-96373" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hollywood Reporter</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2011/02/03/abc-news-beheading-egypt-brian-hartman_n_818303.html" rel="nofollow">(The Huffington Post)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> passes a motion supporting <a href="/wiki/Democracy" title="Democracy">democracy</a> in Egypt and calling on <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> to begin transferring power. <a class="external text" href="http://voices.washingtonpost.com/44/2011/02/senate-expected-to-pass-resolu.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>: Thousands of pro- and anti-government supporters demonstrate in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a> over the rule of President <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a> in a planned "day of rage". <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201123105140512715.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Algerian_protests" title="2010–2011 Algerian protests">2010–2011 Algerian protests</a>: <a href="/wiki/President_of_Algeria" title="President of Algeria">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Abdelaziz_Bouteflika" title="Abdelaziz Bouteflika">Abdelaziz Bouteflika</a> vows to lift the country's state of emergency, in force since 1992, in the "very near future". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12359750" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Syrian_protests" title="2011 Syrian protests">2011 Syrian protests</a>: Social media mobilises the people of <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> for rallies demanding freedom, <a href="/wiki/Human_rights" title="Human rights">human rights</a> and the end to emergency law, scheduled for Friday and Saturday in front of the parliament in <a href="/wiki/Damascus" title="Damascus">Damascus</a> and at Syrian embassies internationally. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201122171649677912.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Gunmen open fire in <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>'s majority Muslim <a href="/wiki/Pattani_Province" title="Pattani Province">Pattani Province</a> killing five people and injuring three people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2011/02/03/3129269.htm?section=justin" rel="nofollow">(AFP via ABC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.mcot.net/cfcustom/cache_page/164550.html" rel="nofollow">(Thai News Agency)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Awal_Gul" title="Awal Gul">Awal Gul</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghan</a> accused of being a <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> base commander, who has been imprisoned without charge since 2002, dies while exercising at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay_detention_center" title="Guantanamo Bay detention center">Guantanamo Bay detention center</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.miamiherald.com/2011/02/03/2048865/suspected-taliban-commander-dead.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Miami Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-12361834" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Food_and_Agriculture_Organisation" title="Food and Agriculture Organisation">Food and Agriculture Organisation</a> announces that world food prices have risen to a record high. <a class="external text" href="http://www.fao.org/news/story/en/item/50519/icode/" rel="nofollow">(FAO)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/03/food-fao-index-idUSLDE7111TR20110203" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-12354402" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The price of a barrel of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brent_crude" title="Brent crude">Brent crude</a> oil rises to $103 following violent clashes in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/03/idINIndia-54638520110203" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Cyclone Yasi
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Severe_Tropical_Cyclone_Yasi_(2011)" title="Severe Tropical Cyclone Yasi (2011)">Cyclone Yasi</a> hits <a href="/wiki/North_Queensland" title="North Queensland">North Queensland</a> in <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> with the worst affected towns including <a href="/wiki/Mission_Beach,_Queensland" title="Mission Beach, Queensland">Mission Beach</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tully,_Queensland" title="Tully, Queensland">Tully</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cardwell,_Queensland" title="Cardwell, Queensland">Cardwell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Innisfail,_Queensland" title="Innisfail, Queensland">Innisfail</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theage.com.au/environment/weather/tully-residents-reveal-horror-of-cyclones-wrath-20110203-1ae48.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Melbourne Age</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/special-reports/queensland-cyclone-yasi/story-fn7rxoal-1225998348468" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald Sun</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/events/yasi/" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>So far, there have been no reports of deaths or serious injury caused by the cyclone. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/environment/weather/second-surge-threatens-north-queensland-20110201-1acgp.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2011/02/201123124411681378.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The cyclone is downgraded from a Category 4 severe tropical cyclone to a category 1 <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">tropical cyclone</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/breaking-news/floodrelief/north-queensland-braces-for-cyclone-anthony-as-cyclone-yasi-brews-behind-it/story-fn7ik2te-1225998711771" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/environment/weather/100-stayed-at-cardwell-to-face-yasis-fury-still-no-word-20110203-1ae7a.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Death toll of second blast reaches 18 in <a href="/wiki/Ankara" title="Ankara">Ankara</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.trtenglish.com/trtworld/en/newsDetail.aspx?HaberKodu=450ca0c7-bad3-487a-94aa-bc65c1e0d238" rel="nofollow">(TRT)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.aa.com.tr/en/blast-in-turkish-capital-kills-4-injuries-27.html" rel="nofollow">(Anadolu Agency)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.cntv.cn/20110204/102109.shtml" rel="nofollow">(CNTV)</a></li>
<li>Two people are killed and 223 injured in Beijing as a result of <a href="/wiki/Fireworks" title="Fireworks">fireworks</a> set off on the first day of the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_New_Year" title="Chinese New Year">Chinese New Year</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-02/03/c_13718487.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Italy's parliament rejects a search request by prosecutors investigating <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Silvio Berlusconi</a> for having <a href="/wiki/Sexual_intercourse" title="Sexual intercourse">sexual intercourse</a> with an under-age <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prostitute" title="Prostitute">prostitute</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12361443" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A former policeman questions the <a href="/wiki/Suicide" title="Suicide">suicide</a> verdict recorded in the 1979 death of French cabinet minister <a href="/wiki/Robert_Boulin" title="Robert Boulin">Robert Boulin</a>, claiming he could not have drowned. His family believe he was murdered. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12353857" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Lawmakers in <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepal</a> vote to elect a new <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Nepal" title="Prime Minister of Nepal">Prime Minister</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-12352525" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reviewnepal.com/detail_news.php?id=1734" rel="nofollow">(Review Nepal)</a></li>
<li>Lawmakers in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a> elect two out of three Vice Presidents, one of whom will become the President. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12352764" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.oneindia.in/2011/02/03/juntaspm-chosen-myanmars-new-vicepresident-aid0126.html" rel="nofollow">(One India)</a></li>
<li>Haiti's presidential run-off candidates are named. They are former First Lady <a href="/wiki/Mirlande_Manigat" title="Mirlande Manigat">Mirlande Manigat</a> and popular singer <a href="/wiki/Michel_Martelly" title="Michel Martelly">Michel Martelly</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12342870" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/2011/02/03/uk-haiti-elections-idUKTRE7123AM20110203?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=worldNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Protein_folding" title="Protein folding">Protein folding</a> is advanced by the announcement of a discovery of a key mechanism in the relationship of protein folding to surrounding water by Olivier Collet at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nancy_University" title="Nancy University">Nancy University</a> (<a href="/wiki/Nancy-Universit%C3%A9" title="Nancy-Université">Nancy-Université</a>). <a class="external text" href="http://www.technologyreview.com/blog/arxiv/26341/?p1=Blogs" rel="nofollow">(Technology Review)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Anti-government protesters demonstrate against the Mubarak regime for an eleventh day - the "Day of Departure". <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/blog/2011/feb/04/egypt-protests-day-departure-live" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/node/3164" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>

<ul>
<li>Falling ice injures seven people at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cowboys_Stadium" title="Cowboys Stadium">Cowboys Stadium</a> in <a href="/wiki/Arlington,_Texas" title="Arlington, Texas">Arlington, Texas</a>, due to host <a href="/wiki/Super_Bowl_XLV" title="Super Bowl XLV">Super Bowl XLV</a> on Sunday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dallasnews.com/sports/super-bowl/local/20110204-falling-ice-at-cowboys-stadium-injures-7-one-critically.ece" rel="nofollow">(Dallas News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Albert_Haynesworth" title="Albert Haynesworth">Albert Haynesworth</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Washington_Redskins" title="Washington Redskins">Washington Redskins</a> is charged with assault in <a href="/wiki/Reston,_Virginia" title="Reston, Virginia">Reston, Virginia</a>, following an alleged <a href="/wiki/Road_rage" title="Road rage">road rage</a> incident. <a class="external text" href="http://voices.washingtonpost.com/crime-scene/tom-jackman/albert-haynesworth-charged-in.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Cleveland_Cavaliers" title="Cleveland Cavaliers">Cleveland Cavaliers</a> match the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">National Basketball Association</a> record for a single-season losing streak by losing their 23rd straight match to the <a href="/wiki/Memphis_Grizzlies" title="Memphis Grizzlies">Memphis Grizzlies</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://sports.espn.go.com/nba/recap?gameId=310204029" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> February 5, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-02-05</span>)</span> (Saturday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_5&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_5&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_5&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
