<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Anti-<a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Mubarak</a> forces continue their nationwide protests for a twelfth day, remaining in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/04/live-blog-feb-5-egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/blog/2011/feb/05/egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.skynews.com.au/topstories/article.aspx?id=573526&amp;vId=" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>The media reports that <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President</a> Mubarak's son <a href="/wiki/Gamal_Mubarak" title="Gamal Mubarak">Gamal</a> resigns as head of the <a href="/wiki/National_Democratic_Party_(Egypt)" title="National Democratic Party (Egypt)">National Democratic Party</a> bureau. Secretary <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Safwat_el-Sharif&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Safwat el-Sharif (page does not exist)">Safwat el-Sharif</a> and the six-member Steering Committee of the General Secretariat also resign. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/ondeadline/post/2011/02/mubarak-resigns-as-head-of-egypts-ruling-party-but-remains-president/1" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://thelede.blogs.nytimes.com/2011/02/05/latest-updates-on-day-12-of-egypt-protests/#ongoing-confusion-about-mubaraks-role" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Egypt-Hosni-Mubarak-Stands-Firm-After-Day-Of-Departure-Protests-As-Britons-Head-Home-From-Cairo/Article/201102115923449" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>Protesters form a <a href="/wiki/Human_chain" title="Human chain">human chain</a> in Tahrir Square to prevent tanks from entering the area. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/africa/02/05/egypt.unrest.standoff/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112513454758210.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>International response to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Israel" title="President of Israel">President of Israel</a> <a href="/wiki/Shimon_Peres" title="Shimon Peres">Shimon Peres</a>, speaking at a <a href="/wiki/European_Friends_of_Israel" title="European Friends of Israel">European Friends of Israel</a> (EFI) conference in <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a>, defends Mubarak, calling him a "peacemaker" whose "contribution to peace would never be forgotten". <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/babylonbeyond/2011/02/egypt-israeli-president-calls-president-mubarak-a-peacemaker.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4024283,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynetnews)</a></li>
<li>U.S. TV coverage of the uprising in Egypt is criticised for being both pessimistic and superficial and for its focus on what events mean for the U.S. and its regional allies. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/video/americas/2011/02/201125102520170918.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> halts sales of arms and riot equipment to Egypt. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110205-france-suspends-sale-arms-police-riot-gear-egypt-amid-turmoil" rel="nofollow">(France 24)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Tunisian_uprising" title="2010–2011 Tunisian uprising">2010–2011 Tunisian uprising</a>: Tunisian police shoot dead two people and injure another 17 during a protest in the city of <a href="/wiki/El_Kef" title="El Kef">El Kef</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12375255" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110205-police-open-fire-protesters-northern-el-kef-tunisia" rel="nofollow">(France24)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cambodian%E2%80%93Thai_border_stand-off" title="Cambodian–Thai border stand-off">Cambodian–Thai border stand-off</a>: A Thai soldier is shot dead and four wounded in clashes with Cambodian troops in a disputed border area. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12372121" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2011/02/20112585738205310.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>At least 20 people are killed in a shootout among the military in <a href="/wiki/Malakal" title="Malakal">Malakal</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Southern_Sudan" title="Southern Sudan">Southern Sudan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71404520110205?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201125163010915364.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XVI" title="Pope Benedict XVI">Pope Benedict XVI</a> ordains five new bishops, including a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> prelate from <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> despite attempts by China's official church to ordain bishops without his approval. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5ik_EGEkOB-17HBN-WwSPwmqt8Pvw?docId=1f0221eece014603a48b44f4dcb6f8ef" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>Comedian <a href="/wiki/Steve_Coogan" title="Steve Coogan">Steve Coogan</a> criticises the presenters of <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> television series <i><a href="/wiki/Top_Gear_(2002_TV_series)" title="Top Gear (2002 TV series)">Top Gear</a></i> in relation to their recent insulting of Mexicans. He also criticies the BBC's "pitiful" and "mealy-mouthed" apology after it offended Mexicans. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/culture/2011/feb/05/steve-coogan-top-gear-jeremy-clarkson-mexicans" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Inception" title="Inception">Inception</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Social_Network" title="The Social Network">The Social Network</a></i> win top prizes at the <a href="/wiki/Writers_Guild_of_America" title="Writers Guild of America">Writers Guild of America</a> awards. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/news/local/la-et-writers-guild-20110206,0,2837606.story" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Cold weather persists in northern <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> in the aftermath of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/January_31%E2%80%93February_2,_2011_North_American_winter_storm" title="January 31–February 2, 2011 North American winter storm">January 31–February 2, 2011 North American winter storm</a> with power shortages. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sun-sentinel.com/news/nationworld/sns-ap-lt-mexico-frigid-weather-animals,0,645438.story" rel="nofollow">(AP via Sun-Sentinel)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12370717" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>An explosion at the <a href="/wiki/Uricani_Coal_Mine" title="Uricani Coal Mine">Uricani Coal Mine</a> in southwestern <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a> kills five people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110205-explosion-kills-five-electrical-workers-uricani-mine-romania" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France 24)</a></li>
<li>Six <a href="/wiki/Firefighter" title="Firefighter">firefighters</a> die and two are injured fighting a fire in <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zhejiang_Province" title="Zhejiang Province">Zhejiang Province</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-02/06/c_13720268.htm" rel="nofollow">(China)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>UK prime minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> uses an important speech at a security conference in <a href="/wiki/Munich" title="Munich">Munich</a> to say "state multiculturalism" has failed, adding that the UK needs a stronger national identity and promising to promote <a href="/wiki/Western_world" title="Western world">Western</a> values. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-12371994" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/02/2011255620810460.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/politics/2011/feb/05/david-cameron-speech-criticised-edl" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph" title="The Daily Telegraph">The Daily Telegraph</a></i> publishes <a href="/wiki/WikiLeaks" title="WikiLeaks">WikiLeaks</a> cables stating that the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> provided <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> with the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>'s serial numbers of every <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trident_missile" title="Trident missile">Trident missile</a>, which are manufactured and maintained in the U.S. and supplied to Britain, in return for the Russians signing the <i><a href="/wiki/New_START" title="New START">New START</a></i> treaty. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/wikileaks/8304654/WikiLeaks-cables-US-agrees-to-tell-Russia-Britains-nuclear-secrets.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> cancels a planned appearance in <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>; <a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> link the cancellation to growing pressure for Bush to be arrested over his approval of <a href="/wiki/Waterboarding" title="Waterboarding">waterboarding</a> torture, saying Bush is "avoiding handcuffs". <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,,14820489,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.radionz.co.nz/news/world/67885/swiss-visit-by-bush-cancelled" rel="nofollow">(Radio New Zealand)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://betaus.mobile.reuters.com/article/idUSTRE7141CU20110205?WT.tsrc=Social%20Media&amp;ca=rdt" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The largest anti-government demonstration in years occurs in <a href="/wiki/Belgrade" title="Belgrade">Belgrade</a>, with thousands of disenchanted <a href="/wiki/Serbs" title="Serbs">Serbs</a> travelling to the parliament building from across the country to call for early elections there. An opposition party leader at the event compares it to the uprisings in Tunisia and Egypt. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12373901" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,,14820181,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idAFTRE71418Q20110205" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_people" title="Italian people">Italians</a> attend a rally to demand the resignation of <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Italian Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Silvio Berlusconi</a> over a sex scandal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.skynews.com.au/politics/article.aspx?id=573740" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/International_Cricket_Council" title="International Cricket Council">ICC</a> bans <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_national_cricket_team" title="Pakistan national cricket team">Pakistani</a> cricketers <a href="/wiki/Salman_Butt" title="Salman Butt">Salman Butt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mohammad_Asif" title="Mohammad Asif">Mohammad Asif</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mohammad_Amir" title="Mohammad Amir">Mohammad Amir</a> for five years for match-fixing. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/cricket/other_international/pakistan/9388422.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC Sport)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/sport/cricket/2011/02/201125152457400525.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Richard_Dent" title="Richard Dent">Richard Dent</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Faulk" title="Marshall Faulk">Marshall Faulk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ed_Sabol" title="Ed Sabol">Ed Sabol</a>, <a href="/wiki/Deion_Sanders" title="Deion Sanders">Deion Sanders</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chris_Hanburger" title="Chris Hanburger">Chris Hanburger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Les_Richter" title="Les Richter">Les Richter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shannon_Sharpe" title="Shannon Sharpe">Shannon Sharpe</a> are elected to the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Pro_Football_Hall_of_Fame" title="Pro Football Hall of Fame">Pro Football Hall of Fame</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/thehuddle/post/2011/02/deion-sanders-marshall-faulk-among-new-hall-of-famers/1" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://views.washingtonpost.com/theleague/nflnewsfeed/2011/02/chris-hanburger-elected-to-hall-of-fame.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Premier_League" title="2010–11 Premier League">English Premier League</a> news: <a class="external text" href="http://nbcsports.msnbc.com/id/41438590/ns/sports-soccer/" rel="nofollow">(AP via MSNBC)</a>
<ul>
<li>A new <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> scoring record is set with 41 goals scored in 8 matches.</li>
<li>League leaders <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Manchester_United_F.C._season" title="2010–11 Manchester United F.C. season">Manchester United</a> are stunned 2–1 by last-place <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Wolverhampton_Wanderers_F.C._season" title="2010–11 Wolverhampton Wanderers F.C. season">Wolverhampton Wanderers</a>, ending United's 29-match unbeaten streak in Premiership play.</li>
<li>Second-place <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Arsenal_F.C._season" title="2010–11 Arsenal F.C. season">Arsenal</a> become the first team since the establishment of the Premier League in 1992 to blow a 4–0 lead, as <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Newcastle_United_F.C._season" title="2010–11 Newcastle United F.C. season">Newcastle United</a> storm back to draw 4–4.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Cleveland_Cavaliers" title="Cleveland Cavaliers">Cleveland Cavaliers</a> set a new record for consecutive losses in a single <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">National Basketball Association</a> season in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://sports.espn.go.com/nba/recap?gameId=310205005&amp;campaign=rss&amp;source=twitter&amp;ex_cid=Twitter_espn_6094469" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_6&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>People demonstrate against the Mubarak regime for the thirteenth consecutive day, dubbed the "Day of Martyrs" in memory of those killed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.com/detail/163865.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/05/live-blog-feb-6-egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/06/egypt-hosni-mubarak" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Graphic rooftop footage emerges of a protester being gunned down in <a href="/wiki/Alexandria" title="Alexandria">Alexandria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/06/egypt-hosni-mubarak#block-5" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Protestors express anger at the governments of France, Israel and the United States due to their support of the thirty-year Mubarak dictatorship. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/163958.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> expresses increased concerns at the continuing targeting by the Egyptian authorities of journalists, human rights defenders, and youth activists, while another <a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> reporter is arrested. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/06/egypt-hosni-mubarak#block-7" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/06/egypt-hosni-mubarak#block-23" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>An Israeli man is released from custody. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.com/detail/163863.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li>Traffic to <a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a>'s English-language website, which features <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/watch_now/" rel="nofollow">a live stream</a> of events, increases by 2,500 per cent during the past week of its coverage of the events in Egypt, with as much as 60 per cent of this coming from the United States. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/babylonbeyond/2011/02/egypt-al-jazeera-official-says-web-traffic-skyrocketed-during-protests.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Two people are married in <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/06/egypt-hosni-mubarak#block-27" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Images emerge on <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a> of a man being shot at close range, possibly by police, in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a> / <a href="/wiki/Alexandria" title="Alexandria">Alexandria</a>; his condition is unknown. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201126145542683316.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> banks reopen for the first time in a week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/06/us-egypt-banks-idUSTRE7150EZ20110206" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-12376403" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/06/egypt-hosni-mubarak#block-4" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112681158721997.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Tunisian_uprising" title="2010–2011 Tunisian uprising">2010–2011 Tunisian uprising</a>
<ul>
<li>Police in <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a> kill at least two people during a protest in the northwestern town of <a href="/wiki/El_Kef" title="El Kef">El Kef</a> demanding the resignation of a police chief - crowds retaliate by burning the police station. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12375255" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/disp/story.mpl/ap/top/all/7415559.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201126185250639125.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Tunisia's interior minister suspends activities of the former ruling party <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Constitutional_Democratic_Rally" title="Constitutional Democratic Rally">Constitutional Democratic Rally</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/06/tunisia-protests-party-idUSLDE7150FS20110206" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12378006" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cambodian%E2%80%93Thai_border_stand-off" title="Cambodian–Thai border stand-off">Cambodian–Thai border stand-off</a>
<ul>
<li>Cambodia says a disputed 11th Century temple has been damaged on the third day of cross border clashes with Thailand. (<a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12377626" rel="nofollow">BBC</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>U.S.-led forces kill four civilians, including a woman, in northern <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/163867.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> soldiers have shot three Palestinians, two while they collected <a href="/wiki/Gravel" title="Gravel">gravel</a> from destroyed homes in <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza</a>, and another while he worked in the northern Gaza Strip. <a class="external text" href="http://english.peopledaily.com.cn/90001/90777/90854/7280406.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>People's Daily</i>)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.paltelegraph.com/palestine/gaza-strip/8399-three-workers-wounded-by-israeli-gunfire-in-gaza.html" rel="nofollow">(The Palestine Telegraph)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Indian_Army" title="Indian Army">Indian Army</a> insists it is to inquire "on its own" the death of a man in <a href="/wiki/Kashmir" title="Kashmir">Kashmir</a>, allegedly killed in an army ambush. His family says he was snatched from his home before being shot. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sify.com/news/army-to-conduct-its-own-probe-in-kashmir-youth-killing-army-chief-news-national-lcgsuedhdde.html" rel="nofollow">(Sify)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.kashmirobserver.net/index.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=6860:troops-kill-handwara-youth-massive-protests-erupt&amp;catid=15:top-news&amp;Itemid=2" rel="nofollow">(<i>Kashmir Observer</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least 50 people have died in a <a href="/wiki/Mutiny" title="Mutiny">mutiny</a> of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sudan_People%27s_Armed_Forces" title="Sudan People's Armed Forces">Sudan People's Armed Forces</a> in southern <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/sudanNews/idAFLDE7150AV20110206" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12375876" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Afghanistan" title="President of Afghanistan">President of Afghanistan</a> <a href="/wiki/Hamid_Karzai" title="Hamid Karzai">Hamid Karzai</a> says that a transfer of security authority from international to <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghan</a> forces will begin on March 21. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/asiapcf/02/06/afghanistan.security/index.html?eref=edition&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter#" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Indian_Navy" title="Indian Navy">Indian Navy</a> captures 28 suspected <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Piracy_in_Somalia" title="Piracy in Somalia">Somali pirates</a> on a <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> fishing vessel in the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian Ocean</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/06/AR2011020600921.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via the <i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/World_Heritage_Site" title="World Heritage Site">World Heritage Site</a> is damaged and collapses due to a dispute between <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12377626" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2011/02/20112613152324529.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Police on <a href="/wiki/Easter_Island" title="Easter Island">Easter Island</a> evict <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Easter_Island_History#Today" title="Easter Island History">indigenous protesters</a> battling for ancestral lands and a larger share of tourist revenues from the grounds of a luxury hotel. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sfgate.com/cgi-bin/article.cgi?f=%2Fn%2Fa%2F2011%2F02%2F06%2Finternational%2Fi113127S56.DTL" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>San Francisco Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

</dl>
<ul>
<li>Severe flood kills 13 in Sri Lanka. (Xinhua)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>:
<ul>
<li>Thousands of people in the Australian state of <a href="/wiki/Victoria_(Australia)" title="Victoria (Australia)">Victoria</a> are forced to evacuate due to flooding. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/national/weather-promts-3500-calls-for-help/story-e6frfkvr-1226000805781?from=public_rss" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sydney" title="Sydney">Sydney</a> experiences record weather conditions, hottest night on record. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/environment/weather/hottest-night-on-record-but-relief-only-hours-away-20110206-1ai0i.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>More than 100 people flee their homes from bushfire in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Perth,_Western_Australia" title="Perth, Western Australia">Perth</a>'s east. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/environment/weather/residents-flee-perth-bushfire-20110206-1ai55.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bushfire" title="Bushfire">Bushfires</a> threaten the suburbs of <a href="/wiki/Brigadoon,_Western_Australia" title="Brigadoon, Western Australia">Brigadoon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Baskerville,_Western_Australia" title="Baskerville, Western Australia">Baskerville</a>, <a href="/wiki/Millendon,_Western_Australia" title="Millendon, Western Australia">Willendon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Red_Hill,_Western_Australia" title="Red Hill, Western Australia">Red Hill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Herne_Hill,_Western_Australia" title="Herne Hill, Western Australia">Herne Hill</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Perth,_Western_Australia" title="Perth, Western Australia">Perth, Western Australia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.skynews.com.au/eco/article.aspx?id=573817&amp;vId=" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Widespread <a href="/wiki/Power_outage" title="Power outage">blackout</a> in eight <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> <a href="/wiki/States_of_Brazil" title="States of Brazil">states</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://en.mercopress.com/2011/02/04/massive-blackout-in-brazil-exposes-vulnerability-of-energy-infrastructure" rel="nofollow">(MercoPress)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB125798817743744475.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Wall Street Journal)</i></a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Palestinian leaders express disappointment at the refusal of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Middle_East_Quartet" title="Middle East Quartet">Middle East Quartet</a> — <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>, <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> — to hear their call for unilateral statehood and failure to take a strong stance on <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>'s settlement construction at its February 5 meeting in <a href="/wiki/Munich" title="Munich">Munich</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/world/20110206/162479087.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>'s foreign policy chief <a href="/wiki/Catherine_Ashton" title="Catherine Ashton">Catherine Ashton</a> expresses what she believes is the even more crucial need for progress in peace talks between the Israelis and the Palestinians due to events in Egypt and other countries. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.ie/world-news/middle-east/eu-says-mideast-events-make-peace-top-priority-2527389.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sunday Independent</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Spain" title="Law enforcement in Spain">Spanish police</a> remove more than 100 rowdy <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgian</a> students from an aeroplane. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12378558" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>24-year-old <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anat_Kamm" title="Anat Kamm">Anat Kamm</a>, a former soldier of <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>, signs a <a href="/wiki/Plea_bargain" title="Plea bargain">plea bargain</a> to plead guilty in <a href="/wiki/Tel_Aviv" title="Tel Aviv">Tel Aviv</a> District Court to a lesser charge of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anat_Kamm-Uri_Blau_affair" title="Anat Kamm-Uri Blau affair">leaking more than 2,000 secret military documents</a> to the <i><a href="/wiki/Haaretz" title="Haaretz">Haaretz</a></i> newspaper; she may be jailed for 15 years. <i>Haaretz</i> reported a possibly-illegal Israeli assassination operation against Palestinians in the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a>; her lawyer says she "believed she stumbled onto evidence of <a href="/wiki/War_crime" title="War crime">war crimes</a>". <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5jiIZ8ycojqrzwZolOrO8eD0Xdndw?docId=5869980" rel="nofollow">(CP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12377580" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/2011/02/06/idINIndia-54688620110206" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/06/israeli-soldier-anat-kam-faces-prison" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The trial of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%932011_detention_of_American_hikers_by_Iran" title="2009–2011 detention of American hikers by Iran">three American hikers</a> Sarah Shourd, Shane Bauer and Josh Fattal on <a href="/wiki/Espionage" title="Espionage">espionage</a> charges begin today in <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/02/06/136458.html" rel="nofollow">(Al-Arabiya)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011265380160303.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>One student is killed and 11 injured following shootings at a party in <a href="/wiki/Youngstown,_Ohio" title="Youngstown, Ohio">Youngstown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">Ohio</a>. Two men are later arrested in connection with the incident. <a class="external text" href="http://www.kentucky.com/2011/02/06/1625080/police-1-dead-11-shot-at-ohio.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Lexington Herald-Leader)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/CRIME/02/06/ohio.students.shot/index.html?eref=rss_topstories&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+rss%2Fcnn_topstories+%28RSS%3A+Top+Stories%29&amp;utm_content=Google+International#" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Reputed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mexican_drug_cartel" title="Mexican drug cartel">Mexican drug cartel</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Sandra_%C3%81vila_Beltr%C3%A1n" title="Sandra Ávila Beltrán">Sandra Ávila Beltrán</a> is sentenced to a year in jail for weapons possession charges. <a class="external text" href="http://www.elpasotimes.com/newupdated/ci_17311293" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>El Paso Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> billionaire <a href="/wiki/Ashot_Egiazaryan" title="Ashot Egiazaryan">Ashot Egiazaryan</a>, facing charges of financial crimes, flees to the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> claiming persecution. <a class="external text" href="http://finance.yahoo.com/news/AP-Exclusive-Fearful-Russian-apf-203931339.html?x=0&amp;sec=topStories&amp;pos=6&amp;asset=&amp;ccode=" rel="nofollow">(AP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
</ul>

<li>Embattled <a class="mw-redirect mw-disambig" href="/wiki/Kevin_Foley_(politician)" title="Kevin Foley (politician)">Kevin Foley</a> resigns as <a href="/wiki/Deputy_Premier_of_South_Australia" title="Deputy Premier of South Australia">deputy premier</a> and treasurer of <a href="/wiki/South_Australia" title="South Australia">South Australia</a> but insists on maintaining his defense portfolio. <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-national/foley-steps-down-as-sa-deputy-premier-20110206-1ai62.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Japan_Sumo_Association" title="Japan Sumo Association">Japan Sumo Association</a> cancels the <a href="/wiki/Sumo" title="Sumo">Spring Grand Sumo Tournament</a> in light of a <a href="/wiki/Match_fixing" title="Match fixing">match fixing</a> scandal, the first time the event has been canceled since 1946. <a class="external text" href="http://www.yomiuri.co.jp/dy/sports/20110206dy01.htm" rel="nofollow">(Daily Yomiuri Online)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12375649" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Danes" title="Danes">Dane</a> <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Bj%C3%B8rn" title="Thomas Bjørn">Thomas Bjørn</a> birdies three of his last four holes to achieve a four-shot victory of the <a href="/wiki/Qatar_Masters" title="Qatar Masters">Qatar Masters</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Doha_Golf_Club" title="Doha Golf Club">Doha Golf Club</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/sport/2011/02/201126152224625309.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Formula_1" title="Formula 1">Formula 1</a> racer <a href="/wiki/Robert_Kubica" title="Robert Kubica">Robert Kubica</a> crashes at a rally in <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>, fracturing his right arm, leg and hand. He undergoes surgery as a result. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/motorsport/formula_one/9388940.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC Sport)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">National Football League</a>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">American football</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Green_Bay_Packers" title="Green Bay Packers">Green Bay Packers</a> defeat the <a href="/wiki/Pittsburgh_Steelers" title="Pittsburgh Steelers">Pittsburgh Steelers</a> in <a href="/wiki/Super_Bowl_XLV" title="Super Bowl XLV">Super Bowl XLV</a> by a score of 31-25. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/thehuddle/post/2011/02/nfl-super-bowl-xlv-green-bay-packers-pittsburgh-steelers-mvp/1" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://msn.foxsports.com/nfl/gameTrax?gameId=20110206009" rel="nofollow">(Fox Sports)</a> <a href="/wiki/Aaron_Rodgers" title="Aaron Rodgers">Aaron Rodgers</a>, the Packers' <a href="/wiki/Quarterback" title="Quarterback">quarterback</a>, is named as the <a href="/wiki/Super_Bowl_Most_Valuable_Player_Award" title="Super Bowl Most Valuable Player Award">Most Valuable Player</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/thehuddle/post/2011/02/packers-aaron-rodgers-named-mvp-of-super-bowl-xlv/1" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cambodian%E2%80%93Thai_border_stand-off" title="Cambodian–Thai border stand-off">Cambodian–Thai border stand-off</a>
<ul>
<li>Clashes occur between <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodian</a> forces near the <a href="/wiki/Preah_Vihear_Temple" title="Preah Vihear Temple">Preah Vihear Temple</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.watoday.com.au/breaking-news-world/thai-cambodian-clashes-resume-20110207-1aj95.html" rel="nofollow">(WA Today)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_diplomatic_cables_leak" title="United States diplomatic cables leak">United States diplomatic cables leak</a>:
<ul>
<li>Newly released cables reveal <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> formed an alliance in February 2008 to share secret intelligence from spy satellite. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/technology/technology-news/australia-and-the-us-agree-on-a-spy-satellite-deal-20110206-1aii0.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>Newly released cables sent from the U.S. embassy in Cairo in 2008 refer to Egypt's Defence Minister, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Field_Marshal" title="Field Marshal">Field Marshal</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mohamed_Tantawi" title="Mohamed Tantawi">Mohamed Tantawi</a>, as "<a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Mubarak</a>'s poodle", though conclude that he "retains Mubarak's support, and could easily remain in place for years to come". <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/technology/technology-news/poodle-who-holds-key-to-a-nations-future-20110206-1aii6.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Luke_Harding" title="Luke Harding">Luke Harding</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a>'</i>s <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> correspondent is expelled from <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> as a result of the paper publishing cables about Russia becoming a "mafia state". <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/2011/feb/07/guardian-moscow-correspondent-expelled-from-russia?CMP=twt_gu" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> approves plans for two new buildings to be built in <a href="/wiki/East_Jerusalem" title="East Jerusalem">East Jerusalem</a>, <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">Palestine</a> with the Palestinians currently living there to be evicted.<a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/164101.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>

<li>Files regarding <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a>'s sexual indecency charges against Julian Assange are leaked on the Internet. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-1353989/WikiLeaks-Police-sex-files-Julian-Assange-leaked-online.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> <a href="/wiki/Knesset" title="Knesset">Knesset</a> approves the "<a href="/wiki/Azmi_Bishara" title="Azmi Bishara">Bishara</a> Bill", which would revoke the pension payments of Knesset members if they fail to appear at criminal proceedings held against them, or if convicted of severe felonies. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4025621,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Ynetnews</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>
<ul>
<li>The protests continue in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> for a fifteenth day, hours after a detained <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a> executive is released with the crowds the biggest yet. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112851424979539.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://thelede.blogs.nytimes.com/2011/02/08/latest-updates-on-day-15-of-egypt-protests/?src=twt&amp;twt=thelede#video-of-protest-at-egyptian-parliament" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_Egypt" title="Vice President of Egypt">Vice President of Egypt</a> <a href="/wiki/Omar_Suleiman" title="Omar Suleiman">Omar Suleiman</a> promises that the government will not pursue protesters. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/41469240/ns/world_news-mideastn_africa/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> claims that government-controlled health services in Egypt have been 'told to downplay protest deaths'. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2011/02/09/3133668.htm?section=justin" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> Cabinet Secretary <a href="/wiki/Angelo_Reyes" title="Angelo Reyes">Angelo Reyes</a> dies following an apparent <a href="/wiki/Suicide" title="Suicide">suicide</a> attempt possibly prompted by a scandal over alleged military corruption. <a class="external text" href="http://www.philstar.com/Article.aspx?articleId=655532&amp;publicationSubCategoryId=200" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philippines Star</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://newsinfo.inquirer.net/breakingnews/nation/view/20110208-319114/Angelo-Reyes-shot" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philippines Inquirer</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.gmanews.tv/story/212458/ex-afp-chief-reyes-declared-dead-from-gunshot-wound#" rel="nofollow">(GMA News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/George_Osborne" title="George Osborne">George Osborne</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_the_Exchequer" title="Chancellor of the Exchequer">Chancellor of the Exchequer</a>, announces that the <a href="/wiki/Tax" title="Tax">tax</a> on bank profits will become permanent. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Article/201102115925669" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(UK)" title="Labour Party (UK)">British Labour</a> MP <a href="/wiki/Eric_Illsley" title="Eric Illsley">Eric Illsley</a> <a href="/wiki/Resignation_from_the_British_House_of_Commons" title="Resignation from the British House of Commons">resigns his seat</a> two days before he is due to be sentenced for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_Parliamentary_expenses_scandal" title="United Kingdom Parliamentary expenses scandal">dishonestly claiming parliamentary expenses</a>, thus triggering a <a href="/wiki/Barnsley_Central_by-election,_2011" title="Barnsley Central by-election, 2011">by-election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-south-yorkshire-12400076" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> fails to pass extensions of key provisions of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USA_Patriot_Act" title="USA Patriot Act">USA Patriot Act</a> by the necessary two-thirds majority. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-09/house-rejects-extensions-of-patriot-act-provisions.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> environmentalists and <a href="/wiki/Indigenous_rights" title="Indigenous rights">indigenous rights</a> activists protest against the <a href="/wiki/Belo_Monte_Dam" title="Belo Monte Dam">Belo Monte Dam</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brasilia" title="Brasilia">Brasilia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/americas/02/08/brazil.dam.protests/index.html?eref=edition&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter#" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Somali_pirates" title="Somali pirates">Somali pirates</a> seize an oil supertanker off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Oman" title="Oman">Oman</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12403528" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>At least seven people are killed and dozens of others are injured during three explosions in <a href="/wiki/Kirkuk" title="Kirkuk">Kirkuk</a>, Iraq. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201129124643685401.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Serial blasts rock <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Grozny" title="Grozny">Grozny</a>, at least five people are wounded. <a class="external text" href="http://english.people.com.cn/90001/90777/90853/7282438.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>People's Daily</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Nationwide protests against <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> and his regime continue for a sixteenth day. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/08/live-blog-feb-9-egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/news/blog/2011/feb/09/egypt-protests-live-updates-9-february" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Labour unions involving thousands of workers go on a nationwide strike, boosting the pro-democracy demonstrations occurring across the country. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112913546831171.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Human rights groups say the military is secretly detaining and torturing hundreds and possibly thousands of suspected government opponents and has been doing so since the protests started. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/09/egypt-army-detentions-torture-accused" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The government threatens a crackdown as the protests spread. <a class="external text" href="http://www.khaleejtimes.com/DisplayArticle09.asp?xfile=data/middleeast/2011/February/middleeast_February275.xml&amp;section=middleeast" rel="nofollow">(<i>Khaleej Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/english/news/middle-east/In-Egypt-Protesters-Government-Dig-In-115625749.html" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
<li>Egyptians mourn those killed for protesting against their government. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201129181744289932.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>After being released by the authorities, <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a> executive <a href="/wiki/Wael_Ghonim" title="Wael Ghonim">Wael Ghonim</a> addresses the crowds in <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/video/2011/feb/09/wael-ghonim-tahrir-square-video" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> publishes <a href="/wiki/United_States_diplomatic_cables_leak" title="United States diplomatic cables leak">WikiLeaks cables</a> claiming that <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> had exaggerated its <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Crude_oil" title="Crude oil">crude oil</a> reserves by nearly 40% and will have trouble keeping a cap on oil prices. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/business/2011/feb/08/saudi-oil-reserves-overstated-wikileaks" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>A leaked memo shows <a href="/wiki/Nokia" title="Nokia">Nokia</a> chief executive <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Elop" title="Stephen Elop">Stephen Elop</a>'s belief that the company is too slow in its response to trend changes. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/business/2011/02/201129144053920207.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Activision_Blizzard" title="Activision Blizzard">Activision Blizzard</a> announces that it is dissolving its <a href="/wiki/Guitar_Hero" title="Guitar Hero">Guitar Hero</a> division and not publishing any more games. <a class="external text" href="http://www.gamasutra.com/view/news/32946/Activision_Dissolves_Guitar_Hero_Business_Refocuses_On_Digital.php" rel="nofollow">(Gamasutra)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/ConocoPhillips" title="ConocoPhillips">ConocoPhillips</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marathon_Oil" title="Marathon Oil">Marathon Oil</a> announce plans to shut down a <a href="/wiki/Liquefied_natural_gas" title="Liquefied natural gas">liquefied natural gas</a> plant in <a href="/wiki/Kenai,_Alaska" title="Kenai, Alaska">Kenai</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>, United States. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ktuu.com/news/ktuu-natural-gas-plant-lng-plant-in-kenai-to-shut-down-20110209,0,3583558.story" rel="nofollow">(AP via KTUU)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Project_Merlin" title="Project Merlin">Project Merlin</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/9_February" title="9 February">9 February</a> - Project Merlin, an agreement on aspects of <a href="/wiki/Banking_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Banking in the United Kingdom">banking activity in the United Kingdom</a>, is agreed between the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_coalition_government_(2010%E2%80%93present)" title="United Kingdom coalition government (2010–present)">coalition government</a> and the country's four major high street banks. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-12402469" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democrats" title="Liberal Democrats">Liberal Democrat</a> peer <a href="/wiki/Matthew_Oakeshott,_Baron_Oakeshott_of_Seagrove_Bay" title="Matthew Oakeshott, Baron Oakeshott of Seagrove Bay">Lord Oakeshott</a> resigns as a <a href="/wiki/HM_Treasury" title="HM Treasury">Treasury</a> spokesman in the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Lords" title="House of Lords">House of Lords</a> after making an outspoken attack on the agreement. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-12411664" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A major fire breaks out in <a href="/wiki/Bombay_House" title="Bombay House">Bombay House</a>, a historic building in <a href="/wiki/Mumbai" title="Mumbai">Mumbai</a>, <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>, which serves as the headquarters of the <a href="/wiki/Tata_Group" title="Tata Group">Tata Group</a>, resulting in at least three deaths. <a class="external text" href="http://ibnlive.in.com/news/mumbai-fire-at-bombay-house/142826-3.html" rel="nofollow">(Press Trust of India via IBN-Live)</a></li>
<li>Thieves tapping a <a href="/wiki/Pemex" title="Pemex">Pemex</a> oil pipeline cause a <a href="/wiki/Diesel_fuel" title="Diesel fuel">diesel fuel</a> spill south of <a href="/wiki/Tijuana" title="Tijuana">Tijuana</a> in <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/2011/02/09/mexico-oil-spill-idUKN0921714220110209" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Two small planes (took off from <a href="/wiki/Langley_Regional_Airport" title="Langley Regional Airport">Langley Regional Airport</a>) collide mid-air near <a href="/wiki/Mission,_British_Columbia" title="Mission, British Columbia">Mission, British Columbia</a>, in western <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, with at least one person dead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ctvbc.ctv.ca/servlet/an/local/CTVNews/20110209/bc_plane_crash_110209/20110209?hub=BritishColumbiaHome" rel="nofollow">(CTV)</a></li>
<li>An explosion occurs in <a href="/wiki/Allentown,_Pennsylvania" title="Allentown, Pennsylvania">Allentown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">Pennsylvania</a>, United States, resulting in two people being missing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.mcall.com/news/breaking/mc-allentown-house-explodes-020911,0,7470195.story" rel="nofollow">(The Morning Call)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President of France</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> calls for an end to government ministers holidaying abroad after it emerges they went to countries such as <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a> while <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Arab_world_protests" title="2010–2011 Arab world protests">anti-regime protests were underway</a>. The controversy has led to calls for resignations. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/02/20112917101935120.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Korean talks
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> agrees in principle to resume discussions with <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> on humanitarian issues including reuniting families separated by the <a href="/wiki/Korean_War" title="Korean War">Korean War</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12401126" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Military talks end without agreement as North Korea refuses to apologise for the <a href="/wiki/Bombardment_of_Yeonpyeong" title="Bombardment of Yeonpyeong">Bombardment of Yeonpyeong</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/national/2011/02/09/83/0301000000AEN20110209009100315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>U.S. Homeland Security Secretary <a href="/wiki/Janet_Napolitano" title="Janet Napolitano">Janet Napolitano</a> claims the possibility of terrorism being carried out against the country "has evolved significantly" and, she claims, is "at its most heightened state" since <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">the 9/11 attacks</a>". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-12407859" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>In a new agreement, Denmark and Russia will for the first time, cooperate within military. <a class="external text" href="http://jp.dk/uknews/article2334212.ece" rel="nofollow">(Jyllandsposten)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Prime Minister of Italy</a> <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Silvio Berlusconi</a> brands "disgusting" a request by prosecutors in <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">Milan</a> to have him put on trial immediately in relation to sexual relations with underage prostitutes which allegedly occurred at one of his house parties. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12404554" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Detective" title="Detective">Detectives</a> investigating claims over tabloid <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/News_of_the_World_phone_hacking_affair" title="News of the World phone hacking affair">phone hacking</a> in Britain are re-examining whether a string of high-profile individuals and celebrities were targeted. <a href="/wiki/Scotland_Yard" title="Scotland Yard">Scotland Yard</a> is taking a second look. <a class="external text" href="http://www.radioaire.co.uk/Article.asp?id=2105600&amp;spid=25211" rel="nofollow">(Radioaire)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Lemi_Milla" title="Jimmy Lemi Milla">Jimmy Lemi Milla</a>, a <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudanese</a> minister, and his bodyguard are shot dead apparently as a result of a personal dispute. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201129133511388343.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The trial of former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Liberia" title="President of Liberia">President of Liberia</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charles_Taylor_(Liberia)" title="Charles Taylor (Liberia)">Charles Taylor</a> is adjourned until Friday after he does not attend court in <a href="/wiki/The_Hague" title="The Hague">The Hague</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12402254" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Daniel_Patrick_Boyd" title="Daniel Patrick Boyd">Daniel Patrick Boyd</a> pleads guilty to <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorism</a> charges in a trial in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">US</a> state of <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">North Carolina</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/nation/115655454.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Minneapolis Tribune</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Spanish <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Basque_nationalists" title="Basque nationalists">Basque nationalists</a> announce a new political party named <a href="/wiki/Sortu" title="Sortu">Sortu</a> (meaning "born" in the <a href="/wiki/Basque_language" title="Basque language">Basque language</a>), categorically rejecting all violence, including that of <a href="/wiki/ETA_(separatist_group)" title="ETA (separatist group)">ETA</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.monstersandcritics.com/news/europe/news/article_1617787.php/New-Basque-separatist-party-unveils-its-name-Sortu" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Presse-Agentur)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_of_Pakistan" title="Cabinet of Pakistan">Cabinet of Pakistan</a> submit their resignations to the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Pakistan" title="Prime Minister of Pakistan">prime minister</a>, who intends to appoint a smaller <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_(government)" title="Cabinet (government)">cabinet</a> in order to reduce government spending at a time of <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Pakistan" title="Economy of Pakistan">economic crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5i8jZd9DQPiTclbcq2U9o-kVxxE-A?docId=CNG.5b1299bcf195e527eee38fa8e23c0446.161" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">US Representative</a> <a href="/wiki/Chris_Lee_(New_York_politician)" title="Chris Lee (New York politician)">Chris Lee</a> representing <a href="/wiki/New_York%27s_26th_congressional_district" title="New York's 26th congressional district">New York's 26th congressional district</a> resigns after it is revealed that he sent a racy photo to a woman who was not his wife. <a class="external text" href="http://cityroom.blogs.nytimes.com/2011/02/09/new-york-congressman-resigns-over-shirtless-photo/?src=tptw" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Leadership_Council" title="Democratic Leadership Council">Democratic Leadership Council</a> consisting of centrist <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democrats</a> announces that it will wind up. <a class="external text" href="http://www.tnr.com/article/politics/83086/democratic-leadership-council-requiem-dlc?page=0,0" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New Republic</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Councillors_of_Tunisia" title="Chamber of Councillors of Tunisia">Chamber of Councillors of Tunisia</a> passes legislation allowing the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Tunisia" title="President of Tunisia">President</a> to rule by decree. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12410704?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Owners and players in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">National Football League</a> resume talks in an effort to avoid a <a href="/wiki/Lockout_(industry)" title="Lockout (industry)">lockout</a> next season. <a class="external text" href="http://sports.espn.go.com/nfl/news/story?id=6105114" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Florida_Panthers" title="Florida Panthers">Florida Panthers</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">National Hockey League</a> team acquires <a href="/wiki/Jack_Skille" title="Jack Skille">Jack Skille</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hugh_Jessiman" title="Hugh Jessiman">Hugh Jessiman</a> and <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=David_Pacan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="David Pacan (page does not exist)">David Pacan</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Chicago_Blackhawks" title="Chicago Blackhawks">Chicago Blackhawks</a> in exchange for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Michael_Frolik" title="Michael Frolik">Michael Frolik</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alexander_Salak" title="Alexander Salak">Alexander Salak</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://panthers.nhl.com/club/news.htm?id=552202" rel="nofollow">(National Hockey League)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_10&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_10&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Protests against the <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Mubarak</a> regime go on nationwide for a seventeenth consecutive day. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/blog/2011/feb/10/egypt-middleeast" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/10/live-blog-feb-10-egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> President <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> refuses to resign in an address to the nation. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011210172519776830.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/blog/2011/feb/10/egypt-hosni-mubarak-resignation-rumours" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>At least 16 people have been killed the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Southern_Sudan" title="Southern Sudan">Southern Sudanese</a> <a href="/wiki/States_of_Sudan" title="States of Sudan">state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Jonglei" title="Jonglei">Jonglei</a>, breaking a ceasefire agreed last month. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201121011658114721.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bomber" title="Suicide bomber">suicide bomber</a> attacks a <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Army" title="Pakistan Army">Pakistan Army</a> recruitment centre in northwestern <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> causing at least 27 deaths and 40 injuries. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/10/us-pakistan-violence-idUSTRE7190QW20110210" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.couriermail.com.au/news/breaking-news/bomb-kills-at-least-14-troops-in-pakistan/story-e6freonf-1226003784759" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Courier Mail</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-12413469" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.sify.com/news/27-cadets-killed-as-schoolboy-attacks-pakistan-army-centre-news-international-lckoOfagaec.html" rel="nofollow">(Sify)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Armed_Forces_of_Colombia" title="Revolutionary Armed Forces of Colombia">FARC</a> organisation releases the first of five hostages promised this week as a gesture of peace to the government in <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12411841" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> forces remove Palestinian tents near <a href="/wiki/Nablus" title="Nablus">Nablus</a> of which 8 were reportedly used as homes.<a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Headlines/Article.aspx?id=207539" rel="nofollow">(Jerusalem Post)</a><a class="external text" href="http://arabnews.com/middleeast/article255266.ece" rel="nofollow">(Arab News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a> is to host the debut <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=International_Choir_Festival&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="International Choir Festival (page does not exist)">International Choir Festival</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://vietnamnews.vnagency.com.vn/Life-Style/208288/Viet-Nam-to-host-debut-International-Choir-Festival.html" rel="nofollow">(Vietnam News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Eight people are killed in a warehouse fire in <a href="/wiki/Perm" title="Perm">Perm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.itar-tass.com/eng/level2.html?NewsID=15940223&amp;PageNum=0" rel="nofollow">(Itar Tass)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5h636x1-B_2ydOYExEizAiBNIlByg?docId=CNG.b52a4404d74c4dd16459e5190c7894de.a91" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Manx2" title="Manx2">Manx2</a> flight from Belfast to <a href="/wiki/Cork_Airport" title="Cork Airport">Cork</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Manx2_Metroliner_crash" title="Manx2 Metroliner crash">crashes</a> on landing, killing six and injuring at least another six. It is the deadliest in Irish aviation since 1968. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/blog/2011/feb/10/cork-plane-crash-latest-news" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0210/cork.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/world/story/2011/02/10/cork-plane-crash-ireland.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC News)</a></li>
<li>Three people are dead, and two others are missing after a natural gas line rupture and explosion in the city of <a href="/wiki/Allentown,_Pennsylvania" title="Allentown, Pennsylvania">Allentown, Pennsylvania</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/US/02/10/pennsylvania.explosion/index.html?hpt=T2" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Snowstorm" title="Snowstorm">snowstorm</a> hits the <a href="/wiki/Southeastern_United_States" title="Southeastern United States">Southeastern United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tennessee_Valley" title="Tennessee Valley">Tennessee Valley</a> with warnings in place across ten states. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/US/02/10/winter.storm/index.html?eref=rss_topstories&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed:+rss/cnn_topstories+(RSS:+Top+Stories)&amp;utm_content=Google+Feedfetcher" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_Cuba" title="Communist Party of Cuba">Cuban Information and Communications</a> Minister <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Medardo_Diaz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Medardo Diaz (page does not exist)">Medardo Diaz</a> welcomes the arrival of an <a href="/wiki/Submarine_communications_cable" title="Submarine communications cable">undersea fibre-optic cable</a> linking it to <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a>, which offered to help the island speed up its internet connection after the <a href="/wiki/Federal_government_of_the_United_States" title="Federal government of the United States">United States</a> refused. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12411845" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> reports that it will not conduct further talks with <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>, citing a perceived lack of seriousness on South Korea's part. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/41500043/ns/world_news-asiapacific/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>Reuters reports that <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> have agreed to resume peace talks that were broken off after the <a href="/wiki/2008_Mumbai_attacks" title="2008 Mumbai attacks">2008 Mumbai attacks</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/10/india-pakistan-idUSSGE71903F20110210?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=hotStocksNews&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_campaign=DTN+Stock+Market%3A&amp;utm_content=Google+International" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2011/02/2011210151917721372.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The trial of <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> <a href="/wiki/Muslim" title="Muslim">Muslim</a> cleric <a href="/wiki/Abu_Bakar_Bashir" title="Abu Bakar Bashir">Abu Bakar Bashir</a> on <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorism</a> charges begins in <a href="/wiki/Jakarta" title="Jakarta">Jakarta</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.theage.com.au/breaking-news-world/bashir-terror-trial-begins-in-jakarta-20110210-1anur.html" rel="nofollow">(AAP via <i>The Age</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12406081" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Blind <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> activist <a href="/wiki/Chen_Guangcheng" title="Chen Guangcheng">Chen Guangcheng</a> says, in a secretly shot video, that he is still under <a href="/wiki/House_arrest" title="House arrest">house arrest</a> after being released from prison. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12413660" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rthk.org.hk/rthk/news/englishnews/20110210/news_20110210_56_733078.htm" rel="nofollow">(Radio Television Hong Kong)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5gh_YBnc-TUxyrqZm5_xBJy-JjYhg?docId=CNG.458a0d151f257d778da027d14bf85c6b.c1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="House of Commons of the United Kingdom">British House of Commons</a> votes 234-22 against <a href="/wiki/Hirst_v_United_Kingdom_(No_2)" title="Hirst v United Kingdom (No 2)">prisoners receiving the right to vote</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-12409426" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(UK)" title="Labour Party (UK)">British Labour</a> MP <a href="/wiki/Eric_Illsley" title="Eric Illsley">Eric Illsley</a> is jailed for 12 months for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_Parliamentary_expenses_scandal" title="United Kingdom Parliamentary expenses scandal">dishonestly claiming parliamentary expenses</a>. The sentence comes on the same day that <a href="/wiki/Jim_Devine" title="Jim Devine">Jim Devine</a>, another former Labour MP, is convicted of dishonestly claiming £8,385 of expenses by using false invoices for cleaning and printing work. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-12418223" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Utah_Jazz" title="Utah Jazz">Utah Jazz</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Utah_Jazz_head_coaches" title="List of Utah Jazz head coaches">head coach</a> <a href="/wiki/Jerry_Sloan" title="Jerry Sloan">Jerry Sloan</a>, the longest-tenured coach in any of <a href="/wiki/Major_professional_sports_leagues_in_the_United_States_and_Canada" title="Major professional sports leagues in the United States and Canada">North America's four major leagues</a>, announces his resignation effective immediately. Sloan, inducted in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_coaches_in_the_Basketball_Hall_of_Fame" title="List of coaches in the Basketball Hall of Fame">Basketball Hall of Fame</a> in 2009, had been with the Jazz since <a href="/wiki/1988%E2%80%9389_Utah_Jazz_season" title="1988–89 Utah Jazz season">1988</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://sports.espn.go.com/nba/news/story?id=6109031" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ray_Allen" title="Ray Allen">Ray Allen</a> scores his 2,561st 3-point shot, passing <a href="/wiki/Reggie_Miller" title="Reggie Miller">Reggie Miller</a> for the all-time NBA record for 3-point field goals made.</li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_11&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_11&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_11&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
