<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_Revolution_of_2011" title="Egyptian Revolution of 2011">Egyptian Revolution of 2011</a> / Downfall of <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a>:
<ul>
<li>Protests continue following last night's non-resignation speech of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President of Egypt</a> <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/10/live-blog-feb-11-egypt-protests" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/blog/2011/feb/11/egypt-protests-mubarak" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of pro-democracy demonstrators march on state television and presidential palaces as "Farewell Friday", the eighteenth day of protests against the <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Mubarak</a> regime, gets underway. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201121125158705862.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_ElBaradei" title="Mohamed ElBaradei">Mohamed ElBaradei</a> warns "Egypt will explode" in response to Mubarak's non-resignation speech last night. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/africa/02/10/egypt.protests.reax/index.html?iref=NS1" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Military leaders pledge to end the 30-year state of emergency law when the protests end. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201121161511674298.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The Mubaraks flee <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a> and head for the <a href="/wiki/Red_Sea" title="Red Sea">Red Sea</a> resort of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sharm_el-Sheikh" title="Sharm el-Sheikh">Sharm el-Sheikh</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/11/c_13728121.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/stories/2011/02/11/501364/main20031477.shtml" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4027193,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynetnews)</a></li>
<li>At least 5 people are killed by police in <a href="/wiki/Arish" title="Arish">Arish</a> in the <a href="/wiki/North_Sinai_Governorate" title="North Sinai Governorate">North Sinai Governorate</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/blog/2011/feb/11/egypt-hosni-mubarak-left-cairo#block-5" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Denmark" title="Prime Minister of Denmark">Prime Minister of Denmark</a> <a href="/wiki/Lars_L%C3%B8kke_Rasmussen" title="Lars Løkke Rasmussen">Lars Løkke Rasmussen</a>, speaking in <a href="/wiki/Copenhagen" title="Copenhagen">Copenhagen</a>, becomes the first <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> leader to tell Mubarak to resign, saying Mubarak is "history" and that he "made a huge blunder yesterday" by giving his non-resignation speech. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5jfxszj9wlBGrS1-dCx83NF6El6Bw?docId=5917466" rel="nofollow">(CP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_Egypt" title="Vice President of Egypt">Vice President</a> <a href="/wiki/Omar_Suleiman" title="Omar Suleiman">Omar Suleiman</a> announces on state television the resignation of <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> as <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President of Egypt</a> after 30 years in power. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12307698" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201121125158705862.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> resigns as <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President of Egypt</a> and hands power to <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Hussein_Tantawi" title="Mohamed Hussein Tantawi">Mohamed Hussein Tantawi</a>, head of the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Council_of_the_Armed_Forces" title="Supreme Council of the Armed Forces">Supreme Council of the Armed Forces</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/11/AR2011021102386.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/egyptNews/idAFLDE7192I62011021" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The death toll from clashes between rebels loyal to <a href="/wiki/George_Athor" title="George Athor">George Athor</a> and the army in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Southern_Sudan" title="Southern Sudan">Southern Sudan</a> rises to 100. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12430115" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivian</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Bolivia" title="President of Bolivia">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Evo_Morales" title="Evo Morales">Evo Morales</a> abandons an event in the south of the country after crowds booed him and threw <a href="/wiki/Dynamite" title="Dynamite">dynamite</a> in a protest over rising food prices. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12427057" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5hKQxQLMRfW7GXBWbjCny9tN73FXQ?docId=b5764ed4c5df40f9a335b37f54808d01" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2011/02/11/Dynamite-causes-Morales-to-cancel-speech/UPI-91971297432460/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> forces fire gas agents and rubber-coated bullets against <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinian</a> protesters in <a href="/wiki/Silwan" title="Silwan">Silwan</a>, injuring dozens.<a class="external text" href="http://www.muslimnews.co.uk/news/news.php?article=19638" rel="nofollow">(Muslim News)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.paltelegraph.com/palestine/west-bank/8455-clashes-erupted-after-friday-prayer-in-silwan.html" rel="nofollow">(The Palestine Telegraph)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The U.S. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Department_of_Agriculture" title="Department of Agriculture">Department of Agriculture</a> says it has deregulated a genetically engineered corn. See <a href="/wiki/Genetically_modified_food" title="Genetically modified food">genetically modified food</a>. The corn in question is designed for the manufacture of <a href="/wiki/Ethanol" title="Ethanol">ethanol</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/11/us-agriculture-usda-corn-idUSTRE71A71L20110211" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A road in <a href="/wiki/Copenhagen" title="Copenhagen">Copenhagen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a> has been proposed a new name after former US president <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Reagan" title="Ronald Reagan">Ronald Reagan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://jp.dk/uknews/article2336716.ece" rel="nofollow">(Jyllandsposten)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The first investigation into <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flight_Avia_Flight_7100" title="Flight Avia Flight 7100">yesterday's plane crash</a> at <a href="/wiki/Cork_Airport" title="Cork Airport">Cork Airport</a> is expected within a month; the airport remains closed today. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0211/cork.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>An American man is held responsible for the "cold-blooded murder" of two men in <a href="/wiki/Lahore" title="Lahore">Lahore</a>, Pakistan, by city police chief Aslam Tareen. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-12427518" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>China's foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Yang_Jiechi" title="Yang Jiechi">Yang Jiechi</a> visits <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a> as the countries agree a $10 billion trade deal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12427423" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> asks its embassies worldwide to appeal for aid to feed its population. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/asia/north-korea-sends-sos-to-world-to-feed-its-starving-people-2211240.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Computer security company <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/McAfee" title="McAfee">McAfee</a> says <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hacker_(computer_security)" title="Hacker (computer security)">hackers</a> based in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a> have targeted computer networks of global <a href="/wiki/Petroleum_industry" title="Petroleum industry">oil companies</a> and individuals in <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" title="Republic of China">Taiwan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Computer_insecurity" title="Computer insecurity">steal information</a> starting in 2009. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_633712.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Straits Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://world.globaltimes.cn/americas/2011-02/621760.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Global Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Liberia" title="President of Liberia">President of Liberia</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charles_Taylor_(Liberia)" title="Charles Taylor (Liberia)">Charles Taylor</a>'s trial in <a href="/wiki/The_Hague" title="The Hague">The Hague</a> is extended. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12427390" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Seven <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Somali_pirates" title="Somali pirates">Somali pirates</a> are charged with firearms offences in a <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysian</a> court, in a move that could see them hanged. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71A09G20110211?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> police arrest 13 people over two incidents of religious violence in which three people were killed and churches burnt. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/asia/221042/indonesia-arrests-13-over-religious-violence" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> activist <a href="/wiki/Chen_Guangcheng" title="Chen Guangcheng">Chen Guangcheng</a> and his wife are reportedly beaten after filming a secret video showing their <a href="/wiki/House_arrest" title="House arrest">house arrest</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12428385" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rthk.org.hk/rthk/news/englishnews/20110211/news_20110211_56_733315.htm" rel="nofollow">(Radio Television Hong Kong)</a></li>
<li>Anniversary of <a href="/wiki/Iranian_Revolution" title="Iranian Revolution">Iranian Revolution</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> marks the 32nd anniversary of its <a href="/wiki/Iranian_Revolution" title="Iranian Revolution">Revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irinn.ir" rel="nofollow">(IRINN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Iran" title="President of Iran">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad" title="Mahmoud Ahmadinejad">Mahmoud Ahmadinejad</a> insists that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iranian_people" title="Iranian people">nation</a> remains determined to continue its <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iranian_nuclear_programme" title="Iranian nuclear programme">nuclear path</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/164669.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li>Ahmadinejad said that the new <a href="/wiki/Middle_East" title="Middle East">Middle East</a> will be formed soon where there will be no room for the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irna.ir" rel="nofollow">(IRNA)</a></li>
<li>Iranian opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Mehdi_Karroubi" title="Mehdi Karroubi">Mehdi Karroubi</a> is placed under house arrest after calling for demonstrations in support of <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">the uprisings</a> in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/middle-east/iranian-opposition-leader-under-house-arrest-2210951.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Algerian_protests" title="2010–2011 Algerian protests">2010–2011 Algerian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Thousands of people, inspired by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_Revolution_of_2011" title="Egyptian Revolution of 2011">Egyptian Revolution of 2011</a>, take to the streets of <a href="/wiki/Algiers" title="Algiers">Algiers</a> to protest against their own regime and to call for the removal of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Algeria" title="President of Algeria">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Abdelaziz_Bouteflika" title="Abdelaziz Bouteflika">Abdelaziz Bouteflika</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/africa/2011/02/12/live-blog-feb-13-eye-algeria" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12438015" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110212-algeria-protest-defy-ban-demonstration-clash-police-algiers-bouteflika-egypt" rel="nofollow">(France24)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/ipad/thousands-demonstrate-in-algeria/story-fn6s850w-1226005122586" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>Algerian police and security forces attempt to prevent the people from participating in the illegal march for democracy and change in Algiers. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/12/c_13729299.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>The Algerian government shuts down the internet as <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Plastic_bullet" title="Plastic bullet">plastic bullets</a> are deployed and journalists, especially those seen with cameras, targeted by state-sponsored thugs. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/africaandindianocean/algeria/8320772/Algeria-shuts-down-internet-and-Facebook-as-protest-mounts.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of riot police crack down on those protesting against the ruling Bouteflika regime. Protesters chant "Bouteflika out!" <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/12/algerian-riot-police-protest-algiers" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.gulf-times.com/site/topics/article.asp?cu_no=2&amp;item_no=415815&amp;version=1&amp;template_id=57&amp;parent_id=56" rel="nofollow">(<i>Gulf Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/13/world/africa/13algeria.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HltzgRQYjgM" rel="nofollow">(euronews)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/africaandindianocean/algeria/8320273/Algerian-protesters-clash-with-police.html" rel="nofollow"><i>(The Daily Telegraph)</i></a></li>
<li>The opposition says approximately 5,000 people took part in today's attempt to bring down the Bouteflika regime. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/13/c_13729471.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>International response to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Algerian_protests" title="2010–2011 Algerian protests">2010–2011 Algerian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>A demonstration occurs from the streets of <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">Montreal</a> in <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> to the front of the Algerian consulate as people, including many Tunisians and Egyptians, join international calls for Abdelaziz Bouteflika's resignation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5igNMLCmsK4D_8o41M1TOo7kcTjdw?docId=CNG.4e201b9124c065f698a3b89b09e38576.1151" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.montrealgazette.com/news/Algerian+Montrealers+call+democracy/4272630/story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Montreal Gazette</i>)</a></li>
<li>A peaceful protest occurs at the initiative of the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=National_Coordination_for_Change_and_Democracy_in_Algeria&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="National Coordination for Change and Democracy in Algeria (page does not exist)">National Coordination for Change and Democracy in Algeria</a> in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> against Algerian police brutality, <a href="/wiki/Forced_disappearance" title="Forced disappearance">forced disappearances</a> and the state of emergency that the regime has imposed upon the country. <a class="external text" href="http://ireport.cnn.com/docs/DOC-554533?ref=feeds%2Foncnn" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Thousands of anti-government protesters gather in <a href="/wiki/Sana%27a" title="Sana'a">Sana'a</a> calling for the resignation of President <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a>, who has ruled the country since 1978. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201121211858966496.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jaoZWnvhll-OqIlQLyOlJK1WQCBw?docId=CNG.34b0a7cfb441605b61894f84b5a9eda2.f1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>Anti-government protesters march towards <a href="/wiki/Sana%27a_University" title="Sana'a University">Sana'a University</a>, chanting slogans such as "Get out, Get out Ali" and "The people want the regime to fall." <a class="external text" href="http://www.timeslive.co.za/world/article909790.ece/Yemen-revolt-begins-in-central-Sanaa" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times</i> LIVE)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/164919.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li>Demonstrators also attempt to celebrate yesterday's resignation of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">President of Egypt</a> <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a>, brought down by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_Revolution_of_2011" title="Egyptian Revolution of 2011">an 18-day popular revolution</a>, but police clamp down on the celebrations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12441246" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Yemeni police use clubs to beat those protesting against the Saleh regime, leaving Yemen's ally, the United States, in a "delicate position". <a class="external text" href="http://www.taipeitimes.com/News/front/archives/2011/02/13/2003495758" rel="nofollow">(<i>Taipei Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.radionz.co.nz/news/world/68386/march-broken-up-in-yemen" rel="nofollow">(Radio New Zealand)</a></li>
<li>The United States lifts its ban on freight flights from the country after finding Yemen to have sufficiently developed its airport security measures and that there would be "no problems with resuming cargo flights from Yemen anymore". <a class="external text" href="http://yemenpost.net/Detail123456789.aspx?ID=3&amp;SubID=3129&amp;MainCat=3" rel="nofollow">(<i>Yemen Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Yemen's government offers its "respect" for the choice of the Egyptian people to protest and force the resignation of Hosni Mubarak. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/egyptNews/idAFLDE71B01C20110212" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mehbooba_Mufti" title="Mehbooba Mufti">Mehbooba Mufti</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jammu_and_Kashmir_People%27s_Democratic_Party" title="Jammu and Kashmir People's Democratic Party">People's Democratic Party</a> (PDP) president, criticises the <a href="/wiki/Jammu_and_Kashmir" title="Jammu and Kashmir">Jammu and Kashmir</a> government for "dismissing the Kashmiri youth who led the summer unrest" as drug addicts and people from the <a href="/wiki/Lashkar-e-Taiba" title="Lashkar-e-Taiba">Lashkar-e-Taiba</a>, saying the situation is akin to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_Revolution_of_2011" title="Egyptian Revolution of 2011">Egypt</a> and announcing protest demonstrations for 14 February. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thehindu.com/news/national/article1448115.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hindu</i>)</a></li>
<li>An attack on police headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Kandahar" title="Kandahar">Kandahar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>, kills 16 officers and 3 civilians, and injures 53 others.<a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/13/world/asia/13afghanistan.html?partner=rss&amp;emc=rss" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2011/02/201121215356118383.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Italy" title="Government of Italy">Government of Italy</a> declares a humanitarian emergency after thousands of <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisian</a> immigrants land on the small island of <a href="/wiki/Lampedusa" title="Lampedusa">Lampedusa</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/02/20112122328974957.html" rel="nofollow">(Al-Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>At least 33 people die following a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bombing" title="Suicide bombing">suicide bombing</a> near the <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Samarra" title="Samarra">Samarra</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.news.yahoo.com/18/20110213/twl-death-toll-from-iraqi-suicide-attack-ba734b9.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> releases its inquiry into the <a href="/wiki/Gaza_flotilla_raid" title="Gaza flotilla raid">Gaza flotilla raid</a>, finding Israel violated international law and used "excessive, indiscriminate and disproportionate force" during the attack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jK3IgJl6rYAjWWgxJkbp_wkJmAsQ?docId=CNG.680158c3fc877f3521627185c89de338.be1" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The extent of looting of the <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Museum" title="Egyptian Museum">Egyptian Museum</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a> during the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a> is worse than previously announced. <a class="external text" href="http://thelede.blogs.nytimes.com/2011/02/12/latest-updates-on-egypts-transition/" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Julie_Andrews" title="Julie Andrews">Julie Andrews</a>, <a href="/wiki/Roy_Haynes" title="Roy Haynes">Roy Haynes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Juilliard_String_Quartet" title="Juilliard String Quartet">Juilliard String Quartet</a>, <a href="/wiki/The_Kingston_Trio" title="The Kingston Trio">the Kingston Trio</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dolly_Parton" title="Dolly Parton">Dolly Parton</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Ramones" title="The Ramones">The Ramones</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Beverly_Shea" title="George Beverly Shea">George Beverly Shea</a> win <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Lifetime_Achievement_Award" title="Grammy Lifetime Achievement Award">Grammy Lifetime Achievement Awards</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/13/us-grammys-lifetime-idUSTRE71C03B20110213" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least eleven people are killed during an election rally for the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Nigeria" title="President of Nigeria">President of Nigeria</a> <a href="/wiki/Goodluck_Jonathan" title="Goodluck Jonathan">Goodluck Jonathan</a> in <a href="/wiki/Port_Harcourt" title="Port Harcourt">Port Harcourt</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/13/us-nigeria-election-stampede-idUSTRE71B1RX20110213?WT" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A fire destroys 20 homes on the <a href="/wiki/Yakama_Indian_Reservation" title="Yakama Indian Reservation">Yakama Indian Reservation</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">US</a> state of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington_(U.S._state)" title="Washington (U.S. state)">Washington</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.yakima-herald.com/stories/2011/2/12/fire-that-destroyed-several-white-swan-homes-about-25-percent-contained" rel="nofollow">(<i>Yakima Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Myanmar" title="Myanmar">Myanmar</a> arrests the <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> owner and editor of the <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Myanmar_Times" title="Myanmar Times">Myanmar Times</a></i> newspaper, detained under immigration laws. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12440879" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/asia/221216/myanmar-times-editor-in-chief-arrested" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>A Pakistani court issues an <a href="/wiki/Arrest_warrant" title="Arrest warrant">arrest warrant</a> for former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Pakistan" title="President of Pakistan">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Pervez_Musharraf" title="Pervez Musharraf">Pervez Musharraf</a>, alleging his involvement in the <a href="/wiki/Assassination_of_Benazir_Bhutto" title="Assassination of Benazir Bhutto">assassination of Benazir Bhutto</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://apnews.myway.com/article/20110212/D9LB81BO0.html" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia/2011/02/20112129419939362.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Tammy Marquardt's 1995 conviction for the murder of her 2-year-old epileptic son is quashed by the Ontario Court of Appeal, remedying a <a href="/wiki/List_of_miscarriage_of_justice_cases#Canada" title="List of miscarriage of justice cases">miscarriage of justice</a> in Canada. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/canada/toronto/story/2011/02/10/tammy-marquardt-court546.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thestar.com/news/article/936281--15-years-later-court-overturns-child-murder-conviction" rel="nofollow">(<i>Toronto Star</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> railway minister <a href="/wiki/Liu_Zhijun" title="Liu Zhijun">Liu Zhijun</a> is placed under investigation for "serious disciplinary violations". <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/china/2011-02/12/c_13729242.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12440198" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/china/Chinese-railway-minister-sacked-awaits-possible-arrest/articleshow/7483748.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saeb_Erekat" title="Saeb Erekat">Saeb Erekat</a>, chief negotiator for the <a href="/wiki/Palestine_Liberation_Organization" title="Palestine Liberation Organization">Palestine Liberation Organization</a>, resigns after the <a href="/wiki/Palestine_Papers" title="Palestine Papers">Palestine Papers</a> were found to have been leaked from his office. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011212135152355248.html" rel="nofollow">(Aljazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Mixed_martial_arts" title="Mixed martial arts">mixed martial arts</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sergei_Kharitonov" title="Sergei Kharitonov">Sergei Kharitonov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ant%C3%B4nio_Silva_(fighter)" title="Antônio Silva (fighter)">Antônio Silva</a> advance to the semi-finals of the <a href="/wiki/Strikeforce_(mixed_martial_arts)" title="Strikeforce (mixed martial arts)">Strikeforce</a> World Grand Prix Heavyweight Tournament by defeating <a href="/wiki/Andrei_Arlovski" title="Andrei Arlovski">Andrei Arlovski</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fedor_Emelianenko" title="Fedor Emelianenko">Fedor Emelianenko</a>, respectively, at <i><a href="/wiki/Strikeforce:_Fedor_vs._Silva" title="Strikeforce: Fedor vs. Silva">Strikeforce: Fedor vs. Silva</a></i> in <a href="/wiki/East_Rutherford,_New_Jersey" title="East Rutherford, New Jersey">East Rutherford, New Jersey</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">US</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sherdog.com/news/news/Bigfoot-Batters-Fedor-Forces-Stoppage-30129" rel="nofollow">(Sherdog)</a></li>
<li>An investigation is launched after two horses are believed to have been electrocuted by underground cabling in the paddock at <a href="/wiki/Newbury_Racecourse" title="Newbury Racecourse">Newbury Racecourse</a> in <a href="/wiki/Berkshire" title="Berkshire">Berkshire</a>, England. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport1/hi/other_sports/horse_racing/9395743.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC Sport)</a></li>
</ul>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> plans to withdraw 10,000 troops from <a href="/wiki/Jammu_and_Kashmir" title="Jammu and Kashmir">Jammu and Kashmir</a> this year and renew peace talks. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5gUAbZFQ4fYWCx6DaPgunYO2Wo3ng?docId=CNG.8c103da1ea380e74948a1d04a4c553e8.861" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.hindustantimes.com/Centre-may-bring-back-at-least-10-000-troops-from-J-K/Article1-661766.aspx" rel="nofollow">(<i>Hindustan Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraq_War" title="Iraq War">Iraq War</a>: <a href="/wiki/Jeremy_Paxman" title="Jeremy Paxman">Jeremy Paxman</a> faces being punished by the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> after being judged to have violated the corporation's strict impartiality rules by writing an article for <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> in which he stated that <a href="/wiki/Tony_Blair" title="Tony Blair">Tony Blair</a>'s "lies" had led Britain to war with Iraq. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-1356590/Jeremy-Paxman-warned-BBC-impartiality-Iraq-war-article-Blairs-lies.html?ito=feeds-newsxml" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>People in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a> march on the presidential palace in <a href="/wiki/Sana%27a" title="Sana'a">Sana'a</a> in an attempt to bring down <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.asianage.com/international/yemeni-protesters-march-palace-363" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Asian Age</i>)</a></li>
<li>Police block the protesters who shout slogans such as "The Yemeni people want the fall of the regime" and "A Yemeni revolution after the Egyptian revolution", as Saleh postpones a visit to his <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> allies "due to the current circumstances in the region". <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/13/us-yemen-idUSTRE71C0L520110213" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/13/c_13730385.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>Police and people clash in <a href="/wiki/Sana%27a" title="Sana'a">Sana'a</a> on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">the third day of protests</a> against the regime of <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a> in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12443463" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5j3KvyddFmup05BIwGmxdzkf17Vww?docId=CNG.e6210a294125e6051fab15d1b9c3fb5a.c71" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li>Opposition leaders in <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> call for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Iranian_protests" title="2011 Iranian protests">nationwide anti-government rallies</a> on Monday, in attempts to mimic the recent <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Tunisian_revolution" title="2010–2011 Tunisian revolution">Tunisian</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_Revolution_of_2011" title="Egyptian Revolution of 2011">Egyptian</a> revolutions. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011212162526150718.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a>'s security forces monitor the people as opposition groups <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">call for protests tomorrow</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011213185556388117.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Egypt's army suspends the constitution and dissolves parliament with elections due in six months as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_Revolution_of_2011" title="Egyptian Revolution of 2011">people promise to continue demonstrating</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011213132610927713.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a>'s foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Ahmed_Ounaies" title="Ahmed Ounaies">Ahmed Ounaies</a> resigns over controversial compliments he paid to his French counterpart <a href="/wiki/Mich%C3%A8le_Alliot-Marie" title="Michèle Alliot-Marie">Michèle Alliot-Marie</a> which <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Tunisian_uprising" title="2010–2011 Tunisian uprising">angered people in Tunisia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201121314913447933.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Julian_Assange" title="Julian Assange">Julian Assange</a> of <a href="/wiki/WikiLeaks" title="WikiLeaks">WikiLeaks</a> hails the website's role in the revolts, crediting material published via the <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanese</a> newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/Al_Akhbar_(Lebanon)" title="Al Akhbar (Lebanon)">Al Akhbar</a></i> as "significantly influential" in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Tunisian_revolution" title="2010–2011 Tunisian revolution">the fall</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Zine_El_Abidine_Ben_Ali" title="Zine El Abidine Ben Ali">Zine El Abidine Ben Ali</a> regime in <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a>. He promises a "broad spectrum" of <a href="/wiki/United_States_diplomatic_cables_leak" title="United States diplomatic cables leak">fresh cables about Australia</a> involving a "number of large companies and international politics". <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5gNJhV-MEAbPHUuZ_WzQXzeXOrwAQ?docId=CNG.e6210a294125e6051fab15d1b9c3fb5a.621" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>U.S. military commander <a href="/wiki/Admiral_(United_States)" title="Admiral (United States)">Admiral</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mike_Mullen" title="Mike Mullen">Mike Mullen</a> visits <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> to "discuss security issues of mutual concern" according to <a href="/wiki/The_Pentagon" title="The Pentagon">The Pentagon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201121395356723720.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Women against <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Berlusconi</a>:
<ul>
<li>Tens of thousands of women hold nationwide protests in 200 cities against <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Prime Minister of Italy</a> <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Silvio Berlusconi</a>, whom they say has damaged the standing of women with his string of sex scandals. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12442833" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/italy/8321277/Italy-day-of-protests-in-200-cities-against-Berlusconi.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/ipad/italians-rally-against-berlusconi/story-fn6s850w-1226005449240" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>Solidarity protests by women abroad also occur, including one outside the Italian consulate in <a href="/wiki/Tokyo" title="Tokyo">Tokyo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.indianexpress.com/news/thousands-of-italian-women-rally-against-berlusconi/749557/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Indian Express</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>18 people are injured after a <a href="/wiki/Car_bomb" title="Car bomb">car bomb</a> is detonated in <a href="/wiki/Yala,_Thailand" title="Yala, Thailand">Yala</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2011/02/201121315920359878.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_Red_Cross" title="International Red Cross">International Red Cross</a> states that the <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombian</a> <a href="/wiki/FARC" title="FARC">FARC</a> rebel group has released its fourth captive over the past few days but failed to release two others. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/world/116122189.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Minneapolis Star-Tribune</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>'s Minister of State for Antiquities <a href="/wiki/Zahi_Hawass" title="Zahi Hawass">Zahi Hawass</a> says several pieces have been stolen from the <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Museum" title="Egyptian Museum">Egyptian Museum</a> during the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_Revolution_of_2011" title="Egyptian Revolution of 2011">revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/World/Story/STIStory_634540.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Straits Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/culture/2011-02/13/c_13730279.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>A giant <a href="/wiki/Andy_Scott_(sculptor)" title="Andy Scott (sculptor)">Andy Scott</a> sculpture is knocked over in a car accident in <a href="/wiki/Tullibody" title="Tullibody">Tullibody</a>, <a href="/wiki/Clackmannanshire" title="Clackmannanshire">Clackmannanshire</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-scotland-tayside-central-12443756" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bono" title="Bono">Bono</a> <a href="/wiki/Boer" title="Boer">Boer</a> controversy:
<ul>
<li>Irish pop star <a href="/wiki/Bono" title="Bono">Bono</a> walks into a "political minefield" in <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a> after apparently endorsing a song with the <a href="/wiki/Lyrics" title="Lyrics">lyrics</a>: "Shoot the <a href="/wiki/Boer" title="Boer">Boer</a>", a song currently appearing before the country's highest court. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12444061" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.mg.co.za/article/2011-02-13-bono-causes-stir-over-shoot-the-boer-song/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Mail &amp; Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/entertainment/music/bono-causes-stir-in-south-africa-over-shoot-the-farmer-song-20110213-1arww.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Steve_Hofmeyr" title="Steve Hofmeyr">Steve Hofmeyr</a> responds to Bono's comments by dumping <a href="/wiki/South_African_rand" title="South African rand">R</a>5 000 worth of <a href="/wiki/U2" title="U2">U2</a> concert tickets in the <a href="/wiki/Jukskei_River" title="Jukskei River">Jukskei River</a> and urges <a href="/wiki/Neil_Diamond" title="Neil Diamond">Neil Diamond</a> to "keep his political trap shut" as well. Hofmeyr's actions cause a stir on <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thenewage.co.za/10379-1007-53-Hofmeyr_dumps_U2_tickets_over_Bono_comments" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New Age</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.iol.co.za/tonight/music/twitter-buzz-after-steve-dumps-u2-tickets-1.1025559" rel="nofollow">(IOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.eyewitnessnews.co.za/articleprog.aspx?id=59320" rel="nofollow">(Primedia Broadcasting - Eyewitness News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_King%27s_Speech" title="The King's Speech">The King's Speech</a></i> wins seven awards at the <a href="/wiki/64th_British_Academy_Film_Awards" title="64th British Academy Film Awards">64th British Academy Film Awards</a> including best film and Best Actor for <a href="/wiki/Colin_Firth" title="Colin Firth">Colin Firth</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/entertainment-arts-12432378" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/53rd_Grammy_Awards" title="53rd Grammy Awards">53rd Grammy Awards</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dave_Haywood" title="Dave Haywood">Dave Haywood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Josh_Kear" title="Josh Kear">Josh Kear</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charles_Kelley" title="Charles Kelley">Charles Kelley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Scott_(singer)" title="Hillary Scott (singer)">Hillary Scott</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Song_of_the_Year" title="Grammy Award for Song of the Year">Grammy Award for Song of the Year</a> for the song "<a href="/wiki/Need_You_Now_(Lady_Antebellum_song)" title="Need You Now (Lady Antebellum song)">Need You Now</a>" performed by <a href="/wiki/Lady_Antebellum" title="Lady Antebellum">Lady Antebellum</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/awards/2011/02/grammy-awards-song-of-the-year.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Singer <a href="/wiki/Esperanza_Spalding" title="Esperanza Spalding">Esperanza Spalding</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Best_New_Artist" title="Grammy Award for Best New Artist">Grammy Award for Best New Artist</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://loadtest.story.news.yahoo.com/s/nm/20110214/music_nm/us_grammys_newartist" rel="nofollow">(Reuters vis Yahoo! News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arcade_Fire" title="Arcade Fire">Arcade Fire</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Album_of_the_Year" title="Grammy Award for Album of the Year">Grammy Award for Album of the Year</a> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Suburbs_(Arcade_Fire_album)" title="The Suburbs (Arcade Fire album)"><i>The Suburbs</i></a> <a class="external text" href="http://artsbeat.blogs.nytimes.com/2011/02/13/live-blogging-the-grammys/?src=twt&amp;twt=artsbeat#album-of-the-year-goes-to-arcade-fire" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Lady Antebellum wins the <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Record_of_the_Year" title="Grammy Award for Record of the Year">Grammy Award for Record of the Year</a> for "Need You Now". <a class="external text" href="http://artsbeat.blogs.nytimes.com/2011/02/13/live-blogging-the-grammys/?src=twt&amp;twt=artsbeat#album-of-the-year-goes-to-arcade-fire" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Board_of_directors" title="Board of directors">board of directors</a> of <a href="/wiki/NYSE_Euronext" title="NYSE Euronext">NYSE Euronext</a> meets to discuss a proposed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Merger" title="Merger">merger</a> with <a href="/wiki/Deutsche_B%C3%B6rse" title="Deutsche Börse">Deutsche Börse</a>, while New York's U.S. Senator, <a href="/wiki/Chuck_Schumer" title="Chuck Schumer">Chuck Schumer</a> tells reporters that he is confident the NYSE would run the merged entity. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/14/us-nyse-deutscheboerse-schumer-idUSTRE71C1V420110214" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> reports two more outbreaks of <a href="/wiki/Influenza_A_virus_subtype_H5N1" title="Influenza A virus subtype H5N1">bird flu</a> near <a href="/wiki/Seoul" title="Seoul">Seoul</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/business/2011/02/13/95/0501000000AEN20110213001500320F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a>'</i>s Moscow Correspondent <a href="/wiki/Luke_Harding" title="Luke Harding">Luke Harding</a>, who was expelled from <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, is issued a new entry visa ahead of <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Russia)" title="Minister of Foreign Affairs (Russia)">Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Lavrov" title="Sergey Lavrov">Sergey Lavrov</a>'s visit to <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idAFTRE71C14220110213" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/russia/20110213/162582570.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li>Pakistan's former foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Shah_Mehmood_Qureshi" title="Shah Mehmood Qureshi">Shah Mehmood Qureshi</a> dismisses claims by U.S. authorities that the American gunman who recently shot two Pakistanis dead is a diplomat. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/13/c_13730171.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>Nearly 1,000 <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisian</a> refugees arrive on the <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> island of <a href="/wiki/Lampedusa" title="Lampedusa">Lampedusa</a> overnight, a day after the government declared a humanitarian emergency. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jQWIKgiq3crIxhUnNxcMnoFKVfAw?docId=CNG.7019387216ceafe233df45fb263bc775.101" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Immigration_to_Canada" title="Immigration to Canada">Immigration to Canada</a> hits a record high, while <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Minister_of_Citizenship_and_Immigration_(Canada)" title="Minister of Citizenship and Immigration (Canada)">Minister of Citizenship and Immigration</a> <a href="/wiki/Jason_Kenney" title="Jason Kenney">Jason Kenney</a> states that abuse of the immigration system must end. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nationalpost.com/news/canada/Immigration+abuse+must+stop+minister/4275325/story.html" rel="nofollow">(National Post)</a></li>
</ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a> votes in its gun control referendum, rejecting the proposal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12441834" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/europe/2011/02/2011213115710819915.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> and <a href="/wiki/LGBT_rights_in_the_United_States" title="LGBT rights in the United States">LGBT rights</a> campaigner <a href="/wiki/Fred_Karger" title="Fred Karger">Fred Karger</a> launches a campaign in the <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">U.S. states</a> of <a href="/wiki/Iowa" title="Iowa">Iowa</a> and <a href="/wiki/New_Hampshire" title="New Hampshire">New Hampshire</a> aiming to become <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/13/republicans-gay-rights-presidential-race" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Observer</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a> releases two more <a href="/wiki/Political_prisoner" title="Political prisoner">political prisoners</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12441483" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hina_Rabbani_Khar" title="Hina Rabbani Khar">Hina Rabbani Khar</a> is appointed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foreign_Minister_of_Pakistan" title="Foreign Minister of Pakistan">Minister of Foreign Affairs</a> of <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> by <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Pakistan" title="Prime Minister of Pakistan">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Yousaf_Raza_Gillani" title="Yousaf Raza Gillani">Yousaf Raza Gillani</a> to become the first female Foreign Minister. <a class="external text" href="http://thestar.com.my/news/story.asp?file=/2011/2/12/nation" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Star</i>)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of protesters in <a href="/wiki/Dresden" title="Dresden">Dresden</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> form a <a href="/wiki/Human_chain" title="Human chain">human chain</a> to mark the 66th anniversary of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dresden_bombing" title="Dresden bombing">Dresden bombing</a> and to protest against racism. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110213-human-chain-dresden-marks-wwii-bombing" rel="nofollow">(France24)</a></li>
<li>Writing in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Observer" title="The Observer">The Observer</a></i>, British Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> defends his vision for a <a href="/wiki/Big_Society" title="Big Society">Big Society</a>, dismissing claims that it is a "cover" for spending cuts. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/Politics/David-Cameron-Defends-Big-Society-Against-Claims-Its-A-Cover-For-Spending-Cuts/Article/201102215929469?lpos=Politics_News_Your_Way_Region_3&amp;lid=NewsYourWay_ARTICLE_15929469_David_Cameron_Defends_Big_Society_Against_Claims_Its_A_Cover_For_Spending_Cuts" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sky News</i>)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least seven people are killed in clashes between rival militant groups in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iKOqV5EL1hBAJ-IKE1XJzAlT8wJg?docId=CNG.26f85a77fe573d0130a10eb475c1a65e.b31" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Julian_Assange" title="Julian Assange">Julian Assange</a>'s mother criticises leading figures in the U.S. government who called for her son's assassination on television, and expresses concerns that her son is being targeted by an American <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fatw%C4%81" title="Fatwā">fatwā</a> similar to <a href="/wiki/The_Satanic_Verses_controversy" title="The Satanic Verses controversy">the one brought against</a> the writer <a href="/wiki/Salman_Rushdie" title="Salman Rushdie">Salman Rushdie</a> in 1989. <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/breaking-news/fatwa-on-my-son-says-julian-assanges-mum/story-e6frf7jx-1226005567637" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Armed_Forces_of_Colombia" title="Revolutionary Armed Forces of Colombia">FARC</a> organisation in <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a> releases a fourth hostage in the past week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12444820" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Iranian_protests" title="2011 Iranian protests">2011 Iranian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Anti-regime protests are due to occur in <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011212162526150718.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Reports said that hundreds of protesters are in <a href="/wiki/Azadi_Square" title="Azadi Square">Azadi Square</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-14/iran-cheers-egypt-tunisia-revolts-as-ahmadinejad-stifles-domestic-dissent.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">Tear gas</a> is fired by police to disperse the opposition protesters. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12447225" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/MiddleEast/Article.aspx?id=208182&amp;R=R3" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011214232945422335.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>A protestor dies in <a href="/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/14/iran-opposition-killed-idUSHAF47403720110214" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">2011 Bahraini protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Anti-regime protests occur in <a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011213185556388117.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Injuries and deaths occur. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011214925802473.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Wefaq" title="Al-Wefaq">Al-Wefaq</a> MPs step down in protest at violence against pro-democracy demonstrators.<a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011215194859291708.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://gulfnews.com/news/gulf/bahrain/al-wefaq-bloc-pulls-out-of-bahrain-s-parliament-1.763950" rel="nofollow">(Gulf News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a> events:
<ul>
<li>New <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_Revolution" title="2011 Egyptian Revolution">protests</a> erupt in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> demanding a civilian leadership, an end to <a href="/wiki/Emergency_law_in_Egypt" title="Emergency law in Egypt">the emergency law</a> and better pay. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/meast/02/14/egypt.revolution/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12448413" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_diplomatic_cables_leak" title="United States diplomatic cables leak">Newly released cables</a> show U.S. officials referring to the head of Egypt's military <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Hussein_Tantawi" title="Mohamed Hussein Tantawi">Mohamed Hussein Tantawi</a> as "old and resistant to change". <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/14/wikileaks-cables-egyptian-military-head" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Protesters, including scholars and academics, in <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza</a> request that Egypt open the Rafah border. <a class="external text" href="http://www.tehrantimes.com/index_View.asp?code=235833" rel="nofollow">(<i>Tehran Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.maannews.net/eng/ViewDetails.aspx?ID=359811" rel="nofollow">(Ma'an News Agency)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>: Street battles take place between protesters and police in the <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Sana%27a" title="Sana'a">Sana'a</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12454983" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://yemenpost.net/Detail123456789.aspx?ID=3&amp;SubID=3137" rel="nofollow">(<i>Yemen Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nation.co.ke/News/world/-/1068/1107498/-/4hldmxz/-/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Nation Kenya</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201121211858966496.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Algerian_protests" title="2010–2011 Algerian protests">2010–2011 Algerian protests</a>: Youths clash with security forces in the northern <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algerian</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Akbou" title="Akbou">Akbou</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12460486" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://story.malaysiasun.com/index.php/ct/9/cid/b8de8e630faf3631/id/744537/cs/1/ht/Algerian-town-riots-create-friction-between-youths-and-police-/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Malaysia Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>The Algerian government says it will the end the <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">state of emergency</a>, in place since 1992, "within a few days". <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/Algeria-lifts-emergency-rule-as-protests-rage/articleshow/7496089.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/British_Army" title="British Army">British Army</a> soldier from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2nd_Battalion,_The_Parachute_Regiment" title="2nd Battalion, The Parachute Regiment">2nd Battalion, The Parachute Regiment</a> is killed in an explosion in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-12460051" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Scientists blame chemicals for <a href="/wiki/Vincent_van_Gogh" title="Vincent van Gogh">Vincent van Gogh</a>'s bright yellows turning brown. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/science-environment-12453610" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Central_Bank_of_Egypt" title="Central Bank of Egypt">Central Bank of Egypt</a> closes <a href="/wiki/Bank" title="Bank">banks</a> as a result of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.voanews.com/breaking-news/2011/02/13/egypts-banks-to-close-as-labor-unrest-spreads/" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> records a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trade_surplus" title="Trade surplus">trade surplus</a> of $6.5 billion for <a href="/wiki/January" title="January">January</a>, less than expected. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnbc.com/id/41570491" rel="nofollow">(CNBC)</a></li>
<li>A court in the city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lago_Agrio" title="Lago Agrio">Lago Agrio</a>, on behalf of 30,000 <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuadorean</a> people, orders <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> oil company <a href="/wiki/Chevron_Corporation" title="Chevron Corporation">Chevron</a> to pay more than $8 billion in environmental damages for dumping <a href="/wiki/Wastewater" title="Wastewater">wastewater</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Amazon_River" title="Amazon River">Amazon River</a> twenty years ago. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/14/ecuador-chevron-plaintiff-idUSN149620320110214" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-14/chevron-to-appeal-adverse-judgment-in-ecuador-pollution-case.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12460333" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/General_Motors" title="General Motors">General Motors</a> announces that it will pay its <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Hourly_worker" title="Hourly worker">hourly workers</a> more than $4000 each as a share of <a href="/wiki/Profit_(economics)" title="Profit (economics)">profits</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.freep.com/article/20110214/BUSINESS0101/110214013/1318/HSS1201/GM-says-ll-pay-hourly-workers-bonuses-topping-4-000" rel="nofollow">(<i>Detroit Free Press</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eurozone" title="Eurozone">Eurozone</a> finance ministers agree to set up a permanent bail-out fund of €500 billion - the <a href="/wiki/European_Stability_Mechanism" title="European Stability Mechanism">European Stability Mechanism</a> (ESM). This replaces the <a href="/wiki/European_Financial_Stability_Facility" title="European Financial Stability Facility">European Financial Stability Facility</a> (EFSF). <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/business-12460527" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Fourteen people <a href="/wiki/Central_American_Airways_Flight_731" title="Central American Airways Flight 731">die in a plane crash</a> in <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduras</a> including a deputy minister in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Honduras" title="Government of Honduras">Government of Honduras</a> <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Rodolfo_Robelo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Rodolfo Robelo (page does not exist)">Rodolfo Robelo</a> and former finance minister <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Carlos_Chahin&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Carlos Chahin (page does not exist)">Carlos Chahin</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12458867?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_Government_of_Australia" title="Federal Government of Australia">Federal Government of Australia</a> is helping the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> investigate Australians involved with the <a href="/wiki/WikiLeaks" title="WikiLeaks">WikiLeaks</a> website according to <a href="/wiki/Julian_Assange" title="Julian Assange">Julian Assange</a>, who requests that Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Julia_Gillard" title="Julia Gillard">Julia Gillard</a> and Attorney-General <a href="/wiki/Robert_McClelland_(Australian_politician)" title="Robert McClelland (Australian politician)">Robert McClelland</a> reveal every detail of assistance to foreign governments. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2011/02/14/3137972.htm?section=justin" rel="nofollow">(ABC News and Current Affairs)</a></li>
<li>Ireland's <a href="/wiki/Fine_Gael" title="Fine Gael">Fine Gael</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Enda_Kenny" title="Enda Kenny">Enda Kenny</a> travels to <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> to brief <a href="/wiki/Angela_Merkel" title="Angela Merkel">Angela Merkel</a> on matters of economic concern. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0213/politics.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> calls for a permanent ceasefire on the <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>-<a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a> border near the <a href="/wiki/Preah_Vihear_Temple" title="Preah Vihear Temple">Preah Vihear Temple</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.voanews.com/breaking-news/2011/02/14/un-security-council-urges-permanent-cease-fire-on-thai-cambodian-frontier/" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>11 members of a family are found dead in eastern <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a> after being kidnapped by <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Ugandan</a> Islamist rebels. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71D0KE20110214" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessweek.com/news/2011-02-14/ugandan-rebels-kill-12-in-congo-s-north-kivu-local-leader-says.html" rel="nofollow">(Business Week)</a></li>
<li>Supporters of 23-year-old <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bradley_Manning" title="Bradley Manning">Bradley Manning</a>, including a member of the legal advocacy team, criticise the <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">White House</a> for its "thuggish behaviour" and "torture" in trying to break the soldier by pressuring him to implicate <a href="/wiki/Julian_Assange" title="Julian Assange">Julian Assange</a> in the alleged theft of <a href="/wiki/United_States_diplomatic_cables_leak" title="United States diplomatic cables leak">250,000 documents</a> the U.S. government wished to keep secret. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2011/02/14/3137816.htm?section=world" rel="nofollow">(ABC News and Current Affairs)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Abu_Bakar_Ba%27asyir" title="Abu Bakar Ba'asyir">Abu Bakar Ba'asyir</a>'s trial resumes in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12445335" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/asia-pacific/2011/02/201121442836375689.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> <a href="/wiki/Feng_shui" title="Feng shui">feng shui</a> master Tony Chan loses his appeal to inherit the fortune of <a href="/wiki/Nina_Wang" title="Nina Wang">Nina Wang</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12445500" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Mumtaz Qadri is charged with murdering the <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Punjab,_Pakistan" title="Governor of Punjab, Pakistan">Governor of Punjab</a> <a href="/wiki/Salmaan_Taseer" title="Salmaan Taseer">Salmaan Taseer</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> court. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-12445519" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<ul>

<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> puts forward a <a href="/wiki/United_States_federal_budget" title="United States federal budget">budget</a> for 2012 proposing heavy spending cuts but still predicting substantial <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Budget_Deficit" title="United States Budget Deficit">budget deficits</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://money.cnn.com/2011/02/14/news/economy/obama_budget_spending_cuts/index.htm?eref=edition&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/10_Downing_Street" title="10 Downing Street">10 Downing Street</a> receives a new cat to boost the battle against mice seen on television scuttling past British prime minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/lifeandstyle/2011/feb/14/10-downing-street-cat-larry" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> votes to extend the <a href="/wiki/Patriot_Act" title="Patriot Act">Patriot Act</a> for another nine months. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/politics/2011/02/14/house-representatives-votes-extend-patriot-act/#" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>

<ul>

<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> lodges an official complaint against the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> after America's landing of a military plane loaded with undeclared "sensitive material", including guns, drugs and satellite phones, leading the Argentinian government to express concerns that the U.S. was attempting to sneak its cargo into the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/15/argentina-us-weapons-country" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State" title="United States Secretary of State">United States Secretary of State</a> <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> outlines a new policy on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Internet_freedom" title="Internet freedom">Internet freedom</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/15/world/15clinton.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/UNASUR_Constitutive_Treaty" title="UNASUR Constitutive Treaty">UNASUR Constitutive Treaty</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Union_of_South_American_Nations" title="Union of South American Nations">Union of South American Nations</a> will come into force on March 11th, following the deposit of its ninth instrument of ratification, by the <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Uruguay" title="Foreign relations of Uruguay">Uruguayan government</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.itamaraty.gov.br/sala-de-imprensa/notas-a-imprensa/entrada-em-vigor-do-tratado-constitutivo-da-unasul" rel="nofollow">(Brazilian Foreign Ministry)</a></li>

<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islamic</a> morality police arrest over 80 <a href="/wiki/Muslim" title="Muslim">Muslims</a> in <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> to prevent them from celebrating <a href="/wiki/Valentine%27s_Day" title="Valentine's Day">Valentine's Day</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12466875" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Prime Minister of Italy</a> <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Silvio Berlusconi</a> is <a href="/wiki/Indictment" title="Indictment">indicted</a> on charges of paying for sex with an underaged girl and <a href="/wiki/Abuse_of_power" title="Abuse of power">abuse of power</a> in the so-called <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rubygate" title="Rubygate">Rubygate</a> scandal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12083491" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/15/AR2011021500612.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>A coroner has given his verdict into the <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Linda_Norgrove" title="Death of Linda Norgrove">death of Linda Norgrove</a> by stating that the soldier who threw the grenade had "acted unaware of Linda's presence". <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/UK-News/Afghanistan-Family-Of-Linda-Norgrove-Attend-Inquest-Into-Her-Death-Following-Failed-Rescue-Bid/Article/201102315931433?lpos=UK_News_Carousel_Region_0&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15931433_Afghanistan%3A_Family_Of_Linda_Norgrove_Attend_Inquest_Into_Her_Death_Following_Failed_Rescue_Bid" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>Amanda Knox's parents have been indicted for allegedly libeling police in Perugia, Italy in statements made surrounding the <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Meredith_Kercher" title="Murder of Meredith Kercher">murder of Meredith Kercher</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/europe/02/15/italy.knox.parents/index.html?hpt=T2" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>An analysis of the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">FBI</a>'s scientific work in the investigation of the <a href="/wiki/2001_anthrax_attacks" title="2001 anthrax attacks">2001 anthrax attacks</a> on the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> finds that the Bureau overstated the strength of the links to a supply held by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bruce_Ivins" title="Bruce Ivins">Bruce Ivins</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/16/us/16anthrax.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/U.S._Immigration_and_Customs_Enforcement" title="U.S. Immigration and Customs Enforcement">U.S. Immigration and Customs Enforcement</a> officers are shot while travelling between <a href="/wiki/Monterrey" title="Monterrey">Monterrey</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mexico_City" title="Mexico City">Mexico City</a> with one officer dying. <a class="external text" href="http://news.blogs.cnn.com/2011/02/15/2-ice-agents-shot-while-driving-in-mexico/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinian</a> teen is released from <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> custody after the police officer who alledegly <a href="/wiki/Police_brutality" title="Police brutality">beat a confession</a> out of him fails to show up to an inquiry. The teenager was held in Israel for 7 months for allegedly throwing rocks before being released.<a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/news/national/police-revoke-charges-against-east-jerusalem-teen-allegedly-beaten-by-police-during-detainment-1.343577" rel="nofollow">(Haaretz)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> <a href="/wiki/Knesset" title="Knesset">Knesset</a> has passed a bill making <a href="/wiki/Boycotts_of_Israel" title="Boycotts of Israel">boycotting Israeli</a> individuals or organizations illegal.<a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/news/national/knesset-committee-approves-bill-allowing-israel-boycotters-to-be-fined-1.343596" rel="nofollow">(Haaretz)</a></li>
<li>A proposal by a consortium of private contractors to attack <a href="/wiki/WikiLeaks" title="WikiLeaks">WikiLeaks</a> and to discredit journalists in favour of the website - including <a href="/wiki/Glenn_Greenwald" title="Glenn Greenwald">Glenn Greenwald</a> - is uncovered after thousands of e-mails are leaked onto the internet, some of which call for people who donate to be tracked and intimidated. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/americas/the-us-bank-and-the-secret-plan-to-destroy-wikileaks-2215059.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Summer Olympics</a> timetable is released. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/olympic_games/london_2012/9397378.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC Sport)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/International_Cricket_Council" title="International Cricket Council">International Cricket Council</a> bans the use of <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> by players and officials during the <a href="/wiki/2011_Cricket_World_Cup" title="2011 Cricket World Cup">2011 Cricket World Cup</a> due to fears that players will be contacted by illegal <a href="/wiki/Bookmaker" title="Bookmaker">bookmakers</a> during matches. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/sport/cricket/icc-bans-twitter-use-during-cup-matches-due-to-corruption-fears-20110215-1av5x.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>Foxcliffe Hickory Wind, a <a href="/wiki/Scottish_Deerhound" title="Scottish Deerhound">Scottish Deerhound</a>, wins <a href="/wiki/List_of_Best_in_Show_winners_of_the_Westminster_Kennel_Club_Dog_Show" title="List of Best in Show winners of the Westminster Kennel Club Dog Show">Best in Show</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Westminster_Kennel_Club_Dog_Show" title="Westminster Kennel Club Dog Show">Westminster Kennel Club Dog Show</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://sports.espn.go.com/espn/news/story?id=6126781&amp;campaign=rss&amp;source=ESPNHeadlines&amp;utm_source=%23frankguillen&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_campaign=FrankGuillen+Buzz" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
