<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> February 16, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-02-16</span>)</span> (Wednesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_16&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_16&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_16&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Piracy
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> will fly the bodies of eight <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Piracy_in_Somalia" title="Piracy in Somalia">Somali pirates</a> killed in a commando raid on a <a href="/wiki/Cargo_ship" title="Cargo ship">freighter</a> last month from <a href="/wiki/Muscat,_Oman" title="Muscat, Oman">Muscat, Oman</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/02/16/15/0200000000AEN20110216005500315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/HMS_Cornwall_(F99)" title="HMS Cornwall (F99)">HMS <i>Cornwall</i></a> from the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> frees five <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> fishermen held by Somali pirates. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Article/201009115933218" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> state TV reports clashes between pro-<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Iran" title="Government of Iran">government</a> and anti-government forces at a funeral for someone killed in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Iranian_protests" title="2011 Iranian protests">2011 Iranian protests</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dawn.com/2011/02/16/clashes-at-funeral-of-iran-protest-victim-tv.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Dawn</i>)</a></li>
<li>Fourteen people are hurt in clashes between <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> protestors and security forces in <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a> as <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">protests</a> spread. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110216-14-injured-libya-clashes" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France 24)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/20112167051422444.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> Ministry for Health estimates that at least 365 people were killed and 5,500 injured in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://en.rian.ru/world/20110216/162636598.html" rel="nofollow">(RIA Novosti)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Yemen" title="Law enforcement in Yemen">Yemeni police</a> shoot and kill two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">protestors</a> in the southern city of <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/s/afp/20110216/wl_afp/yemenpoliticsunrest_20110216165553" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombian</a> <a href="/wiki/FARC" title="FARC">FARC</a> movement releases another two hostages. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5j3OsbqxYUh7Uj3nukN03GHyo-84Q?docId=CNG.cf88f624a89cb6ef996e074922a948f5.b31" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>U.S. <a href="/wiki/Pop_music" title="Pop music">pop</a> singer <a href="/wiki/Bruno_Mars" title="Bruno Mars">Bruno Mars</a> pleads guilty to <a href="/wiki/Cocaine" title="Cocaine">cocaine</a> possession in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Las_Vegas,_Nevada" title="Las Vegas, Nevada">Las Vegas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nevada" title="Nevada">Nevada</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.lasvegassun.com/news/2011/feb/16/pop-singer-bruno-mars-pleads-guilty-cocaine-charge/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Las Vegas Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>Researchers from <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Natural_History_Museum,_London" title="Natural History Museum, London">Natural History Museum</a> claim that ancient skulls found in <a href="/wiki/Gough%27s_Cave" title="Gough's Cave">Gough's Cave</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Cheddar_Gorge" title="Cheddar Gorge">Cheddar Gorge</a> in the southwestern <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> county of <a href="/wiki/Somerset" title="Somerset">Somerset</a> show signs of <a href="/wiki/Cannibalism" title="Cannibalism">cannibalism</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/2011/02/16/idINIndia-54947920110216?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=entertainmentNews&amp;WT.tsrc=Social%20Media&amp;WT.z_smid=twtr-RtrsIN_Entrtnmt&amp;WT.z_smid_dest=Twitter" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jens_Weidmann" title="Jens Weidmann">Jens Weidmann</a> is chosen to succeed <a href="/wiki/Axel_A._Weber" title="Axel A. Weber">Axel A. Weber</a> as President of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deutsche_Bundesbank" title="Deutsche Bundesbank">Deutsche Bundesbank</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.faz.net/s/Rub0E9EEF84AC1E4A389A8DC6C23161FE44/Doc~E66115796AF004491B99C2ABCC384205A~ATpl~Ecommon~Scontent.html" rel="nofollow">(FAZ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/BT-CO-20110216-703981.html" rel="nofollow">(WSJ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Borders_Group" title="Borders Group">Borders Group</a>, the second largest bookstore chain in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, files for <a href="/wiki/Bankruptcy" title="Bankruptcy">bankruptcy</a> with plans to sell at least 200 stores. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-16/borders-book-chain-files-for-bankruptcy-protection-with-1-29-billion-debt.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Northern_Territory" title="Northern Territory">Northern Territory</a> Emergency Service in the north of <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> warns residents in low-lying coastal areas including in the capital <a href="/wiki/Darwin,_Northern_Territory" title="Darwin, Northern Territory">Darwin</a> ahead of <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Australian_region_cyclone_season" title="2010–11 Australian region cyclone season">Tropical Cyclone Carlos</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/breaking-news/national/darwin-told-to-prepare-evacuation-plan/story-e6frfku9-1226007041677" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a></li>
<li>Explosions occur following an accident at a <a href="/wiki/Tanzania_People%27s_Defence_Force" title="Tanzania People's Defence Force">Tanzania People's Defence Force</a> ammunition dump near the <a href="/wiki/Julius_Nyerere_International_Airport" title="Julius Nyerere International Airport">Julius Nyerere International Airport</a> in <a href="/wiki/Dar_es_Salaam" title="Dar es Salaam">Dar es Salaam</a> with casualties reported. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/16/AR2011021604397.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://ireport.cnn.com/docs/DOC-556802" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>At least four people die and dozens injured following a train crash in <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>, <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://dunyanews.tv/index.php?key=Q2F0SUQ9MyNOaWQ9MjA0NDg=" rel="nofollow">(Dunya News)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Whaling_in_Japan" title="Whaling in Japan">Japan's whaling fleet</a> is leaving the <a href="/wiki/Antarctic" title="Antarctic">Antarctic</a> under pressure from conservationists and diplomats. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/environment/whale-watch/japan-to-quit-antarctic-whaling-20110216-1aw0k.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12477398" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abduwali_Muse" title="Abduwali Muse">Abduwali Muse</a>, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Piracy_in_Somalia" title="Piracy in Somalia">Somali pirate</a>, is sentenced to almost 34 years in prison in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> for his role in attempting to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maritime_hijacking" title="Maritime hijacking">hijack</a> the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MV_Maersk_Alabama" title="MV Maersk Alabama">MV <i>Maersk Alabama</i></a>. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Blotter/somali-pirate-muse-sentenced-34-years/story?id=12930166" rel="nofollow">(ABC News USA)</a></li>
<li>Three <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._marshal" title="U.S. marshal">U.S. marshals</a> are shot in <a href="/wiki/Elkins,_West_Virginia" title="Elkins, West Virginia">Elkins</a>, <a href="/wiki/West_Virginia" title="West Virginia">West Virginia</a>, while trying to serve a <a href="/wiki/Arrest_warrant" title="Arrest warrant">warrant</a>, resulting in the death of one marshal and the shooter. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wvgazette.com/News/201102160569" rel="nofollow">(<i>West Virginia Gazette</i>)</a></li>
<li>In an FBI Eurasian Organized Crime Task Force <b><a href="/wiki/Operation_Power_Outage" title="Operation Power Outage">Operation Power Outage</a></b>, 74 members of <a href="/wiki/Armenian_Power" title="Armenian Power">Armenian Power</a> criminal syndicate have been arrested on charges of racketeering offenses, bank fraud schemes, kidnappings, and drug trafficking. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/CRIME/02/16/california.armenian.power/#" rel="nofollow">(<i>CNN</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>An ally of outgoing <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burmese</a> ruler General <a href="/wiki/Than_Shwe" title="Than Shwe">Than Shwe</a> resigns two weeks into the new parliament. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12483025" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irrawaddy.org/highlight.php?art_id=20770" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irrawaddy</i>)</a></li>
<li>Celebrations marking the birthday of <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-il" title="Kim Jong-il">Kim Jong-il</a> take place in <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12469577" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">Protesters in Bahrain</a> continue to occupy a square in the capital, <a href="/wiki/Manama" title="Manama">Manama</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201121635518925202.html#" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Hawaii_Senate" title="Hawaii Senate">Hawaii Senate</a> approves <a href="/wiki/Hawaii_Senate_Bill_232" title="Hawaii Senate Bill 232">Hawaii Senate Bill 232</a> legalising <a href="/wiki/Civil_union" title="Civil union">civil unions</a> for gay and lesbian couples and will be sent to the <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Hawaii" title="Governor of Hawaii">Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Neil_Abercrombie" title="Neil Abercrombie">Neil Abercrombie</a> for approval. <a class="external text" href="http://www.staradvertiser.com/news/breaking/116352634.html#" rel="nofollow">(<i>Honolulu Star-Advertiser</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/IBM" title="IBM">IBM</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Watson_(artificial_intelligence_software)" title="Watson (artificial intelligence software)">Watson</a> <a href="/wiki/Artificial_intelligence" title="Artificial intelligence">artificial intelligence</a> program wins on the U.S. quiz show <i><a href="/wiki/Jeopardy!" title="Jeopardy!">Jeopardy!</a></i>, defeating <a href="/wiki/Brad_Rutter" title="Brad Rutter">Brad Rutter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ken_Jennings" title="Ken Jennings">Ken Jennings</a>, the series' most successful contestants. <a class="external text" href="http://www.pcmag.com/article2/0,2817,2380489,00.asp?kc=PCRSS03069TX1K0001121&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+ziffdavis%2Fpcmag%2Fbreakingnews+%28PCMag.com+Breaking+News%29&amp;utm_content=Google+International#" rel="nofollow">(PC Mag)</a> <i>Watson</i> used <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, among other sources, as its <a href="/wiki/Knowledge_base" title="Knowledge base">knowledge base</a> <i><a class="external text" href="http://www.vancouversun.com/entertainment/Watson+computer+Ottawa+roots/4290481/story.html" rel="nofollow">(The Vancouver Sun)</a></i> <i><a class="external text" href="http://www.npr.org/2011/02/11/133686004/IBM-Computer-Faces-Off-Against-Jeopardy-Champs" rel="nofollow">(NPR)</a></i> <i><a class="external text" href="http://www.ibm.com/ibm100/us/en/icons/watson/" rel="nofollow">(IBM)</a></i></li>
<li>It is announced that people who suffer from <a href="/wiki/Laron_syndrome" title="Laron syndrome">Laron syndrome</a> have a gene that inhibits cancer. <a class="external text" href="http://www.scientificamerican.com/article.cfm?id=defective-growth-gene-in-dwarfism" rel="nofollow">(Scientific American)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.pbs.org/newshour/rundown/2011/02/dwarfism-gene-may-offer-protection-from-cancer-diabetes.html" rel="nofollow">(PBS)</a></li>
</ul>

</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lance_Armstrong" title="Lance Armstrong">Lance Armstrong</a> officially announces his retirement from professional <a href="/wiki/Cycling" title="Cycling">cycling</a>, again. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/SPORT/02/16/lance.armstrong/index.html?hpt=T2" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">2011 Bahraini protests</a>:

<li><a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a> police launch an attack on protesters in the <a href="/wiki/Pearl_Roundabout" title="Pearl Roundabout">Pearl Roundabout</a> in the capital <a href="/wiki/Manama" title="Manama">Manama</a>, using <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Baton_(law_enforcement)" title="Baton (law enforcement)">batons</a> to disperse the crowd. <a class="external text" href="http://globalvoicesonline.org/2011/02/17/bahrain-breaking-news-police-attack-protesters-at-pearl-roundabout/?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(Global voices)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/s/ap/ml_bahrain_protests" rel="nofollow">(AP via Yahoo!)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/meast/02/16/bahrain.protests/index.html?eref=rss_topstories&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+rss%2Fcnn_topstories+%28RSS%3A+Top+Stories%29&amp;utm_content=Google+International#" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12490286?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A thousand or more non-citizen residents of <a href="/wiki/Kuwait" title="Kuwait">Kuwait</a> demonstrated yesterday demanding <a href="/wiki/Rights" title="Rights">rights</a> given to Kuwaiti citizen. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/energyOilNews/idAFLDE71H22B20110218" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a><a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011218183819888842.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera English)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/meast/02/18/kuwait.protests/index.html?iref=allsearch" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Police and indigenous protesters clash in <a href="/wiki/Panama" title="Panama">Panama</a> during a protest against changes to the country's mining law. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5gi17WcBb7cR99qQ77ApSKDiEwNbA?docId=CNG.caf89b431a9c66f3e75cf5c8f5b2c68e.ed1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>At least 37 people are killed and others are wounded in a U.S.-led airstrike in <a href="/wiki/Kunar_Province" title="Kunar Province">Kunar Province</a>, <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/165845.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li>Retired <a href="/wiki/Central_Intelligence_Agency" title="Central Intelligence Agency">CIA</a> officer-turned-political activist <a href="/wiki/Ray_McGovern" title="Ray McGovern">Ray McGovern</a> is thrown out, bloodied and arrested while protesting a speech given by <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Internet_freedom" title="Internet freedom">internet freedom</a> at <a href="/wiki/George_Washington_University" title="George Washington University">George Washington University</a> in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> <a href="/wiki/Veterans_for_Peace" title="Veterans for Peace">Veterans for Peace</a> requests that Clinton apologise. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/165779.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://americanindependent.com/170062/anti-war-protester-seized-claims-he-was-bloodied-by-guards-at-clinton-address-about-free-speech" rel="nofollow">(American Independent)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">2011 Bahraini protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Troops and tanks patrol <a href="/wiki/Manama" title="Manama">Manama</a> as the Bahraini military sets up checkpoints; a ban on public gatherings is announced. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112184122210251.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/King_of_Bahrain" title="King of Bahrain">King of Bahrain</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hamad_ibn_Isa_Al_Khalifa" title="Hamad ibn Isa Al Khalifa">Hamad ibn Isa Al Khalifa</a> visits and praises the military for its nighttime crackdown on pro-democracy demonstrators in <a href="/wiki/Manama" title="Manama">Manama</a>, lauding their "bravery and readiness to assume their national duties". <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/165781.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of people attend the first funerals of those killed by security forces in yesterday's massacre at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pearl_Square" title="Pearl Square">Pearl Square</a>, many making known their anger at the Bahraini regime. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12502820" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a>'s military fires at hundreds of mourners advancing towards <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pearl_Square" title="Pearl Square">Pearl Square</a> with reports of live ammunition being used. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/19/world/middleeast/19bahrain.html?hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Djibouti_protests" title="2011 Djibouti protests">2011 Djibouti protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Police shoot <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> at thousands of people demonstrating against the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ismail_Omar_Guelleh" title="Ismail Omar Guelleh">Ismail Omar Guelleh</a> regime in <a href="/wiki/Djibouti" title="Djibouti">Djibouti</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201121816513686216.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Jordanian_protests" title="2011 Jordanian protests">2011 Jordanian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>At least 8 people are injured during an attack on a pro-democracy protest rally in <a href="/wiki/Amman" title="Amman">Amman</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/165886.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/photo/2011-02/19/c_13739653.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li>Anti-regime protests continue overnight after yesterday's "Day of Rage". Funerals of those killed due today. <a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> lists 24 killed and many wounded. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12502657" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.hrw.org/en/news/2011/02/17/libya-security-forces-fire-day-anger-demonstrations" rel="nofollow">(Human Rights Watch)</a></li>
<li>Libyans in <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a> take over <a class="external text" href="http://libya.blog-video.tv/" rel="nofollow">a radio station</a>; it broadcasts its message to the world - calling on the international media to cover what "the criminal <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Gaddafi</a>" is doing - while <a class="external text" href="http://www.libyafeb17.com/" rel="nofollow">libya17.com</a> posts videos in English. <a class="external text" href="http://blog.foreignpolicy.com/posts/2011/02/18/radio_free_benghazi" rel="nofollow">(<i>Foreign Policy</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> shuts off access to the <a href="/wiki/Internet" title="Internet">Internet</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://techcrunch.com/2011/02/18/reports-libya-follows-egypts-lead-starts-shutting-off-internet-services/?utm_source=%23frankguillen&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_campaign=FrankGuillen+Buzz&amp;utm_content=Google+Feedfetcher" rel="nofollow">(TechCrunch)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> reports that its signal to Libya is being blocked. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/libyaNews/idAFLDE71H2A120110218" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Iraqi_protests" title="2011 Iraqi protests">2011 Iraqi protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Anti-regime protests occur in <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a>, with demonstrators calling for a larger demonstration next Friday as part of an "Iraqi revolution". <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/meast/02/18/iraq.protests/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/video/2011-02/18/c_13738367.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>Deaths and injuries occur during anti-regime demonstrations in <a href="/wiki/Sulaymaniyah" title="Sulaymaniyah">Sulaymaniyah</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.net/2011/02/17/deaths-reported-in-fresh-protests-in-iraq/" rel="nofollow">(euronews)</a></li>
<li>Anti-regime protests occur in the autonomous Kurdish region of northern Iraq. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011218104510878522.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/165817.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/17/AR2011021706418.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Anti-regime protesters gather for the largest of eight days of demonstrations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-18/largest-yemen-protests-to-date-turn-violent-as-security-forces-crack-down.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li>4 people are killed during nationwide protests in Yemen. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/41644921" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>In the southern port city of <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a> one anti-government protester is shot dead and 40 others are injured as police open fire on thousands of demonstrators; thousands of protesters later storm two council buildings setting them on fire. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/19/c_13739101.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_Revolution_of_2011" title="Egyptian Revolution of 2011">Egyptian Revolution of 2011</a>:
<ul>
<li>Some Egyptians march through the streets of Cairo apologising for the way in which <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> was deposed after 30 years in the recent revolution. "Yes to Change, No to Humiliation". <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71H0QO20110218" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ayman_al-Zawahri" title="Ayman al-Zawahri">Ayman al-Zawahri</a>, <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">Al-Qaeda</a>'s deputy leader, issues a video saying that Egypt had long "deviated from Islam" and warning that democracy "can only be non-religious." <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory?id=12953255" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News America)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yusuf_al-Qaradawi" title="Yusuf al-Qaradawi">Yusuf al-Qaradawi</a>, a leading <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islamic</a> preacher associated with the <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> <a href="/wiki/Muslim_Brotherhood#In_Egypt" title="Muslim Brotherhood">Muslim Brotherhood</a>, is to lead public prayers in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a> for the first time in thirty years. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/02/17/138093.html" rel="nofollow">(Al-Arabiya)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a> Events:
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Tunisia" title="President of Tunisia">President of Tunisia</a> <a href="/wiki/Zine_El_Abidine_Ben_Ali" title="Zine El Abidine Ben Ali">Zine El Abidine Ben Ali</a>, ousted during <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Tunisian_revolution" title="2010–2011 Tunisian revolution">the recent popular revolution</a>, is reported to have slipped into a <a href="/wiki/Coma" title="Coma">coma</a> following his stroke in <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201121814354399587.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Prince <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Talal_bin_Abdul-Aziz_Al_Saud" title="Talal bin Abdul-Aziz Al Saud">Talal bin Abdul-Aziz Al Saud</a> warns of the <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a> spreading to <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> unless <a href="/wiki/Abdullah_of_Saudi_Arabia" title="Abdullah of Saudi Arabia">King Abdullah</a> speeds up the reform process. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/world/saudi-prince-talal-warns-of-uprising-threat/story-e6frg6so-1226008023428" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Tens of thousands of people march peacefully through <a href="/wiki/Tirana" title="Tirana">Tirana</a> urging the <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Albania" title="Politics of Albania">Albanian government</a> to resign due to corruption in the <a href="/wiki/Sali_Berisha" title="Sali Berisha">Sali Berisha</a> regime. 4 people were killed in a similar demonstration nearly a month ago. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5i_q8cjVNtmKGLZ4VTJJA6BNENaUg?docId=5993057" rel="nofollow">(CP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/19/world/europe/19briefs-Albania.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/19/c_13739103.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>The corpse of <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Mark_Rybinski&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Mark Rybinski (page does not exist)">Mark Rybinski</a> is found with multiple stab wounds and a slit throat outside a private school in <a href="/wiki/Tunis" title="Tunis">Tunis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/20112191176279419.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Facebook" title="Facebook">Facebook</a> recognises <a href="/wiki/Civil_union" title="Civil union">civil unions</a> and domestic partnerships as relationship statuses in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> and <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sfgate.com/cgi-bin/blogs/techchron/detail?entry_id=83325#ixzz1EGpHQYjb" rel="nofollow">(<i>San Francisco Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The U.S. abandons its criminal investigation of <a href="/wiki/Angelo_Mozilo" title="Angelo Mozilo">Angelo Mozilo</a> former chairman of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Countrywide_Financial" title="Countrywide Financial">Countrywide Financial</a>, in connection with Countrywide's collapse in 2007-08. Mozilo settled a civil action four months ago. <a class="external text" href="http://articles.latimes.com/2011/feb/18/business/la-fi-mozilo-20110219" rel="nofollow">(L.A. Times)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> officially suspends its <a href="/wiki/Whaling_in_Japan" title="Whaling in Japan">whaling</a> program for the season due to interference by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sea_Shepherd" title="Sea Shepherd">Sea Shepherd</a> conservation organisation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nhk.or.jp/daily/english/18_23.html" rel="nofollow">(NHK)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> is announced to visit <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a> and <a href="/wiki/El_Salvador" title="El Salvador">El Salvador</a> from March 19 to 23. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/19/c_13739291.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Prime Minister of Italy</a> <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Silvio Berlusconi</a> proposes a reform of the Italian judiciary system restricting <a href="/wiki/Telephone_tapping" title="Telephone tapping">telephone taps</a>, one of the methods used by prosecutors in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ruby_Rubacuori_scandal" title="Ruby Rubacuori scandal">Ruby Rubacuori scandal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/19/c_13739105.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12508671" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> court upholds an eight year sentence for "stealing state secrets" for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chinese_American" title="Chinese American">Chinese American</a> <a href="/wiki/Geologist" title="Geologist">geologist</a> <a href="/wiki/Xue_Feng" title="Xue Feng">Xue Feng</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12502111" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-18/u-s-geologist-loses-china-appeal-on-state-secrets-charge.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkish</a> court jails three journalists associated with a <a href="/wiki/Dissident" title="Dissident">dissident</a> website pending trials on being part of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ergenekon_(organization)" title="Ergenekon (organization)">Ergenekon</a> organisation allegedly plotting to overthrow the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Turkey" title="Government of Turkey">Government of Turkey</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.mercurynews.com/news/ci_17420552?nclick_check=1" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>San Jose Mercury</i>)</a></li>
<li>A McCann family spokesman insists reports that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Madeleine_McCann" title="Madeleine McCann">Madeleine McCann</a> was taken to the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> after being snatched during a family holiday in <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a> must be treated with caution. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/UK-News/Madeleine-McCann-Family-Spokesman-Sceptical-Of-US-Abduction-Claims/Article/201102315936274?lpos=UK_News_Second_UK_News_Article_Teaser_Region_0&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15936274_Madeleine_McCann%3A_Family_Spokesman_Sceptical_Of_US_Abduction_Claims" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/New_Caledonia" title="New Caledonia">New Caledonia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Coalition_government" title="Coalition government">coalition government</a> collapses after the pro-independence <a href="/wiki/Caledonian_Union" title="Caledonian Union">Caledonian Union</a> party withdraws its support for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_New_Caledonia" title="President of New Caledonia">President</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Philippe_Gomes" title="Philippe Gomes">Philippe Gomes</a> in a dispute over the use of <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_New_Caledonia" title="Flag of New Caledonia">New Caledonian flags</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.radioaustralianews.net.au/stories/201102/3142849.htm?desktop" rel="nofollow">(Radio Australia)</a></li>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a> go to the polls for the <a href="/wiki/Ugandan_general_election,_2011" title="Ugandan general election, 2011">Ugandan general election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/breakingnews/222269/uganda-vote-set-to-extend-museveni-25-year-rule" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201121818435518664.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington_Post" title="Washington Post">Washington Post</a></i> reports that <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_of_the_United_States" title="Senate of the United States">Senator</a> <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Bingaman" title="Jeff Bingaman">Jeff Bingaman</a> of <a href="/wiki/New_Mexico" title="New Mexico">New Mexico</a> will announce that he will not contest the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate_election_in_New_Mexico,_2012" title="United States Senate election in New Mexico, 2012">2012 Senate election for New Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://voices.washingtonpost.com/thefix/senate/jeff-bingaman-to-retire.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obama_administration" title="Obama administration">Obama administration</a> rescinds most of a <a href="/wiki/Regulation" title="Regulation">regulation</a> designed to protect <a href="/wiki/Health_care" title="Health care">health care</a> workers who refuse to provide a service that they find objectionable but retains protections against performing <a href="/wiki/Abortion" title="Abortion">abortions</a> when you have strong anti-abortion convictions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/18/AR2011021803251.html?wpisrc=nl_natlalert" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> blocks <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_the_United_States" title="Government of the United States">Federal</a> funding for <a href="/wiki/Planned_Parenthood" title="Planned Parenthood">Planned Parenthood</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ajc.com/news/nation-world/house-blocks-federal-aid-844689.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Atlanta Journal Constitution)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/19/c_13739110.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">U.S. state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin" title="Wisconsin">Wisconsin</a> has demonstrations in the tens of thousands against a bill forcing public service workers to pay increased pension costs, increased healthcare coverage as well as stripping them of almost all union rights. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wisconsin_Senate" title="Wisconsin Senate">Senators</a> yesterday fled the state to <a href="/wiki/Illinois" title="Illinois">Illinois</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/US/02/18/wisconsin.budget/?hpt=T1" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/news/nationworld/nation/la-na-wisconsin-unions-20110218,0,5074043.story" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/video/2011/02/17/VI2011021705857.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> clears the <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">Space Shuttle Discovery</a> for its final flight on Thursday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.space.com/10903-space-shuttle-discovery-launch-date.html" rel="nofollow">(Space)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Soccer" title="Soccer">soccer</a> player <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a>, who retired recently, joins <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>'s <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> organising committee. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/video/2011-02/18/c_13738500.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> February 19, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-02-19</span>)</span> (Saturday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_19&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_19&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_19&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> claims that <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> security forces have killed 84 people over the past three days. <a class="external text" href="http://www.hrw.org/node/96622" rel="nofollow">(Human Rights Watch)</a></li>
<li>Libyan exiles claim that the total death toll could be as high as 120 with reports that <a href="/wiki/Sniper" title="Sniper">snipers</a> have fired at <a href="/wiki/Funeral" title="Funeral">funerals</a> in <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Libya-Gaddafi-Protest-Deaths-Exiled-Libyans-Claim-Up-To-120-Killed-In-Three-Days/Article/201102315936808?lpos=World_News_Top_Stories_Header_1&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15936808_Libya_Gaddafi_Protest_Deaths:_Exiled_Libyans_Claim_Up_To_120_Killed_In_Three_Days" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>A businessman calls for help from <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a>, saying hospitals are overwhelmed and blood is running out. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/video/africa/2011/02/201121917030797417.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">2011 Bahraini protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Demonstrators chase away riot police in <a href="/wiki/Manama" title="Manama">Manama</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,,14854725,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>At least five people are killed in demonstrations in several cities across <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12507889" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010-2011_Algerian_protests" title="2010-2011 Algerian protests">2010-2011 Algerian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Police break up a pro-<a href="/wiki/Democracy" title="Democracy">democracy</a> protest in the capital <a href="/wiki/Algiers" title="Algiers">Algiers</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011219124435427432.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/middle-east/Algerian-police-break-up-crowd-at-pro-reform-rally/articleshow/7528798.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times of India</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>At least two people are killed in the <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast" title="Ivory Coast">Ivory Coast</a> after Ivorian forces open fire on protesters urging the resignation of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_C%C3%B4te_d%27Ivoire" title="List of heads of state of Côte d'Ivoire">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Gbagbo" title="Laurent Gbagbo">Laurent Gbagbo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12516216" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Riots occur in the <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Moroccan</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Tangier" title="Tangier">Tangier</a> over utility costs. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/19/morocco-riots-idUSLDE71I08K20110219" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict">Israeli–Palestinian conflict</a>:
<ul>
<li>8 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinians</a> are injured while on restricted lands when their anti-<a href="/wiki/Israeli_West_Bank_barrier" title="Israeli West Bank barrier">barrier</a> protests are broken up by <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> forces using live ammunition and <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> among other agents to disperse the protesters. <a class="external text" href="http://www.imemc.org/article/60673" rel="nofollow">(International Middle East Media Center)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.pnn.ps/index.php?option=com_content&amp;task=view&amp;id=9581" rel="nofollow">(Palestine News Network)</a></li>
<li>Demonstrators gather outside the U.S. embassy in <a href="/wiki/Tel_Aviv" title="Tel Aviv">Tel Aviv</a> to protest yesterday's U.S. veto at the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> and call for an end to the “US-supported occupation”. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/NationalNews/Article.aspx?id=208943" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Thousands of people rally in <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spanish</a> municipality of <a href="/wiki/Bilbao" title="Bilbao">Bilbao</a> calling for the legalization of the new separatist party <a href="/wiki/Sortu" title="Sortu">Sortu</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12517087" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Pirates seize a yacht with four <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">Americans</a> off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Oman" title="Oman">Oman</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201121991647312822.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Police shoot <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Water_cannon" title="Water cannon">water cannons</a> as thousands of people protest against an authorized neo-Nazi march in <a href="/wiki/Dresden" title="Dresden">Dresden</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,,14854947,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> director <a href="/wiki/Asghar_Farhadi" title="Asghar Farhadi">Asghar Farhadi</a> wins three awards, including the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Bear" title="Golden Bear">Golden Bear</a>, for his film <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nader_and_Simin,_A_Separation" title="Nader and Simin, A Separation">Nader and Simin, A Separation</a></i> as the <a href="/wiki/61st_Berlin_International_Film_Festival" title="61st Berlin International Film Festival">61st Berlin International Film Festival</a> ends. There are other winners from <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Albania</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hungary" title="Hungary">Hungary</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,,14855532,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/International_Petroleum_Investment_Company" title="International Petroleum Investment Company">International Petroleum Investment Company</a> makes a $4billion bid for the remaining 53% of shares of <a href="/wiki/Compa%C3%B1%C3%ADa_Espa%C3%B1ola_de_Petr%C3%B3leos" title="Compañía Española de Petróleos">Compañía Española de Petróleos</a>.<a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/BT-CO-20110216-705354.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_veto_power" title="United Nations Security Council veto power">vetoes</a> a draft of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.N." title="U.N.">U.N.</a> <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">Security Council</a> resolution critical of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli_settlements" title="Israeli settlements">Israeli settlements</a> in the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/18/us-palestinians-israel-un-vote-idUSTRE71H6W720110218" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/news/diplomacy-defense/palestinian-envoy-u-s-veto-at-un-encourages-israeli-intransigence-on-settlements-1.344364" rel="nofollow">(<i>Haaretz</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.un.org/apps/news/story.asp?NewsID=37572&amp;Cr=palestin&amp;Cr1=" rel="nofollow">(UN News Centre)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a> frees Ivan Hernandez, a dissident who refused to go into exile in <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12516568" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The return of former <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascan</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Madagascar" title="List of Presidents of Madagascar">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Marc_Ravalomanana" title="Marc Ravalomanana">Marc Ravalomanana</a>, in exile in <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a>, is blocked by the government on the island. Tear gas is fired to disperse supporters at the international airport. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/commoditiesNews/idAFLDE71I03I20110219?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iX6WKigrn0NtbNR07UlJjDpSvZqg?docId=CNG.aa700ed9ede281d705dd513aec1459f1.951" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Wisconsin" title="Governor of Wisconsin">Governor of Wisconsin</a> <a href="/wiki/Scott_Walker_(politician)" title="Scott Walker (politician)">Scott Walker</a> rejects union concessions on the state budget as protests continue in <a href="/wiki/Madison,_Wisconsin" title="Madison, Wisconsin">the state capital</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jsonline.com/news/statepolitics/116519738.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Milwaukee Journal-Sentinel</i>)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of political prisoners of former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Tunisia" title="President of Tunisia">President of Tunisia</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zine_al-Abidine_Ben_Ali" title="Zine al-Abidine Ben Ali">Zine al-Abidine Ben Ali</a> are released in <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110219-thousands-political-prisoners-held-under-ben-ali-released-under-general-amnesty-tunisia" rel="nofollow">(France 24)</a></li>
<li>Authorities in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a> crack down on political activists as calls spread online for a "Jasmine Revolution" on Sunday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/19/AR2011021901021.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ahmed_Shafik" title="Ahmed Shafik">Ahmed Shafik</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Egypt" title="Prime Minister of Egypt">Prime Minister of Egypt</a>, announces that the Government will release more than 200 <a href="/wiki/Political_prisoner" title="Political prisoner">political prisoners</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.antaranews.com/en/news/1298165097/egypt-to-release-some-political-prisoners-soon" rel="nofollow">(Antara News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Iran's defense minister <a href="/wiki/Ahmad_Vahidi" title="Ahmad Vahidi">Ahmad Vahidi</a> unveils 32 scientific and research projects conducted at <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Malek_Ashtar_Industrial_University&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Malek Ashtar Industrial University (page does not exist)">Malek Ashtar Industrial University</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/166085.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_20&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_20&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_20&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li>More than 200 people are killed and 900 other are injured as military troops attack protestors in Libya.<a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12517327" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/world/story/2011/02/20/libya-protests.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/20112206386812127.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Members of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Libyan_Army_(1951-2011)" title="Libyan Army (1951-2011)">Libyan Army</a> unit defect and claim to have "liberated" <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Article/201102115937134" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>Shaikh Faraj al Zuway, the head of the <a href="/wiki/Zuwayya" title="Zuwayya">Zuwayya</a> tribe in eastern <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> threatens to cut off <a href="/wiki/Petroleum" title="Petroleum">oil</a> exports unless the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Libya" title="Government of Libya">Government of Libya</a> stops the "suppression of protestors". <a class="external text" href="http://www.lse.co.uk/FinanceNews.asp?ArticleCode=r2q88tjiooucut9&amp;ArticleHeadline=Libya_tribal_chief_threatens_to_block_oil_exports_Jazeera" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via London South East)</a><a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/2011/02/20/uk-libya-protests-idUKTRE71G0AW20110220?pageNumber=2" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> reports that the protests have spread to the capital <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/17/live-blog-libya#" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">2011 Bahraini protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Anti-regime demonstrators continue their overnight occupation of <a href="/wiki/Pearl_Roundabout" title="Pearl Roundabout">Pearl Roundabout</a> junction in <a href="/wiki/Manama" title="Manama">Manama</a>, chanting "Get out <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hamad_ibn_Isa_Al_Khalifa" title="Hamad ibn Isa Al Khalifa">Hamad</a>" in reference to the country's ruler, having reclaimed the junction after earlier being forced out by authorities. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112206279487320.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Moroccan_protests" title="2011 Moroccan protests">2011 Moroccan protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>A coalition of <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Moroccan</a> youth groups called “The February 20 Movement” calls for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Arab_world_protests" title="2010–2011 Arab world protests">peaceful protests</a> in cities throughout the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/02/19/138343.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya)</a></li>
<li>Protests spread to the city of <a href="/wiki/Rabat" title="Rabat">Rabat</a> as thousands march on the central Hassan II Avenue calling for health and educational reform, economic opportunity and assistance against increased cost of living. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201122013428971616.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Thousands of <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Moroccans</a> demonstrate in Rabat demanding that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_Mohammed_VI_of_Morocco" title="King Mohammed VI of Morocco">King Mohammed VI</a> give up some of his powers. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12518116" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.afrol.com/articles/37370" rel="nofollow">(Afrol News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Nationwide anti-regime protests continue for the 11th consecutive day as one leader is arrested in <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a> and thousands of people stage <a href="/wiki/Sit-in" title="Sit-in">sit-ins</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ibb" title="Ibb">Ibb</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ta%27izz" title="Ta'izz">Ta'izz</a> calling for the resignation of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Yemen" title="President of Yemen">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011220132734826964.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Protests in other parts of the world:
<ul>
<li>2011 Chinese protests:
<ul>
<li>Police in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> show up in force in several cities after a call for a "Jasmine Revolution", and disperse protesters in <a href="/wiki/Beijing" title="Beijing">Beijing</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sify.com/news/protesters-gather-in-beijing-shanghai-news-international-lcurOdjfcii.html" rel="nofollow">(Sify India)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12517909" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Iranian_protests" title="2011 Iranian protests">2011 Iranian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Iranians are invited to attend a protest rally in <a href="/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a> and other cities in commememoration of the two people killed while attempting to demonstrate for better freedoms last week. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/20112197512326286.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mehdi_Karroubi" title="Mehdi Karroubi">Mehdi Karroubi</a>, the opposition leader under house arrest, calls for his trial to take place in public so that people can "get to know the truth". He posts the request on his website since he cannot leave his house to personally deliver it. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201122053957526278.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> pledges to investigate itself amid reports of its recent killing of dozens of civilians in eastern Afghanistan. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-south-asia-12518798" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>War in Pakistan:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Army" title="Pakistan Army">Pakistan Army</a> kills up to 15 insurgents in operations in the <a href="/wiki/Mohmand_Agency" title="Mohmand Agency">Mohmand Agency</a> near the Afghan border. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dawn.com/2011/02/20/military-operation-kills-up-to-15-militants.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Dawn</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>War in Afghanistan:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sapper" title="Sapper">Sapper</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Australian_Defence_Force_casualties_in_Afghanistan" title="Australian Defence Force casualties in Afghanistan">Jamie Larkham</a> of the <a href="/wiki/1st_Combat_Engineer_Regiment_(Australia)" title="1st Combat Engineer Regiment (Australia)">1st Combat Engineer Regiment (Australia)</a> and an <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghan</a> interpreter die in overnight fighting. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/national-affairs/defence/another-digger-dies-in-afghanistan-as-his-patrol-comes-under-fire/story-e6frg8yo-1226008918320?from=public_rss" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fazlullah_Wahidi" title="Fazlullah Wahidi">Fazlullah Wahidi</a>, the <a href="/wiki/List_of_governors_of_Kunar" title="List of governors of Kunar">Governor of Kunar Province</a>, claims that air and missile strikes have killed 64 civilians in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ghaziabad_District,_Kunar_Province" title="Ghaziabad District, Kunar Province">Ghaziabad District</a> over the past few days. <a class="external text" href="http://www.fox4kc.com/news/nationworld/sns-rt-international-us-afgtre71j0jv-20110220,0,421910.story" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Fox 4KC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The death is announced of slain <a href="/wiki/Liberation_Tigers_of_Tamil_Eelam" title="Liberation Tigers of Tamil Eelam">LTTE</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Velupillai_Prabhakaran" title="Velupillai Prabhakaran">Velupillai Prabhakaran</a>'s mother Vallipuram Parvathi. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thehindu.com/news/international/article1474405.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hindu</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Disasters</dt>

<ul>
<li>10 children are killed by a fire during their afternoon nap at a home for disabled children in <a href="/wiki/Haapsalu" title="Haapsalu">Haapsalu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/stories/2011/02/20/501364/main20034163.shtml" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-12519860" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/20/estonia-orphanage-fire" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/breaking-news-world/estonia-orphanage-fire-kills-10-children-20110221-1b19d.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>A heavy snowfall in the <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">U.S. state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Minnesota" title="Minnesota">Minnesota</a> results in the cancellation of hundreds of flights from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Minneapolis-Saint_Paul_International_Airport" title="Minneapolis-Saint Paul International Airport">Minneapolis-Saint Paul International Airport</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/local/116562463.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Minneapolis Star-Tribune</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> reports that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Raymond_Allen_Davis_diplomatic_incident" title="Raymond Allen Davis diplomatic incident">Raymond Davis</a>, charged with murder in <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> after shooting dead two men in <a href="/wiki/Lahore" title="Lahore">Lahore</a>, worked for the U.S. <a href="/wiki/Central_Intelligence_Agency" title="Central Intelligence Agency">Central Intelligence Agency</a> (CIA). <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/20/us-raymond-davis-lahore-cia" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/asia/pakistan/8337315/US-official-held-in-Pakistan-is-CIA.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/German%E2%80%93Iranian_relations" title="German–Iranian relations">German–Iranian relations</a>:
<ul>
<li>Following a visit by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/German_Foreign_Minister" title="German Foreign Minister">German Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Guido_Westerwelle" title="Guido Westerwelle">Guido Westerwelle</a> to <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>, two <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Hellwig" title="Marcus Hellwig">German journalists</a> charged with espionage are released and return to <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> having been imprisoned since October for interviewing the son and lawyer of <a href="/wiki/Sakineh_Mohammadi_Ashtiani" title="Sakineh Mohammadi Ashtiani">Sakineh Mohammadi Ashtiani</a>.<a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/meast/02/20/iran.german.journalists/?hpt=T2" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5hRcCzxQGyFZzCsotcTJSLCT_nnzg?docId=6013346" rel="nofollow">(Canadian Press)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4030928,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynet)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/19/iran-germany-release-confirm-idUSLDE71I0EX20110219" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>State-owned <a href="/wiki/Press_TV" title="Press TV">Press TV</a> reports that <a href="/wiki/President_of_Iran" title="President of Iran">President of Iran</a> <a href="/wiki/Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad" title="Mahmoud Ahmadinejad">Mahmoud Ahmadinejad</a> used Westerwelle's visit to say that some countries having a veto on the UN Security council is an insult to other countries and to call for reforms to the <a href="/wiki/World_government#The_current_global_governance_system" title="World government">world governance</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/166088.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> has been observed digging tunnels at a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nuclear_test" title="Nuclear test">nuclear test</a> site in <a href="/wiki/Punggye-ri" title="Punggye-ri">Punggye-ri</a> in <a href="/wiki/North_Hamgyong_Province" title="North Hamgyong Province">North Hamgyong Province</a> raising concerns about another test. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/national/2011/02/20/65/0301000000AEN20110220000500315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
<li><i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Yorker_Magazine" title="New Yorker Magazine">New Yorker Magazine</a></i> reports that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obama_administration" title="Obama administration">Obama administration</a> has entered exploratory talks with the <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.newyorker.com/talk/comment/2011/02/28/110228taco_talk_coll" rel="nofollow">(<i>New Yorker</i>)</a></li>
<li>Intruders steal secret computer files from <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> envoys staying in <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/02/20/0200000000AEN20110220001700315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Tunisia" title="Government of Tunisia">Government of Tunisia</a> asks <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extradiction" title="Extradiction">extradite</a> former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Tunisia" title="President of Tunisia">President of Tunisia</a> <a href="/wiki/Zine_El_Abidine_Ben_Ali" title="Zine El Abidine Ben Ali">Zine El Abidine Ben Ali</a> who it accuses of "several serious crimes.". <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/s/afp/20110220/wl_africa_afp/tunisiapoliticsunrestbenalisaudi" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>

<li>A coalition of anti-war groups, pacifists, religious organisations and digital activists urges people to boycott next month's UK's census due to the involvement of the U.S. arms manufacturer responsible for <a href="/wiki/Trident_(missile)" title="Trident (missile)">Trident</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/uk/2011/feb/19/census-boycott-lockheed-martin" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Observer</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Wisconsin_budget_protests" title="2011 Wisconsin budget protests">Thousands of protesters continue to demonstrate</a> in the <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">U.S. state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin" title="Wisconsin">Wisconsin</a> over reform of unions and taxes. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/americas/2011/02/20112201564409366.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.necn.com/02/20/11/Wisconsin-protests-continue-Gov-defends-/landing_nation.html?blockID=414389&amp;feedID=4207" rel="nofollow">(NECN)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_Civil_War" title="2011 Libyan Civil War">2011 Libyan Civil War</a>:
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Libyan_Air_Force_(1951-2011)" title="Libyan Air Force (1951-2011)">Libyan Air Force</a> launches airstrikes on crowds of protesters. Two civilian helicopters carrying French nationals and two Libyan Mirage jets land in <a href="/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Malta</a>. The Libyan pilots claim that they received orders to bomb protesters, and request political asylum. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4031971,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynetnews)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.npr.org/templates/story/story.php?storyId=133940091" rel="nofollow">(NPR)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/babylonbeyond/2011/02/malta-two-libyan-fighter-jets-seen-landing.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://andrewsullivan.theatlantic.com/the_daily_dish/2011/02/the-military-splits.html" rel="nofollow">(The Atlantic)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.timesofmalta.com/articles/view/20110221/local/two-libyan-fighter-jets-arrive-in-malta-two-helicopters-land" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of Malta</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saif_al-Islam_Gaddafi" title="Saif al-Islam Gaddafi">Saif al-Islam Gaddafi</a>, a son of <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a>, warns in a nationally televised address that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">protests</a> could develop into a <a href="/wiki/Civil_war" title="Civil war">civil war</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/disp/story.mpl/ap/top/all/7438564.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iQvZY4yfGOaNxG6v2yuLBnZxxVhA?docId=CNG.2fa97f53bfcdc1875eb8f281d95222b2.13a1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UAE" title="UAE">UAE</a>-based <a href="/wiki/Al_Arabiya" title="Al Arabiya">Al Arabiya</a> and <a href="/wiki/Qatar" title="Qatar">Qatar</a>-based <a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> reported earlier that Colonel <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a>, head of Libya, has left for <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> or <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english2010/world/2011-02/21/c_13741080.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/20/libya-defiant-protesters-feared-dead" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Libya's representatives to the <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a>, China, India and other countries resign in protest at the violence. <a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/news/international/libya-justice-minister-resigns-to-protest-excessive-use-of-force-against-protesters-1.344796" rel="nofollow">(<i>Haaretz</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/21/libya-pilots-flee-to-malta" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Clashes and gunfire are reported in <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a> for the first time. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201122131439291589.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yusuf_al-Qaradawi" title="Yusuf al-Qaradawi">Yusuf al-Qaradawi</a>, an influential <a href="/wiki/Muslim" title="Muslim">Muslim</a> cleric and the spiritual leader of <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Muslim_Brotherhood#In_Egypt" title="Muslim Brotherhood">Muslim Brotherhood</a>, issues a <a href="/wiki/Fatwa" title="Fatwa">fatwa</a> ordering the death of the Libyan leader <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.africasia.com/services/news_mideast/article.php?ID=CNG.aa651167cd0af745b3cb395cf1d402e3.9a1" rel="nofollow">(Africasia.com)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5i0bbRyEjMASxA90i3tTXp1Fe0Q8A?docId=CNG.aa651167cd0af745b3cb395cf1d402e3.9a1" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li>Islamic leaders and clerics in Libya urge all Muslims to rebel against Gaddafi. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/libyaNews/idAFLDE71K1TQ20110221" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> calls on <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> authorities to "stop this unacceptable bloodshed". <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/middle-east/2011/02/17/live-blog-libya#" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/21/us-libya-usa-idUSTRE71K6D520110221?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+reuters%2FtopNews+%28News+%2F+US+%2F+Top+News%29" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>MPs join protests in the capital <a href="/wiki/Sana%27a" title="Sana'a">Sana'a</a> as President <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a> refuses to step down. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5h1Ald1x-TninRUA3_LTLNU0QW2lw?docId=CNG.9ca55cf302e06a927c19c577032fb5cb.391" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>The cancellation of the <a href="/wiki/2011_Bahrain_Grand_Prix" title="2011 Bahrain Grand Prix">2011 Bahrain Grand Prix</a> is announced. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport1/hi/motorsport/formula_one/9402871.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
