<li>Situation in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>:
<ul>
<li>A car bomb attack in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a> kills 13 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.presstv.ir/detail/166284.html" rel="nofollow">(Press TV)</a></li>
<li>At least five people are killed and dozens injured in clashes between military forces from <a href="/wiki/Somaliland" title="Somaliland">Somaliland</a> and clan militias in the disputed <a href="/wiki/Sool,_Somalia" title="Sool, Somalia">Sool</a> region. <a class="external text" href="http://www.allheadlinenews.com/briefs/articles/90035735?Clashes%20re-start%20in%20northern%20Somalia%20as%20Somaliland%20troops%20attack%20local%20clan%20militias" rel="nofollow">(AHN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>An excavation begins at the Tokyo site of <a href="/wiki/Unit_731" title="Unit 731">Unit 731</a>, a covert <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Japanese_Army" title="Imperial Japanese Army">Imperial Japanese Army</a> <a href="/wiki/Biological_warfare" title="Biological warfare">biological</a> and <a href="/wiki/Chemical_warfare" title="Chemical warfare">chemical warfare</a> site that conducted <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Human_experimentation" title="Human experimentation">human experimentation</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.japantoday.com/category/national/view/japan-to-dig-site-linked-to-wwii-human-experiments" rel="nofollow">(Japan Today)</a></li>
<li>A suspected United States missile strike kills four militants in the <a href="/wiki/South_Waziristan" title="South Waziristan">South Waziristan</a> region of <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ap/article/ALeqM5j2LQ8q4x7lQfYjyWUKoeEUJWil0w?docId=e7eab271e60545f09f4de98ca88007f2" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>

The two companies will also enter into a joint venture for marketing and sourcing <a href="/wiki/Natural_gas" title="Natural gas">natural gas</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/21/us-bp-reliance-idUSTRE71K1U520110221" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ConAgra" title="ConAgra">ConAgra</a> lays off 234 workers from its <a href="/wiki/Slim_Jim_(snack_food)" title="Slim Jim (snack food)">Slim Jim</a> manufacturing plant in <a href="/wiki/Garner,_North_Carolina" title="Garner, North Carolina">Garner, North Carolina</a> prior to the closure of the plant. <a class="external text" href="http://abclocal.go.com/wtvd/story?section=news/local&amp;id=7971221" rel="nofollow">(ABC Local)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.newsobserver.com/business/conagra-laying-off-234-workers-in-garner-as-it-prepares-to-close-slim-jim-plant" rel="nofollow">(<i>News and Observer</i>)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Influenza_A_virus_subtype_H5N1" title="Influenza A virus subtype H5N1">Bird flu</a> is discovered in the Indian state of <a href="/wiki/Andhra_Pradesh" title="Andhra Pradesh">Andhra Pradesh</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/city/hyderabad/Poultry-farmers-on-bird-flu-alert/articleshow/7536271.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>

<li>Jurist <a href="/wiki/Alex_Chernov" title="Alex Chernov">Alex Chernov</a> is appointed as the next <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Victoria" title="Governor of Victoria">Governor</a> of the Australian state of <a href="/wiki/Victoria_(Australia)" title="Victoria (Australia)">Victoria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/victorian-governor-david-de-kretser-steps-down-after-five-years/story-e6frf7jo-1226009401292" rel="nofollow">(<i>Herald Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>Three <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> <a href="/wiki/Hunger_strike" title="Hunger strike">hunger strikers</a> are hospitalised after calling for an international probe into alleged <a href="/wiki/Human_rights" title="Human rights">human rights</a> abuses by the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Venezuela" title="President of Venezuela">President of Venezuela</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/world/116620873.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Star Tribune</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>:
<ul>
<li>The leader of <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a> appears on state television to disprove claims that he has fled. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/breaking-news/gaddafi-makes-brief-tv-appearance/story-e6frfku0-1226009945190" rel="nofollow">(AFP via News Limited)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12533069" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Runway" title="Runway">runways</a> at <a href="/wiki/Benina_International_Airport" title="Benina International Airport">Benina International Airport</a> in <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a> have been destroyed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news24.com/Africa/News/Libya-Benghazi-airport-runways-destroyed-20110222" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via News 24)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> holds a closed-door meeting in response to the crackdown in Libya <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/22/libya-crisis-un-security-council" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Colonel Gaddafi gives a major speech claiming that he will remain head of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/History_of_Libya_under_Gaddafi" title="History of Libya under Gaddafi">revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12544624" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abdul_Fatah_Younis" title="Abdul Fatah Younis">Abdul Fatah Younis</a>, the Libyan Interior Minister and general in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Libyan_Army_(1951-2011)" title="Libyan Army (1951-2011)">Libyan Army</a>, defects. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/africa/2011/02/22/live-blog-libya-feb-22" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Libya" title="Kingdom of Libya">old monarchy-era</a> <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Libya" title="Flag of Libya">flag</a>, which has become a popular symbol among anti-government protesters, is hoisted at the <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> embassy in <a href="/wiki/Stockholm" title="Stockholm">Stockholm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thelocal.se/32204/20110222/" rel="nofollow">(The Local)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5gpm_i4gCtyuAXtsDYQrIX8zrJKHQ?docId=6029350" rel="nofollow">(Canadian Press via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a> suspends diplomatic relations with Libya, becoming the first nation to do so since the unrest, and calls on the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> to introduce a <a href="/wiki/No-fly_zone" title="No-fly zone">no-fly zone</a> over Libyan airspace to stop <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Libyan_Air_Force_(1951-2011)" title="Libyan Air Force (1951-2011)">Libyan Air Force</a> aircraft attacking civilians <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.com.au/news/breaking-news/peru-snaps-ties-with-libya/story-fn3dxity-1226010583957" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-latin-america-12548239" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Clashes take place between pro and anti-government demonstrators across the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5hR07hGGKQKLlHY9UX1bhhrm2TCyg?docId=CNG.fe923605159ddf42b506b51390842eaa.231" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>Armed supporters of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Yemen" title="Government of Yemen">Government of Yemen</a> kill two students and wound another eleven students conducting a <a href="/wiki/Sit-in" title="Sit-in">sit-in</a> at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sanaa_University" title="Sanaa University">Sanaa University</a> demanding the resignation of the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Yemen" title="President of Yemen">President of Yemen</a> <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/1489267/Yemeni-students-shot-in-demonstration" rel="nofollow">(AFP via SBS)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010-2011_Algerian_protests" title="2010-2011 Algerian protests">2010-2011 Algerian protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>The Algerian government adopts a draft law lifting the <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">state of emergency</a> in the country, in place since 1992. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12546346" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Strikes continue in the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5jbpu-ISnw9puQq13ThCOu8WWEUrQ?docId=CNG.62d0f19e811f8964214ef942867ff5e8.781" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Iranian_protests" title="2011 Iranian protests">2011 Iranian protests</a>: <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> security forces arrest the son of opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Mehdi_Karroubi" title="Mehdi Karroubi">Mehdi Karroubi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/1489282/Iranian-opposition-leader's-son-arrested" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via SBS News Australia)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Business</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Moody%27s_Investors_Service" title="Moody's Investors Service">Moody's Investors Service</a> downgrades <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Credit_rating" title="Credit rating">credit rating</a> due to concerns over high levels of <a href="/wiki/Government_debt" title="Government debt">government debt</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-22/japan-s-aa2-government-debt-rating-outlook-changed-to-negative-by-moody-s.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Life_insurance" title="Life insurance">life insurance</a> company <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Metlife" title="Metlife">Metlife</a> expects to sell its <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> unit soon, perhaps as early as April, according to anonymous sources cited by <a href="/wiki/Reuters" title="Reuters">Reuters</a>. Regulators blocked an early effort by MetLife to sell the same unit. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/22/us-metlife-taiwan-idUSTRE71L10B20110222" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Uncertainty in <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> leads to falls in world <a href="/wiki/Stock_market" title="Stock market">stock markets</a> and increases in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Crude_oil" title="Crude oil">crude oil</a> prices. <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052748703529004576159902709491200.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Canterbury_earthquake" title="2011 Canterbury earthquake">2011 Canterbury earthquake</a>:
<ul>
<li>An <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Canterbury_earthquake" title="2011 Canterbury earthquake">earthquake</a> of 6.3 magnitude strikes the region of <a href="/wiki/Canterbury,_New_Zealand" title="Canterbury, New Zealand">Canterbury</a> in the <a href="/wiki/South_Island" title="South Island">South Island</a> of <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, disrupting communications to the area and closing <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Christchurch_Airport" title="Christchurch Airport">Christchurch Airport</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=10707996" rel="nofollow">(<i>New Zealand Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.geonet.org.nz/earthquake/quakes/3468575g.html" rel="nofollow">(Geo Net)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=10707997" rel="nofollow">(<i>New Zealand Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>65 people are confirmed dead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/national/4688231/65-dead-in-devastating-Christchurch-quake" rel="nofollow">(Stuff)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://tvnz.co.nz/national-news/chch-quake-65-confirmed-dead-4038278" rel="nofollow">(TVNZ)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Radio_New_Zealand" title="Radio New Zealand">Radio New Zealand</a> reports that buildings have collapsed with 200 people trapped in one building alone. <a class="external text" href="http://www.radionz.co.nz/news/top/69180/huge-earthquake-hits-christchurch-city-centre" rel="nofollow">(Radio New Zealand)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Article/201102115938201" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.3news.co.nz/Christchurch-quake-200-trapped-in-Pyne-building/tabid/423/articleID/199310/Default.aspx" rel="nofollow">(TV3)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Christchurch_Cathedral" title="Christchurch Cathedral">Christchurch Cathedral</a> is badly damaged in the quake, losing its spire. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/asiapcf/02/21/new.zealand.earthquake/index.html?eref=edition&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter#" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.watoday.com.au/world/huge-quake-hits-christchurch-20110222-1b356.html" rel="nofollow">(WA Today)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_Fire_Service" title="New Zealand Fire Service">New Zealand Fire Service</a> confirms that there have been at least 65 deaths resulting from the earthquake with the city of <a href="/wiki/Christchurch" title="Christchurch">Christchurch</a> not having enough <a href="/wiki/Emergency_medical_services_in_New_Zealand" title="Emergency medical services in New Zealand">ambulances</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.radionz.co.nz/news/canterbury-earthquake/69180/deaths-confirmed-as-huge-quake-hits-christchurch" rel="nofollow">(Radio New Zealand)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.3news.co.nz/Live-updates-Deaths-confirmed-in-Christchurch-quake/tabid/423/articleID/199310/Default.aspx" rel="nofollow">(3 News New Zealand)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://tvnz.co.nz/national-news/live-updates-christchurch-quake-4038261" rel="nofollow">(TV New Zealand)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_New_Zealand" title="Prime Minister of New Zealand">Prime Minister of New Zealand</a> calls an emergency Cabinet meeting while <a href="/wiki/Bob_Parker_(mayor)" title="Bob Parker (mayor)">Bob Parker</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Mayor_of_Christchurch" title="Mayor of Christchurch">Mayor of Christchurch</a>, declares a <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">state of emergency</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.radionz.co.nz/news/canterbury-earthquake/69180/deaths-confirmed-as-huge-quake-hits-christchurch" rel="nofollow">(Radio New Zealand)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=10707997" rel="nofollow">(<i>New Zealand Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010-11_Australian_region_cyclone_season" title="2010-11 Australian region cyclone season">Tropical Cyclone Carlos</a> wreaks damage in the <a href="/wiki/Pilbara" title="Pilbara">Pilbara</a> region of <a href="/wiki/Western_Australia" title="Western Australia">Western Australia</a>, with reports of four tornadoes striking the mining town of <a href="/wiki/Karratha,_Western_Australia" title="Karratha, Western Australia">Karratha</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.watoday.com.au/environment/weather/minitornado-lashes-karratha-as-cyclone-carlos-menaces-wa-20110220-1b0qg.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>WAToday</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iran_Navy" title="Iran Navy">Iran Navy</a> sends two ships through the <a href="/wiki/Suez_Canal" title="Suez Canal">Suez Canal</a> for the first time since the 1979 <a href="/wiki/Iranian_Revolution" title="Iranian Revolution">Iranian Revolution</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/21/egypt-iran-suez-idUSLDE71K2F420110221" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB10001424052748703373404576148414160885824.html" rel="nofollow">(WSJ)</a></li>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Jazeera" title="Al-Jazeera">Al-Jazeera</a> reports <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a> Secretary General Amr Moussa stating that <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> is suspended from sessions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4032530,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynet)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-21/arab-league-to-discuss-libya-turmoil-tomorrow-jazeera-says.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/africa/2011/02/22/live-blog-libya-feb-22" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>

<li>An <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> court convicts 31 people on murder and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Conspiracy_(crime)" title="Conspiracy (crime)">conspiracy</a> charges in relation to the <a href="/wiki/Godhra_train_burning" title="Godhra train burning">Godhra train burning</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.globalnational.com/world/Indian+court+convicts+murder+conspiracy+train+fire/4327565/story.html" rel="nofollow">(Los Angeles Times via <i>Global National</i>)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Mark_Funkhouser" title="Mark Funkhouser">Mark Funkhouser</a> is defeated in a bid to be reelected as the mayor of <a href="/wiki/Kansas_City,_Missouri" title="Kansas City, Missouri">Kansas City</a> with Mike Burke and Sly James contesting a runoff on March 22. <a class="external text" href="http://www.fox4kc.com/news/wdaf-funkhouser-trailing-in-reelection-run-20110222,0,1899536.story" rel="nofollow">(Fox Kansas City)</a></li>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>

<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>'s foreign minister says as many as 1,000 people have been killed in <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> during the unrest. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71M00N20110223?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Anti-government protestors and defectors take control of more cities. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/2011223125256699145.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> condemns the "excessive use of force" against protesters. <a class="external text" href="http://www.apanews.net/apa.php?page=show_article_eng&amp;id_article=141288" rel="nofollow">(African Press Agency)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5j0xcyeoFf5QlwojljcxaaxQ1z4uQ?docId=CNG.867dcb3d94702f9df32e0fdbe6185a98.2a1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bruno_Rodr%C3%ADguez_Parrilla" title="Bruno Rodríguez Parrilla">Bruno Rodríguez Parrilla</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Cuba)" title="Minister of Foreign Affairs (Cuba)">Minister of Foreign Affairs</a>, accuses the US media of inciting violence. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/41741662" rel="nofollow">(AP via MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>More than 5,700 people have fled Libya for <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a> in the past couple of days. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/africa/2011/02/22/live-blog-libya-feb-23" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mustafa_Abdul_Jalil" title="Mustafa Abdul Jalil">Mustafa Abdul Jalil</a>, the former <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> Minister for Justice, claims that <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> dictator <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a> personally authorised the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lockerbie_bombing" title="Lockerbie bombing">Lockerbie bombing</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/23/AR2011022302133.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Washington Post)</a></li>
<li>Nations including the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" title="United States of America">United States of America</a>, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a> evacuate their citizens from Libya. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Libya-The-UK-And-Other-Nations-Are-Evacuating-Foreigners-Trapped-Amid-Ongoing-Civil-Unrest/Article/201102415939265?lpos=World_News_Carousel_Region_0&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15939265_Libya:_The_UK_And_Other_Nations_Are_Evacuating_Foreigners_Trapped_Amid_Ongoing_Civil_Unrest" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Eight members of the ruling <a href="/wiki/General_People%27s_Congress_(Yemen)" title="General People's Congress (Yemen)">General People's Congress</a> party resign after the deaths of protestors. <a class="external text" href="http://www.english.rfi.fr/middle-east/20110223-yemini-protesters-defiant-after-deaths-mps-resign" rel="nofollow">(RFI)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>A missing <a href="/wiki/Enid_Blyton" title="Enid Blyton">Enid Blyton</a> manuscript is found in an archive of her work. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/books/2011/feb/23/enid-blyton-manuscript-found" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Samsung" title="Samsung">Samsung</a> releases, in <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>, a camera that can post photos and videos directly to <a href="/wiki/Facebook" title="Facebook">Facebook</a> and <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/newproduct/2011/02/23/64/5000000000AEN20110223002800320F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> businessman <a href="/wiki/Lachlan_Murdoch" title="Lachlan Murdoch">Lachlan Murdoch</a> is appointed as acting CEO of <a href="/wiki/Network_Ten" title="Network Ten">Network Ten</a> following the sacking of Grant Blackley. <a class="external text" href="http://news.ninemsn.com.au/article.aspx?id=8215388" rel="nofollow">(NineMSN)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oil_prices" title="Oil prices">Oil prices</a> reach a two-year high due to uncertainty in the <a href="/wiki/Middle_East" title="Middle East">Middle East</a> most notably in <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/business/breaking-news/oil-hits-two-year-high-as-libya-teeters-on-edge/story-e6frfkur-1226010834420" rel="nofollow">(AP via News Limited)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> logs its first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trade_deficit" title="Trade deficit">trade deficit</a> in almost two years due to high commodity prices and weak demand for its exports. <a class="external text" href="http://news.brisbanetimes.com.au/breaking-news-world/japan-logs-first-trade-deficit-in-almost-two-years-20110223-1b5b4.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Brisbane Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Stock_market" title="Stock market">Stock markets</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> fall due to uncertainty in the <a href="/wiki/Middle_East" title="Middle East">Middle East</a> and rising oil prices. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-23/euro-won-gain-on-outlook-for-rates-as-oil-rises-asian-stocks-fluctuate.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Canterbury_earthquake" title="2011 Canterbury earthquake">2011 Canterbury earthquake</a>:
<ul>
<li>300 persons are estimated to be still missing in <a href="/wiki/Christchurch" title="Christchurch">Christchurch</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, following yesterday's earthquake with the official death toll reaching 75. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/earthquakes/news/article.cfm?c_id=184&amp;objectid=10708163" rel="nofollow">(<i>NZ Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.couriermail.com.au/news/national/frantic-effort-to-free-christchurch-earthquake-survivors-as-death-toll-mounts/story-e6freooo-1226010364314" rel="nofollow">(<i>Courier Mail</i>)</a></li>
<li>The earthquake shakes off 30 million tonnes of ice loose from the <a href="/wiki/Tasman_Glacier" title="Tasman Glacier">Tasman Glacier</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Aoraki/Mount_Cook_National_Park" title="Aoraki/Mount Cook National Park">Aoraki/Mount Cook National Park</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=10708071" rel="nofollow">(<i>NZ Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>Rescue crews pull out of central Christchurch due to fears that one of the tallest buildings, the Grand Chancellor Hotel, will collapse. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2011/02/23/3146607.htm?section=justin" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_New_Zealand" title="Prime Minister of New Zealand">Prime Minister of New Zealand</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Key" title="John Key">John Key</a> declares a national emergency. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/1489207/Rescuers-focus-on-survivors-of-NZ-quake" rel="nofollow">(SBS)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_New_Zealand" title="Law enforcement in New Zealand">New Zealand police</a> introduce a <a href="/wiki/Curfew" title="Curfew">curfew</a> in central <a href="/wiki/Christchurch" title="Christchurch">Christchurch</a> as six people are arrested for looting. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/world/looters-arrested-as-police-order-christchurch-curfew-20110223-1b588.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Snow and heavy winds affecting areas around <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Constan%C5%A3a" title="Constanţa">Constanţa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>, are predicted to continue until late Friday evening. <a class="external text" href="http://english.hotnews.ro/stiri-top_news-8331003-snow-and-heavy-winds-affect-romania-until-friday-evening.htm" rel="nofollow">(EnglishHotNews)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Philippines" title="President of the Philippines">President of the Philippines</a> <a href="/wiki/Benigno_Aquino_III" title="Benigno Aquino III">Benigno Aquino</a> says the country has not resolved a row with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" title="Republic of China">Taiwan</a> over deportations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5gLjpnaNEQ6hvbogSSoqTtKxSge7A?docId=CNG.a9752ab9a9ad29f39dac145a6ef0e9bf.4e1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Senegal" title="Senegal">Senegal</a> severs <a href="/wiki/Iran%E2%80%93Senegal_relations" title="Iran–Senegal relations">diplomatic relations</a> with <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>, accusing it of supplying weapons to anti-government rebels that killed Senegalese soldiers. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/senegalNews/idAFLDE71M00620110223" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.cri.cn/6966/2011/02/23/1461s622240.htm" rel="nofollow">(China Radio International)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a> refuses to let the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> publish a report on <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a>'s efforts to avoid <a href="/wiki/International_sanctions" title="International sanctions">sanctions</a> on its <a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">nuclear program</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5hU8Sh-tH6n2ZmbyXJbaOonW1WPjg?docId=CNG.867dcb3d94702f9df32e0fdbe6185a98.3f1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>

<li>Three people are arrested in the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> in connection with an alleged attempt to <a href="/wiki/Blackmail" title="Blackmail">blackmail</a> <a href="/wiki/Coleen_Rooney" title="Coleen Rooney">Coleen Rooney</a>, the wife of <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United F.C.</a> star <a href="/wiki/Wayne_Rooney" title="Wayne Rooney">Wayne Rooney</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/1489452/Arrests-for-alleged-plot-to-blackmail-Rooney%27s-wife" rel="nofollow">(BBC via SBS)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Colin_Hatch" title="Colin Hatch">Colin Hatch</a>, a convicted child murderer, is murdered in jail while serving his sentence; a 35-year-old male prisoner has been arrested on suspicion of murder. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/UK-News/Colin-Hatch-Inmate-Arrested-Over-Murder-Of-A-Child-Killer-At-Full-Sutton-Prison-Near-York/Article/201102415939213?lpos=UK_News_First_Home_Article_Teaser_Region_4&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15939213_Colin_Hatch%3A_Inmate_Arrested_Over_Murder_Of_A_Child_Killer_At_Full_Sutton_Prison_Near_York" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>

<li>More towns and cities closer to Tripoli come under the control of protesters and defectors. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/02/24/138986.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya)</a></li>
<li>At least ten people have been killed and dozens injured following an attack by pro-Government forces on the town of <a href="/wiki/Zawiya,_Libya" title="Zawiya, Libya">Zawiya</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/breaking-news/pro-government-forces-kill-10-in-libya/story-e6frf7jx-1226011718493" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Herald-Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>Colonel Gaddafi describes himself as a "symbolic leader" similar to <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Queen Elizabeth II</a> and blames unrest on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al_Qaeda" title="Al Qaeda">al Qaeda</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/ondeadline/post/2011/02/fighting-breaks-out-30-miles-west-of-libyan-capital/1" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>

Caldwell</a> ordered a campaign of "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Psychological_operations" title="Psychological operations">psychological operations</a>" to persuade influential people to continue support for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">War in Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rollingstone.com/politics/news/another-runaway-general-army-deploys-psy-ops-on-u-s-senators-20110223" rel="nofollow">(<i>Rolling Stone</i>)</a></li>

<li>A "one-<a href="/wiki/Dog" title="Dog">dog</a> policy" is announced in <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>, with more than 600,000 unlicensed dogs to be declared illegal.<a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12563432" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.peopledaily.com.cn/90001/90776/90882/7298261.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>People's Daily</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabian</a> student is arrested in <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a> for allegedly planning a terrorist attack against the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dallas,_Texas" title="Dallas, Texas">Dallas</a> home of former <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> as a target as well as <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a> and dams in <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> and <a href="/wiki/Colorado" title="Colorado">Colorado</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.kiiitv.com/Global/story.asp?S=14134222&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(AP via KIII-TV)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/21134540/vp/41758905#41758905" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnewyork.com/news/local-beat/Suspected-Terrorist-had-116832343.html" rel="nofollow">(NBC)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> judge orders <a href="/wiki/Julian_Assange" title="Julian Assange">Julian Assange</a> to be <a href="/wiki/Extradition" title="Extradition">extradited</a> to <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a> but the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wikileaks" title="Wikileaks">Wikileaks</a> founder says that he will appeal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/breaking-news/assange-to-appeal-extradition-order/story-e6frfku0-1226011720300" rel="nofollow">(AAP via News Limited)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">German</a> prosecutors investigate several companies for possible illegal sales of <a href="/wiki/HIV" title="HIV">HIV</a> drugs including those intended for use in <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ktuu.com/sns-bc-eu--germany-hivdrugfraud,0,5822480.story" rel="nofollow">(AP via KTUU)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_the_United_States" title="Law enforcement in the United States">United States authorities</a> arrest more than 60 suspected members of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mexican_drug_cartel" title="Mexican drug cartel">Mexican drug cartels</a> following the execution of a US <a href="/wiki/Drug_Enforcement_Administration" title="Drug Enforcement Administration">Drug Enforcement Administration</a> agent in <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> last week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/us/2011/02/24/60-arrested-nationwide-mexican-drug-gang-sweep/#" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>

<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a>'s opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Kizza_Besigye" title="Kizza Besigye">Kizza Besigye</a> calls for protests against the <a href="/wiki/Ugandan_general_election,_2011" title="Ugandan general election, 2011">disputed presidential election</a> which saw incumbent President <a href="/wiki/Yoweri_Museveni" title="Yoweri Museveni">Yoweri Museveni</a> win a fourth term in office. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71N0BZ20110224" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Shimon_Peres" title="Shimon Peres">Shimon Peres</a>, the President of <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>, is on a four day state visit to <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a> as King <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Juan_Carlos" title="Juan Carlos">Juan Carlos</a> expressed his support for the Middle East peace process. <a class="external text" href="http://www.zimbio.com/King+Juan+Carlos+I/articles/K2LnG09lKF1/Israeli+President+State+Visit+Spain" rel="nofollow">(Zimbio)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Australia" title="Prime Minister of Australia">Prime Minister of Australia</a> <a href="/wiki/Julia_Gillard" title="Julia Gillard">Julia Gillard</a> announces a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Carbon_pricing" title="Carbon pricing">carbon pricing</a> scheme to start on July 1, 2012. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/breaking-news/carbon-price-to-start-july-2012-gillard/story-e6frfku0-1226011297457" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2011/02/24/3147523.htm?section=justin" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/School_Board" title="School Board">School Board</a> in the US city of <a href="/wiki/Providence,_Rhode_Island" title="Providence, Rhode Island">Providence, Rhode Island</a>, votes to send dismissal notices to all of the 1,926 teachers in the <a href="/wiki/Providence_Public_School_District" title="Providence Public School District">Providence Public School District</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://newsblog.projo.com/2011/02/container-for-vote-on-teachers.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Providence Journal</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">Space Shuttle Discovery</a> takes off for its <a href="/wiki/STS-133" title="STS-133">final mission</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/scitech/2011/02/24/space-shuttle-discovery-final-flight/#" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Crusaders_(rugby)" title="Crusaders (rugby)">Canterbury Crusaders</a> cancel a planned <a href="/wiki/2011_Super_Rugby_season" title="2011 Super Rugby season">match</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Wellington" title="Wellington">Wellington</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricanes_(Super_rugby_franchise)" title="Hurricanes (Super rugby franchise)">Hurricanes</a> due to the earthquake with doubts over <a href="/wiki/Christchurch" title="Christchurch">Christchurch</a>'s capacity to host <a href="/wiki/2011_Rugby_World_Cup" title="2011 Rugby World Cup">2011 Rugby World Cup</a> games. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/rugby-union/union-news/rugby-takes-a-back-seat-as-crusaders-can-hurricanes-clash-20110223-1b5lq.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>Police clash with angry cricket fans in <a href="/wiki/Bangalore" title="Bangalore">Bangalore</a> after a <a href="/wiki/2011_Cricket_World_Cup" title="2011 Cricket World Cup">2011 Cricket World Cup</a> fixture between <a href="/wiki/India_national_cricket_team" title="India national cricket team">India</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/England_national_cricket_team" title="England national cricket team">England</a> is sold out. <a class="external text" href="http://www.newsindia-times.com/NewsIndiaTimes/20110224/5435243202359531905.htm?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(<i>News India Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> February 25, 2011<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2011-02-25</span>)</span> (Friday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2011_February_25&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Iraqi_protests" title="2011 Iraqi protests">2011 Iraqi protests</a>
<ul>
<li>At least twenty-nine are killed in a "Day of Rage" protesting against economic problems and corruption in the country. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011224192028229471.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5ia4CeZt15R4Uc6tl1lH0nL1e-rNQ?docId=6063765" rel="nofollow">(CP via Google News)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/26/AR2011022601854.html" rel="nofollow">(Washington Post)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">2011 Bahraini protests</a>
<ul>
<li>Thousands of people stage an anti-government protest in the capital <a href="/wiki/Manama" title="Manama">Manama</a>, on a day of mourning declared by the government following the deaths of protesters. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/25/us-bahrain-protests-idUSTRE71O4VS20110225" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>
<ul>
<li>Leader <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a> addresses a crowd of supporters in the capital <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/2011225165641323716.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/02/25/139234.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/ondeadline/post/2011/02/gadhafi-makes-surprise-appearance-in-tripolis-green-square/1" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a></li>
<li>More defections take place with a <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> envoy to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> changing sides during a meeting at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.N._Human_Rights_Council" title="U.N. Human Rights Council">U.N. Human Rights Council</a> in <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/02/25/139145.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/41779850" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/breaking-news/libyas-un-ambassador-mohammed-shalgham-defects/story-e6frf7jx-1226012395580" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Melbourne Herald-Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> announces sanctions against the government of Libya as does the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/washington/2011/02/gaddafi-obama-libya-sanctions.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://news.tradingcharts.com/futures/0/2/154015820.html" rel="nofollow">(Dow Jones via Trading Charts)</a>
<ul>
<li>Tens of thousands of people participate in anti-government protests in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>, leaving one dead and several people injured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bangkokpost.com/news/world/223538/tens-of-thousands-rally-across-yemen" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bangkok Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.sify.com/news/nine-injured-as-protests-continue-in-yemen-news-international-lczvkpbjbcj.html" rel="nofollow">(Sify India)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Egyptian_protests" title="2011 Egyptian protests">2011 Egyptian protests</a>: <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> protestors claims that the <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Army" title="Egyptian Army">Egyptian Army</a> beat them up in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Tahrir_Square" title="Tahrir Square">Tahrir Square</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://thelede.blogs.nytimes.com/2011/02/25/latest-updates-on-libyas-revolt-and-mideast-protests/" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Rebels in the <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast" title="Ivory Coast">Ivory Coast</a> seize another town from the control of incumbent President <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Gbagbo" title="Laurent Gbagbo">Laurent Gbagbo</a>, who refused to step down following a <a href="/wiki/Ivorian_presidential_election,_2010" title="Ivorian presidential election, 2010">disputed presidential election</a>. Unrest occurs in the capital <a href="/wiki/Yamoussoukro" title="Yamoussoukro">Yamoussoukro</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12582014" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Victorian_era" title="Victorian era">Victorian era</a> photographs and <a href="/wiki/Parole" title="Parole">parole</a> details for women prisoners in the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> are published on <a href="/wiki/Ancestry.com" title="Ancestry.com">Ancestry.com</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/society/2011/feb/25/victorian-female-prisoners-records-genealogy" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The video game <i><a href="/wiki/Mortal_Kombat_(2011_video_game)" title="Mortal Kombat (2011 video game)">Mortal Kombat</a></i> is refused classification in <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.kotaku.com.au/2011/02/mortal-kombat-banned-in-australia/" rel="nofollow">(Kotaku)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Christian_Dior" title="Christian Dior">Christian Dior</a> suspends <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fashion_designer" title="Fashion designer">fashion designer</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Galliano" title="John Galliano">John Galliano</a> following his arrest in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> for allegedly making an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anti-Semitism" title="Anti-Semitism">anti-Semetic</a> rant towards a couple in a cafe as well as an assault. <a class="external text" href="http://fashion.telegraph.co.uk/news-features/TMG8347082/John-Galliano-suspended-by-Dior-following-arrest-over-anti-semitic-rant.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Telegraph</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.elleuk.com/news/fashion-news/a-galliano-update-he-s-been-suspended/(gid)/751533" rel="nofollow">(Elle)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.vogue.co.uk/news/daily/110225-john-galliano-arrested-in-paris-for.aspx" rel="nofollow">(Vogue)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Population_of_Japan" title="Population of Japan">population of Japan</a> records its <a href="/wiki/Population_decline" title="Population decline">slowest increase</a> since <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> first held a <a href="/wiki/Census" title="Census">census</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thejakartapost.com/news/2011/02/25/japan-sees-slowest-population-growth-1920.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Jakarta Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Seoul" title="Seoul">Seoul</a> court orders <a href="/wiki/Chung_Mong-koo" title="Chung Mong-koo">Chung Mong-koo</a>, the Chairman of the <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korean</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hyundai_Kia_Automotive_Group" title="Hyundai Kia Automotive Group">Hyundai Kia Automotive Group</a>, to pay US$73.1 million in compensation to his own company. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2011/02/25/0200000000AEN20110225004000315.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Canterbury_earthquake" title="2011 Canterbury earthquake">2011 Canterbury earthquake</a>
<ul>
<li>The death toll from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Canterbury_earthquake" title="2011 Canterbury earthquake">2011 Canterbury earthquake</a> in <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a> rises to 113 with at least 226 people missing. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/asiapcf/02/24/new.zealand.earthquake/index.html?hpt=C1#" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://tvnz.co.nz/national-news/rain-making-rescue-efforts-more-hazardous-4040248" rel="nofollow">(TV New Zealand)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Zealand_Census_of_Population_and_Dwellings" title="New Zealand Census of Population and Dwellings">New Zealand Census of Population and Dwellings</a>, scheduled for 8 March, has been canceled due to the earthquake.<a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=10708710" rel="nofollow">(<i>New Zealand Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A heavy <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Snowstorm" title="Snowstorm">snowstorm</a> hits the <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">East Coast of the United States</a> causing flight cancellations and school closures. <a class="external text" href="http://www.oregonlive.com/weather/index.ssf/2011/02/winter_storm_wallops_east_coas.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Oregon Live)</a></li>
<li>At least twenty-two people die in <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a> after a bus plunges into a <a href="/wiki/Ravine" title="Ravine">ravine</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/41788734/ns/world_news-americas/" rel="nofollow">(AP via MSNBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Iran" title="Government of Iran">Government of Iran</a> advises the <a href="/wiki/International_Atomic_Energy_Agency" title="International Atomic Energy Agency">International Atomic Energy Agency</a> of serious problems with its <a href="/wiki/Bushehr_Nuclear_Power_Plant" title="Bushehr Nuclear Power Plant">Bushehr Nuclear Power Plant</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/02/26/world/middleeast/26nuke.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a> jails five more dissidents on charges including associating with dissident groups abroad. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/SEAsia/Story/STIStory_638807.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/House_of_Representatives_of_the_Philippines" title="House of Representatives of the Philippines">Representative</a> <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Singson" title="Ronald Singson">Ronald Singson</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> is sentenced to 18 months in a <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> jail for <a href="/wiki/Cocaine" title="Cocaine">cocaine</a> possession. <a class="external text" href="http://ph.news.yahoo.com/ap/20110223/tap-as-hong-kong-philippines-legislator-fe2a5de.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Yahoo News Philippines)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a> gets rid of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_penalty" title="Death penalty">death penalty</a> for 13 non-violent economic crimes. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.voanews.com/breaking-news/2011/02/25/china-scraps-death-penalty-for-13-crimes/" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_States_district_court" title="United States district court">United States district court</a> approves a $624 million payout to former investors in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Countrywide_Financial" title="Countrywide Financial">Countrywide Financial</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/AP8b3ee7b1c005439d9b0b22bdadb76f5d.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a> announces that elections are planned for mid-July 2011, as thousands protest demanding the resignation of Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Ghannouchi" title="Mohamed Ghannouchi">Mohamed Ghannouchi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/2011225181731209442.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>Several people are charged after calling for <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Middle-East style protests</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iEnDihe4M1iR6C_tHDyUKrg7wMPg?docId=CNG.99868b1ecc4e65dad00cb9c958f4949c.391" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_China" title="Communist Party of China">Communist Party of China</a> official <a href="/wiki/Jia_Qinglin" title="Jia Qinglin">Jia Qinglin</a> urges a "renewed struggle" against the <a href="/wiki/14th_Dalai_Lama" title="14th Dalai Lama">Dalai Lama</a> and controls over <a href="/wiki/Tibetan_Buddhism" title="Tibetan Buddhism">Tibetan Buddhism</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_638778.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Straits Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-asia-pacific-12575470" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.indianexpress.com/news/china-urges-renewed-struggle-against-dalai-lama/754706/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Indian Express</i>)</a></li>
<li>Voters in the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Republic of Ireland</a> go to the polls for the <a href="/wiki/Irish_general_election,_2011" title="Irish general election, 2011">Irish general election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-northern-ireland-12574516" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>
<ul>
<li>Internal and international pressure continues on leader <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a> to stand down from power. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201122641559301766.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saif_al-Islam_Gaddafi" title="Saif al-Islam Gaddafi">Saif al-Islam Gaddafi</a> tells <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Arabiya" title="Al-Arabiya">Al-Arabiya</a> television that the unrest in <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> opens up all options including <a href="/wiki/Civil_war" title="Civil war">civil war</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/blog/2011/feb/26/libya-protests-middle-east-gaddafi" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Reuters" title="Reuters">Reuters</a> reports that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Libyan_Interim_Government" title="Libyan Interim Government">Libyan Interim Government</a> led by the former justice minister <a href="/wiki/Mustafa_Abdul_Jalil" title="Mustafa Abdul Jalil">Mustafa Abdul Jalil</a> has been formed in <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.aljazeera.net/live/africa/live-blog-libya-feb-26" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Oil_refinery" title="Oil refinery">oil refinery</a> in <a href="/wiki/Baiji,_Iraq" title="Baiji, Iraq">Baiji</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>, is bombed, resulting in its closure. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/26/iraq-oil-refinery-idUSLDE71P00L20110226?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=hotStocksNews&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_campaign=DTN+Stock+Market:&amp;utm_content=Google+Feedfetcher" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>2011 Croatian protests:
<ul>
<li>Tens of thousands of protesters meet in the <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatian</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Zagreb" title="Zagreb">Zagreb</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Ban_Jela%C4%8Di%C4%87_Square" title="Ban Jelačić Square">Ban Jelačić Square</a> to express their support for indicted <a href="/wiki/Croatian_War_of_Independence" title="Croatian War of Independence">Croatian War of Independence</a> veterans and ask <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Croatia" title="Prime Minister of Croatia">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Jadranka_Kosor" title="Jadranka Kosor">Jadranka Kosor</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Croatia" title="Government of Croatia">government</a> to resign. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jutarnji.hr/braniteljski-prosvjed--vise-stotina-ljudi-sa-slikama-gotovine-i-transparentima-okupiralo-trg/928060/" rel="nofollow">(Jutarnji list)</a></li>
<li>Several dozen of people are injured and arrested as anti-government protests degenerated into clashes with police. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jutarnji.hr/braniteljski-prosvjed--vise-stotina-ljudi-sa-slikama-gotovine-i-transparentima-okupiralo-trg/928060/" rel="nofollow">(Jutarnji list)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20110226-clashes-erupt-croatian-anti-government-protests" rel="nofollow">(France24)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Canterbury_earthquake" title="2011 Canterbury earthquake">2011 Canterbury earthquake</a>
<ul>
<li>The death toll from the earthquake in <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a> rises to 144 and there is great concern about 200 more people missing. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/2011/02/26/uk-newzealand-quake-idUKTRE71L04920110226" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://tvnz.co.nz/national-news/live-updates-christchurch-earthquake-day-five-4040854" rel="nofollow">(TV New Zealand)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_New_Zealand" title="Prime Minister of New Zealand">Prime Minister of New Zealand</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Key" title="John Key">John Key</a> calls for two minutes of silence on Tuesday March 1 at 12:51 pm, exactly one week after the earthquake. <a class="external text" href="http://tvnz.co.nz/national-news/live-updates-christchurch-earthquake-day-five-4040854" rel="nofollow">(TV New Zealand)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Aftershock" title="Aftershock">Aftershocks</a> force the evacuation of residents in <a href="/wiki/Mount_Pleasant,_New_Zealand" title="Mount Pleasant, New Zealand">Mount Pleasant</a>, an outer suburb of <a href="/wiki/Christchurch" title="Christchurch">Christchurch</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://tvnz.co.nz/national-news/aftershocks-trigger-more-evacuations-4041351?ref=rss" rel="nofollow">(TV New Zealand)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a>, after the defected Libyan Ambassador to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UN" title="UN">UN</a> <a href="/wiki/Abdel_Rahman_Shalgham" title="Abdel Rahman Shalgham">Abdel Rahman Mohamed Shalgam's</a> appeal to act against <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a>'s regime escalating violence, being used to crackdown the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>, and following propositions by <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, adopts <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_1970" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 1970">resolution 1970</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.un.org/News/Press/docs/2011/sc10187.doc.htm" rel="nofollow">(UN press release on UNSC resolution 1970)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12587078" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12589434" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.unmultimedia.org/tv/webcast/" rel="nofollow">(UN Multimedia)</a>. "All necessary means" enforcement of said resolution, and imposition of a "No-fly zone" over Libya are rejected. These measures will be however included on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNSCR_1973" title="UNSCR 1973">UNSC resolution 1973</a> of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/March_2011#2011_March_17" title="March 2011">17 March 2011</a>.</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Iraqi_protests" title="2011 Iraqi protests">2011 Iraqi protests</a>
<ul>
<li>Hundreds of Iraqi <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Journalists" title="Journalists">journalists</a>, artists, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Intellectuals" title="Intellectuals">intellectuals</a> are <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arrested" title="Arrested">arrested</a> the day following the country's "Day of Rage" protest, which resulted in at least twenty-nine deaths throughout the country.<a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/26/AR2011022601854.html" rel="nofollow">(Washington Post)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korean</a> man dies after explosives he bought to tie to his body detonated. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/Asia/Story/STIStory_639158.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> judge blocks construction of the <a href="/wiki/Belo_Monte_Dam" title="Belo Monte Dam">Belo Monte Dam</a> on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Amazon_Basin" title="Amazon Basin">Amazon Basin</a> after it fails to meet environmental requirements. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/26/brazil-belo-monte-dam-ruling" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexican</a> judge authorises 40 days of detention for an alleged member of the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Zetas_drug_cartel&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Zetas drug cartel (page does not exist)">Zetas drug cartel</a> suspected in the killing of a <a href="/wiki/U.S._Immigration_and_Customs_Enforcement" title="U.S. Immigration and Customs Enforcement">U.S. Immigration and Customs Enforcement</a> agent. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/26/AR2011022603601.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Irish_general_election,_2011" title="Irish general election, 2011">Irish general election, 2011</a>:
<ul>
<li>The votes are counted, with exit polls predicting <a href="/wiki/Fine_Gael" title="Fine Gael">Fine Gael</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(Ireland)" title="Labour Party (Ireland)">Labour Party</a> to do well while the ruling <a href="/wiki/Fianna_F%C3%A1il" title="Fianna Fáil">Fianna Fáil</a> is expected to do poorly. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/s/afp/20110226/ts_afp/irelandvote" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0226/politics.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2011/0226/breaking2.html?via=rel" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Paul_Gogarty" title="Paul Gogarty">Paul Gogarty</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Green_Party_(Ireland)" title="Green Party (Ireland)">Green Party</a> is the first to concede defeat via <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessandleadership.com/leadership/item/28632-green-party-td-paul-gogarty" rel="nofollow">(Business &amp; Leadership)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2011/0226/breaking6.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The first seat of the general election goes to <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(Ireland)" title="Labour Party (Ireland)">Labour Party</a> finance spokeswoman <a href="/wiki/Joan_Burton" title="Joan Burton">Joan Burton</a>, who tops the poll in the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_West_(D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann_constituency)" title="Dublin West (Dáil Éireann constituency)">Dublin West</a> constituency. <a href="/wiki/Leo_Varadkar" title="Leo Varadkar">Leo Varadkar</a> of <a href="/wiki/Fine_Gael" title="Fine Gael">Fine Gael</a> and <a href="/wiki/Joe_Higgins" title="Joe Higgins">Joe Higgins</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Socialist_Party_(Ireland)" title="Socialist Party (Ireland)">Socialist Party</a> take the second and third seats respectively in this four-seat constituency. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ukpress/article/ALeqM5gNtoL9tI2sx7dhdM4i3PqvKSUGwg?docId=N0177511298733454211A" rel="nofollow">(Press Association via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2011/0226/breaking12.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.breakingnews.ie/election/news/burton-rabbitte-and-varadkar-first-to-be-re-elected-495013.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Examiner</i>)</a></li>
<li>As the ruling <a href="/wiki/Fianna_F%C3%A1il" title="Fianna Fáil">Fianna Fáil</a> party faces national wipeout, outgoing <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Finance_(Ireland)" title="Minister for Finance (Ireland)">Minister for Finance</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brian_Lenihan,_Jnr" title="Brian Lenihan, Jnr">Brian Lenihan, Jnr</a> is saved by his own personality. He takes the final seat in the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_West_(D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann_constituency)" title="Dublin West (Dáil Éireann constituency)">Dublin West</a> constituency, the only Fianna Fáil candidate elected from 47 seats across the capital, with his brother <a href="/wiki/Conor_Lenihan" title="Conor Lenihan">Conor Lenihan</a> and aunt <a href="/wiki/Mary_O%27Rourke" title="Mary O'Rourke">Mary O'Rourke</a> losing out in their bids for re-election elsewhere. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/26/us-ireland-vote-lenihan-idUSTRE71P2P520110226" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2011/0226/breaking29.html?via=rel" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Outgoing <a href="/wiki/T%C3%A1naiste" title="Tánaiste">Tánaiste</a> <a href="/wiki/Mary_Coughlan_(politician)" title="Mary Coughlan (politician)">Mary Coughlan</a> becomes the biggest loser of the <a href="/wiki/Fianna_F%C3%A1il" title="Fianna Fáil">Fianna Fáil</a> meltdown, as her seat in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Donegal_South%E2%80%93West_(D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann_constituency)" title="Donegal South–West (Dáil Éireann constituency)">Donegal South–West</a> constituency goes to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Independent_(politics)" title="Independent (politics)">Independent</a> <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Pringle_(politician)" title="Thomas Pringle (politician)">Thomas Pringle</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.breakingnews.ie/election/news/coughlan-loses-seat-as-fine-gael-move-closer-to-government-495175.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Examiner</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_Gormley" title="John Gormley">John Gormley</a>, leader of the ruling coalition's <a href="/wiki/Green_Party_(Ireland)" title="Green Party (Ireland)">Green Party</a> and former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Minister_for_the_Environment,_Community_and_Local_Government" title="Minister for the Environment, Community and Local Government">Minister for the Environment, Heritage and Local Government</a>, is eliminated in the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_South%E2%80%93East_(D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann_constituency)" title="Dublin South–East (Dáil Éireann constituency)">Dublin South–East</a> constituency. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2011/0226/breaking66.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Independent_(politics)" title="Independent (politics)">Independent</a> long-serving outgoing <a href="/wiki/Seanad_%C3%89ireann" title="Seanad Éireann">Senator</a> <a href="/wiki/Shane_Ross" title="Shane Ross">Shane Ross</a> tops the poll in the <a href="/wiki/Dublin_South_(D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann_constituency)" title="Dublin South (Dáil Éireann constituency)">Dublin South</a> constituency. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2011/0226/breaking20.html?via=rel" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fine_Gael" title="Fine Gael">Fine Gael</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Enda_Kenny" title="Enda Kenny">Enda Kenny</a> tops the poll in the <a href="/wiki/Mayo_(D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann_constituency)" title="Mayo (Dáil Éireann constituency)">Mayo</a> constituency and claims that the results are a "massive endorsement" of his party. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0226/politics.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-northern-ireland-12585048" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/King_of_Bahrain" title="King of Bahrain">King of Bahrain</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hamad_ibn_Isa_Al_Khalifa" title="Hamad ibn Isa Al Khalifa">Hamad ibn Isa Al Khalifa</a> reshuffles his Cabinet in response the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">2011 Bahraini protests</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/meast/02/26/bahrain.protests/index.html?eref=edition&amp;utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Nearly 70,000 people <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Wisconsin_budget_protests" title="2011 Wisconsin budget protests">attend a rally</a> in the U.S. city of <a href="/wiki/Madison,_Wisconsin" title="Madison, Wisconsin">Madison, Wisconsin</a> over plans by the <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Wisconsin" title="Governor of Wisconsin">Governor of Wisconsin</a> <a href="/wiki/Scott_Walker_(politician)" title="Scott Walker (politician)">Scott Walker</a> to remove <a href="/wiki/Collective_bargaining" title="Collective bargaining">collective bargaining</a> rights from most state employees. <a class="external text" href="http://host.madison.com/wsj/news/local/govt-and-politics/article_19c56fb6-41d7-11e0-820b-001cc4c03286.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wisconsin State Journal</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Christy_Clark" title="Christy Clark">Christy Clark</a> becomes the second woman to be <a href="/wiki/Premier_of_British_Columbia" title="Premier of British Columbia">Premier of British Columbia</a> after winning a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_British_Columbia" title="Liberal Party of British Columbia">Liberal Party of British Columbia</a> ballot. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theglobeandmail.com/news/national/british-columbia/bc-politics/christy-clark-to-become-bcs-new-premier/article1922427/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Globe and Mail</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> takes two opposition leaders <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mir_Hossein_Moussavi" title="Mir Hossein Moussavi">Mir Hossein Moussavi</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mehdi_Karrubi" title="Mehdi Karrubi">Mehdi Karrubi</a> and their wives into protection supposedly for their own protection. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/meast/02/26/iran.opposition/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
