<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Six people are killed in a failed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_coup" title="Military coup">coup</a> attempt on the presidential palace in the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71Q06K20110227" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>State television is taken off air in the city of <a href="/wiki/Abidjan" title="Abidjan">Abidjan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast" title="Ivory Coast">Ivory Coast</a>, during clashes between forces loyal to incumbent President <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Gbagbo" title="Laurent Gbagbo">Laurent Gbagbo</a> and rival groups. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71Q01D20110227" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5jAOZ1COy0NUZgWNZgWFMI768L9tw?docId=6083866" rel="nofollow">(CP)</a></li>
<li>At least 115 people are killed in a government offensive against <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">Al-Qaeda</a> linked militants in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/World/Story/STIStory_639529.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Birmingham-Shuttlesworth_International_Airport" title="Birmingham-Shuttlesworth International Airport">Birmingham-Shuttlesworth International Airport</a> in the US city of <a href="/wiki/Birmingham,_Alabama" title="Birmingham, Alabama">Birmingham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alabama" title="Alabama">Alabama</a> is evacuated following the discovery of a suspicious package. <a class="external text" href="http://www.myfoxal.com/Global/story.asp?S=14151628" rel="nofollow">(Fox News Alabama)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Academy Awards
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/83rd_Academy_Awards" title="83rd Academy Awards">83rd Academy Awards</a> are held to honor the best <a href="/wiki/2010_in_film" title="2010 in film">films in 2010</a> at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kodak_Theater" title="Kodak Theater">Kodak Theater</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hollywood" title="Hollywood">Hollywood</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://oscar.go.com/" rel="nofollow">(Academy Awards)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/entertainment/2011/02/27/oscar-academy-awards-red-carpet/?utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+foxnews%2Fentertainment+%28Internal+-+Entertainment+-+Mixed%29&amp;utm_content=Google+International" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
<li><i>The King's Speech</i> wins the <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Picture" title="Academy Award for Best Picture">Academy Award for Best Picture</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/awards/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Colin_Firth" title="Colin Firth">Colin Firth</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actor" title="Academy Award for Best Actor">Academy Award for Best Actor</a> for his role in <i>The King's Speech</i>. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/awards/2011/02/oscars-wins-lead-actor.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Natalie_Portman" title="Natalie Portman">Natalie Portman</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress" title="Academy Award for Best Actress">Academy Award for Best Actress</a> for her role in <i><a href="/wiki/Black_Swan_(film)" title="Black Swan (film)">Black Swan</a></i>. <a class="external text" href="http://latimesblogs.latimes.com/awards/2011/02/oscars-wins-lead-actress.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tom_Hooper_(director)" title="Tom Hooper (director)">Tom Hooper</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Director" title="Academy Award for Best Director">Academy Award for Best Director</a> for <i><a href="/wiki/The_King%27s_Speech" title="The King's Speech">The King's Speech</a></i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.indyposted.com/153632/and-the-oscar-goes-to-complete-list-of-2011-oscar-winners/#" rel="nofollow">(Indy Posted)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Christian_Bale" title="Christian Bale">Christian Bale</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Supporting_Actor" title="Academy Award for Best Supporting Actor">Academy Award for Best Supporting Actor</a> for his role in <i>The Fighter</i>. <a class="external text" href="http://abclocal.go.com/wpvi/story?section=news/entertainment&amp;id=7984298&amp;rss=rss-wpvi-article-7984298" rel="nofollow">(ABC News America)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Melissa_Leo" title="Melissa Leo">Melissa Leo</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Supporting_Actress" title="Academy Award for Best Supporting Actress">Academy Award for Best Supporting Actress</a> for her role in <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Fighter_(2010_film)" title="The Fighter (2010 film)">The Fighter</a></i>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/s/ap/us_oscars;_ylt=Av8LBhrmwqslZ5yapdhN4Kqs0NUE;_ylu=X3oDMTM5ZHVkbjZsBGFzc2V0A2FwLzIwMTEwMjI4L3VzX29zY2FycwRjY29kZQNtb3N0cG9wdWxhcgRjcG9zAzEEcG9zAzIEcHQDaG9tZV9jb2tlBHNlYwN5bl90b3Bfc3RvcnkEc2xrA2xlb3Rha2Vzc3VwcA--" rel="nofollow">(AP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Egypt" title="Government of Egypt">Government of Egypt</a> announces that the <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Exchange" title="Egyptian Exchange">Egyptian stock market</a> will reopen on Tuesday. <a class="external text" href="http://dealbook.nytimes.com/2011/02/27/egyptian-stock-market-set-to-reopen-tuesday/" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A landslide hits <a href="/wiki/La_Paz" title="La Paz">La Paz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a>, after rains killed 44 people. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/WORLD/americas/02/28/bolivia.landslide/?hpt=T2" rel="nofollow">(CNN International)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://mwcnews.net/news/americas/8998-bolivian-aid-for-landslide-homeless.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Media with Conscience</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ncnnews.org/nphweb/html/ncn/article.jsp?sid=10000010&amp;id=10010044" rel="nofollow">(<i>Nazarene Communications Network</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> warns it will take military action against <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> if it continues to distribute information regarding the unrest in the Middle East to its citizens. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/27/AR2011022700351.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/northkorea/2011/02/27/55/0401000000AEN20110227003500315F.HTML" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-27/north-korea-warns-of-military-response-against-south-over-leaflet-drops.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Secretary-General_of_the_United_Nations" title="Secretary-General of the United Nations">Secretary-General of the United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/Ban_Ki-moon" title="Ban Ki-moon">Ban Ki-moon</a> claims that <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a> has broken an international arms embargo on the <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast" title="Ivory Coast">Ivory Coast</a> by delivering three <a href="/wiki/Attack_helicopter" title="Attack helicopter">attack helicopters</a> to military forces supporting the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_the_Ivory_Coast" title="President of the Ivory Coast">President of the Ivory Coast</a> <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Gbagbo" title="Laurent Gbagbo">Laurent Gbagbo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5jAOZ1COy0NUZgWNZgWFMI768L9tw?docId=6083866" rel="nofollow">(Canadian Press via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a></dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">Bahrain</a>: Thousands of anti-government protesters demonstrate in the capital <a href="/wiki/Manama" title="Manama">Manama</a>, as 18 opposition MPs submit their resignations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iwY3NTSpmBl3VTOlFY08tsPi82Rw?docId=CNG.9ffa0c7df5ec323223afd5b1c6a29c99.db1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lebanon#2011_government_collapse" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>: Hundreds of protesters demonstrate in the capital <a href="/wiki/Beirut" title="Beirut">Beirut</a> against the country's sectarian political system. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/27/us-lebanon-protest-idUSTRE71Q1B620110227" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" title="2011 Libyan civil war">Libya</a>:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> adopts <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_1970" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 1970">Resolution 1970</a>, imposing sanctions on <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a>'s regime. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/video/2011/02/27/VI2011022700657.html?hpid=topnews" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Anti-government forces seize the town of <a href="/wiki/Zawiya,_Libya" title="Zawiya, Libya">Zawiya</a>, 30 miles west of the capital <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12591025" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/world/story/2011/02/27/libya.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Omani_protests" title="2011 Omani protests">Oman</a>: Police clash with anti-government protesters in <a href="/wiki/Sohar" title="Sohar">Sohar</a>, leaving two people dead. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011227112850852905.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-12590588" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Sudanese_protests" title="2011 Sudanese protests">Sudan</a>: Riot police break up a demonstration against election fraud in the capital <a href="/wiki/Khartoum" title="Khartoum">Khartoum</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/27/us-sudan-protest-idUSTRE71Q1SU20110227" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tunisian_Revolution" title="Tunisian Revolution">Tunisia</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Beji_Caid_el_Sebsi" title="Beji Caid el Sebsi">Beji Caid el Sebsi</a> is announced as the new Prime Minister. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/27/tunisian-prime-minister-ghannouchi-resigns?utm_source=twitterfeed&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisian</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Tunisia" title="Prime Minister of Tunisia">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Ghannouchi" title="Mohamed Ghannouchi">Mohamed Ghannouchi</a> announces his resignation in a speech on state TV. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12591445" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Clashes take place at a demonstration calling for the resignation of former members of <a href="/wiki/Zine_El_Abidine_Ben_Ali" title="Zine El Abidine Ben Ali">Zine El Abidine Ben Ali</a>'s regime in the interim government. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5iUyF0OYJPntwAMRcXBsLkD1j-kjQ?docId=CNG.6d1f4ccfc419a26d8e1da17eabc8d972.5e1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">Yemen</a>: President <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a> says that protests against his rule are an attempt to split the nation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alarabiya.net/articles/2011/02/27/139430.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/afp/article/ALeqM5inL78d7pU3CXk6UQ7q7Na7l5Hiug?docId=CNG.1de1d43eba079baba9d7893981d8c7a1.321" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Irish_general_election,_2011" title="Irish general election, 2011">Irish general election, 2011</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/People_Before_Profit_Alliance" title="People Before Profit Alliance">PBPA</a> candidate <a href="/wiki/Richard_Boyd_Barrett" title="Richard Boyd Barrett">Richard Boyd Barrett</a> of the <a href="/wiki/United_Left_Alliance" title="United Left Alliance">United Left Alliance</a>, and son of actress <a href="/wiki/Sin%C3%A9ad_Cusack" title="Sinéad Cusack">Sinéad Cusack</a>, defeats former minister and deputy <a href="/wiki/Fianna_F%C3%A1il" title="Fianna Fáil">Fianna Fáil</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Mary_Hanafin" title="Mary Hanafin">Mary Hanafin</a> in the <a href="/wiki/D%C3%BAn_Laoghaire_(D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann_constituency)" title="Dún Laoghaire (Dáil Éireann constituency)">Dún Laoghaire</a> constituency. This leaves Fianna Fáil with one representative in the capital city (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brian_Lenihan,_Jnr" title="Brian Lenihan, Jnr">Brian Lenihan, Jnr</a>) and no Fianna Fáil women at all in the <a href="/wiki/31st_D%C3%A1il" title="31st Dáil">31st Dáil</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/newspaper/breaking/2011/0227/breaking16.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Irish Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.eveningecho.ie/news/ireland/hanafin-loses-out-to-boyd-barrett-in-dun-laoghaire-495322.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Evening Echo</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fine_Gael" title="Fine Gael">Fine Gael</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Enda_Kenny" title="Enda Kenny">Enda Kenny</a> receives international congratulations from <a href="/wiki/Angela_Merkel" title="Angela Merkel">Angela Merkel</a>, <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Manuel_Barroso" title="José Manuel Barroso">José Manuel Barroso</a>, with Cameron inviting him to <a href="/wiki/10_Downing_Street" title="10 Downing Street">10 Downing Street</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2011/0228/election.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Large numbers of police and security forces are deployed in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> cities after calls for protests inspired by <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">events in North Africa and the Middle East</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ft.com/cms/s/0/e7a66d8a-422d-11e0-8b34-00144feabdc0.html?ftcamp=rss" rel="nofollow">(<i>Financial Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.sify.com/news/security-stepped-up-to-check-strolling-protests-in-china-news-international-lc1sadjcfdc.html" rel="nofollow">(Sify India)</a></li>
<li>For a second day, <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatian</a> war veterans gather in the thousands to protest, this time in <a href="/wiki/Split,_Croatia" title="Split, Croatia">Split</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.index.hr/vijesti/clanak/prosvjednik-na-splitskoj-rivi-kolabrirao-i-preminuo/539897.aspx" rel="nofollow">(Index)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin" title="Wisconsin">Wisconsin</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AFL-CIO" title="AFL-CIO">AFL-CIO</a> warns that hundreds of unionists will risk arrest in trying to prevent police clearing the <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin_State_Capitol" title="Wisconsin State Capitol">Wisconsin State Capitol</a> in the US city of <a href="/wiki/Madison,_Wisconsin" title="Madison, Wisconsin">Madison</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jsonline.com/news/statepolitics/117011928.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Milwaukee Journal-Sentinel</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2011/POLITICS/02/27/wisconsin.budget/index.html#" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Anonymous_(group)" title="Anonymous (group)">Anonymous</a> targets <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Political_activities_of_the_Koch_family" title="Political activities of the Koch family">Koch Brothers</a>-backed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Americans_For_Prosperity" title="Americans For Prosperity">Americans For Prosperity</a> to demonstrate against its support of anti-union legislation in Wisconsin and the influence of money in US politics. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/technologylive/post/2011/03/anonymous-actively-probing-koch-brothers-corporate-networks-/1" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://firstread.msnbc.msn.com/_news/2011/02/28/6154621-anonymous-attack" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>The head of the <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a> <a href="/wiki/Amr_Moussa" title="Amr Moussa">Amr Moussa</a> announces that he will run as a candidate in the Egyptian <a href="/wiki/President_of_Egypt" title="President of Egypt">presidential</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_presidential_election,_2011" title="Egyptian presidential election, 2011">election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/disp/story.mpl/ap/top/all/7448341.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and incidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Arab Spring</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_Civil_War" title="2011 Libyan Civil War">Libya</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al_Jazeera" title="Al Jazeera">Al Jazeera</a> reports that many <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">African</a> <a href="/wiki/Migrant_worker" title="Migrant worker">migrant workers</a> in <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> have been victims of violence due to suspicions that they are <a href="/wiki/Mercenary" title="Mercenary">mercenaries</a> for <a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a>'s regime. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/africa/2011/02/201122865814378541.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> sends two planeloads of aid to opponents of the <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> regime in <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/libyaNews/idAFLDE71R0FN20110228" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Forces loyal to Colonel Gaddafi surround the town of <a href="/wiki/Zawiya,_Libya" title="Zawiya, Libya">Zawiya</a> as part of a general counterattack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/28/us-libya-protests-idUSTRE71G0A620110228?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed:+reuters/topNews+(News+/+US+/+Top+News)" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/03/01/world/africa/01unrest.html?hp" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a> announces that he is working on a <a href="/wiki/No-fly_zone" title="No-fly zone">no-fly zone</a> over Libya. <a class="external text" href="http://content.usatoday.com/communities/ondeadline/post/2011/02/britain-working-on-plans-for-a-no-fly-zone-over-libya/1" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State" title="United States Secretary of State">United States Secretary of State</a> <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> announces that the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> will be sending assistance teams to Libya's borders with <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Muammar_Gaddafi" title="Muammar Gaddafi">Muammar Gaddafi</a> tells the <a href="/wiki/BBC_News" title="BBC News">BBC</a> that all of his people love him and refuses to acknowledge that there are protests in <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12603259" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> freezes $30 billion in Libyan assets. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2011/02/28/AR2011022802797.html?hpid=topnews" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Justice_and_Equality_Movement" title="Justice and Equality Movement">Justice and Equality Movement</a> in <a href="/wiki/Darfur" title="Darfur">Darfur</a>, western <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>, asks the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> to rescue its leader in Libya, after accusations he was supporting mercenary activities in the country. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71R0K020110228?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Opposition forces rescue seven rebels 'buried alive' under concrete in a government compound in <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a>, while close to 100,000 <a href="/wiki/Migrant_worker" title="Migrant worker">migrant workers</a> flee Libya. <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/world/colonel-muammar-gaddafis-prisoners-buried-alive-in-benghazi/story-e6frf7lf-1226013599522" rel="nofollow">(Herald Sun)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-1361555/Libya-protests-Rescuers-7-buried-alive-Gaddafis-compound-Benghazi.html?ito=feeds-newsxml" rel="nofollow">(Daily Mail)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2011_Omani_protests" title="2011 Omani protests">2011 Omani protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>Demonstrations calling for economic and political change continue for a third day, amid reports of looting. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/201122814254293647.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Bahraini_protests" title="2011 Bahraini protests">2011 Bahraini protests</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahraini</a> protesters block access to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Bahrain" title="Parliament of Bahrain">Parliament of Bahrain</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/middle-east/Bahrain-protesters-block-Parliament/articleshow/7593904.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a> may attack the <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">al-Shabaab</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamist" title="Islamist">Islamist</a> militant group in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>, following its threat to target Kenya. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71R0GV20110228?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A bomb explodes in <a href="/wiki/Yangon" title="Yangon">Yangon</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a>, injuring eight people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/SEAsia/Story/STIStory_639672.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Frank_Buckles" title="Frank Buckles">Frank Buckles</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_last_surviving_World_War_I_veterans_by_country" title="List of last surviving World War I veterans by country">last surviving veteran</a> of <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, passes away in <a href="/wiki/Charles_Town,_West_Virginia" title="Charles Town, West Virginia">Charles Town, West Virginia</a>, aged 110. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/us/2011/02/28/veteran-wwi-dies-w-va-age-110/?test=faces" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Television_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Television in the United Kingdom">Television</a> <a href="/wiki/Television_advertisement" title="Television advertisement">advertising</a> in the United Kingdom
<ul>
<li>The ban on <a href="/wiki/Product_placement" title="Product placement">product placement</a> in television programmes is lifted, allowing advertisers to pay for their goods to be seen on British TV. The first product to be displayed in this regard is a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nescafe" title="Nescafe">Nescafe</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coffee_machine" title="Coffee machine">coffee machine</a>, which appeared on <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/This_Morning_(TV_series)" title="This Morning (TV series)">This Morning</a></i>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-12593061" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/finance/newsbysector/mediatechnologyandtelecoms/media/8352449/TV-product-placement-makes-a-typically-English-debut.html#" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li>A year-long trial also begins allowing commercial television channels to show up to 12 minutes of adverts per hour during films and dramas, bringing them into line with soap operas where this is already permitted. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/culture/tvandradio/8341764/TV-films-to-be-interrupted-by-12-minutes-of-adverts.html#" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hollywood" title="Hollywood">Hollywood</a> actress and former <a href="/wiki/Sex_symbol" title="Sex symbol">sex symbol</a> <a href="/wiki/Jane_Russell" title="Jane Russell">Jane Russell</a> dies at age 89 of respiratory failure in <a href="/wiki/Santa_Maria,_California" title="Santa Maria, California">Santa Maria, California</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.kcoy.com/global/story.asp?s=14158234" rel="nofollow">(Fox Central Florida)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/03/01/us-janerussell-idUSTRE72001620110301?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews&amp;utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+reuters%2FtopNews+%28News+%2F+US+%2F+Top+News%29" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.hollywoodreporter.com/news/gentlemen-prefer-blondes-star-jane-russell-dies-162533" rel="nofollow">(<i>Hollywood Reporter</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Crude_oil" title="Crude oil">Crude oil</a> prices rise to their highest levels in two years as <a href="/wiki/Stock_market" title="Stock market">stock market</a> indexes fall in <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> due to continued uncertainty in the <a href="/wiki/Arab_Spring" title="Arab Spring">Middle East</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2011-02-28/asia-stocks-fall-as-oil-gains-china-cuts-outlook-euro-drops-on-ireland.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>'s largest bank <a href="/wiki/HSBC" title="HSBC">HSBC</a> doubles its profits to $19bn (£11.8bn) in 2010. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/business/2011/feb/28/hsbc-profits-double-almost-twelve-billion-pounds" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Government" title="United States Government">United States Government</a> grants its first <a href="/wiki/Deepwater_drilling" title="Deepwater drilling">deepwater drilling</a> license since the <a href="/wiki/Deepwater_Horizon_oil_spill" title="Deepwater Horizon oil spill">Deepwater Horizon oil spill</a> to <a href="/wiki/Noble_Energy" title="Noble Energy">Noble Energy</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-12604560" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least 16 people in <a href="/wiki/Bandeira_do_Sul" title="Bandeira do Sul">Bandeira do Sul</a> are killed after a high-voltage electric powerline crashed onto a float participating in a parade ahead of <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Carnival" title="Brazilian Carnival">carnival</a> celebrations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/BreakingNews/World/Story/STIStory_639808.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>New Zealand earthquakes:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a> police evacuate 60 properties in <a href="/wiki/Christchurch" title="Christchurch">Christchurch</a> suburbs after cracks from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Canterbury_earthquake" title="2011 Canterbury earthquake">2011 Canterbury earthquake</a> appear in cliffs. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/1491757/Residents-evacuated-from-NZ-suburbs" rel="nofollow">(SBS)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_New_Zealand" title="Prime Minister of New Zealand">Prime Minister of New Zealand</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Key" title="John Key">John Key</a> estimates that the total cost of the 2011 and <a href="/wiki/2010_Canterbury_earthquake" title="2010 Canterbury earthquake">2010 earthquakes</a> is up to <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_dollar" title="New Zealand dollar">NZ$</a>20 billion. <a class="external text" href="http://www.newstalkzb.co.nz/newsdetail1.asp?storyID=191514" rel="nofollow">(News Talk ZB)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Eleven <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chinese_people" title="Chinese people">Chinese</a> fishermen are missing after their <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fishing_boat" title="Fishing boat">fishing boat</a> sinks in the <a href="/wiki/East_China_Sea" title="East China Sea">East China Sea</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://wrbsyndicate.com/News/Eleven-Chinese-missing-after-fishing-boat-sinks-in-East-China-Sea" rel="nofollow">(BNO via WR Berkley)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/Secretary-General_of_the_United_Nations" title="Secretary-General of the United Nations">Secretary-General</a> <a href="/wiki/Ban_Ki-moon" title="Ban Ki-moon">Ban Ki-moon</a> says <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a> has "seriously violated" the <a href="/wiki/Arms_embargo" title="Arms embargo">arms embargo</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast" title="Ivory Coast">Ivory Coast</a>, after a delivery of attack helicopters and material to the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-africa-12595145" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timeslive.co.za/africa/article941084.ece/Arms-for-Gbagbo" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times Live South Africa</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rosatom" title="Rosatom">Rosatom</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> state nuclear energy corporation, explains that the <a href="/wiki/Bushehr_Nuclear_Power_Plant" title="Bushehr Nuclear Power Plant">Bushehr Nuclear Power Plant</a> has been delayed in opening due to damage to the <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_reactor" title="Nuclear reactor">nuclear reactor</a>'s cooling pumps. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2011/03/01/world/middleeast/01nuke.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Former military leaders in <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> go on trial on charges that they masterminded a plan to steal the children of <a href="/wiki/Dissident" title="Dissident">dissidents</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/americas/2011/02/2011228201231379527.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wing_Chau" title="Wing Chau">Wing Chau</a>, a money manager, files a lawsuit against <a href="/wiki/Michael_Lewis" title="Michael Lewis">Michael Lewis</a>, the author of <a href="/wiki/The_Big_Short" title="The Big Short">The Big Short</a>, a popular book about the financial crisis of 2007-08. Chau alleges the book makes "false and defamtory statements" in order to use Chau as a foil for his protagonist, <a href="/wiki/Steve_Eisman" title="Steve Eisman">Steve Eisman</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/28/us-books-defamation-lewis-idUSTRE71R4XX20110228" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A court in the <a href="/wiki/Seychelles" title="Seychelles">Seychelles</a> sentences ten <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Somali_pirates" title="Somali pirates">Somali pirates</a> to 20 years in prison. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71R0DM20110228" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>In the United Kingdom, three senior fire officers from the <a href="/wiki/Warwickshire_Fire_and_Rescue_Service" title="Warwickshire Fire and Rescue Service">Warwickshire Fire Service</a> are to face <a href="/wiki/Manslaughter_in_English_law#Manslaughter_by_gross_negligence" title="Manslaughter in English law">manslaughter by gross negligence</a> charges over the deaths of four firefighters in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2007_Atherstone_fire" title="2007 Atherstone fire">warehouse blaze in 2007</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-12598130" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/British_Airways" title="British Airways">British Airways</a> IT expert <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Rajib_Karim&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Rajib Karim (page does not exist)">Rajib Karim</a> is convicted on charges related to plotting to blow up a plane. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-tyne-12561994" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>British security guard <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Danny_Fitzsimons&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Danny Fitzsimons (page does not exist)">Danny Fitzsimons</a> is jailed for 20 years by an Iraqi court after being convicted of murdering two colleagues. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-manchester-12594245" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> union leader <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ruben_Gonzalez_(unionist)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ruben Gonzalez (unionist) (page does not exist)">Ruben Gonzalez</a> is sentenced to seven years in jail in connection with a strike at the state <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iron_mining" title="Iron mining">iron mining</a> company. <a class="external text" href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/canadianpress/article/ALeqM5gj1x4tijgLkrFOnqt69AXyxNQMNg?docId=6100659" rel="nofollow">(Canadian Press via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The President of <a href="/wiki/Tanzania" title="Tanzania">Tanzania</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jakaya_Kikwete" title="Jakaya Kikwete">Jakaya Kikwete</a>, accuses the opposition of provoking violence in the country in an attempt to remove the government. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFJOE71R0IN20110228?sp=true" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>'s general prosecutor imposes a travel ban on former President <a href="/wiki/Hosni_Mubarak" title="Hosni Mubarak">Hosni Mubarak</a> and his family. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/middleeast/2011/02/2011228111333371538.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> confirms that it is holding two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iranian_reform_movement" title="Iranian reform movement">Opposition</a> leaders <a href="/wiki/Mir-Hossein_Mousavi" title="Mir-Hossein Mousavi">MirHosein Mousavi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mehdi_Karroubi" title="Mehdi Karroubi">Mehdi Karroubi</a> under <a href="/wiki/House_arrest" title="House arrest">house arrest</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.radiozamaneh.com/english/content/iran-confirms-steps-against-opposition-leaders" rel="nofollow">(Radio Zamaneh)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_Yemeni_protests" title="2011 Yemeni protests">2011 Yemeni protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>President <a href="/wiki/Ali_Abdullah_Saleh" title="Ali Abdullah Saleh">Ali Abdullah Saleh</a> offers to form a unity government with the opposition. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2011/02/28/yemen-government-idUSLDE71R1BG20110228" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> threatens to boycott the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Summer Olympics</a> ostensibly because its <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics#Logo" title="2012 Summer Olympics">logo</a> spells <a href="/wiki/Zion" title="Zion">Zion</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/world/2011/feb/28/iran-london-olympics-logo-zion" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>US <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a> champion <a href="/wiki/Serena_Williams" title="Serena Williams">Serena Williams</a> is hospitalised in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Pulmonary_embolism" title="Pulmonary embolism">pulmonary embolism</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.people.com/people/article/0,,20470190,00.html" rel="nofollow">(People)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
